Baame wane ane mende manditamo dokome, baanya endakali dupanya koo dupa kunao nepakamaitala pyoo nyetana, baanya kenge doko Jisasa lape” lea.
Dopa pitana lao wamba Kamongome propeta mende-kisa pii leamo dake angi jia: “Enda mapukae, akali tole napingi mendeme wane ane mende manditamo, dokonya kenge doko Emanyuele latami.” (Emanyuele dokonya tenge doko, “Gote naima-pipa tole katenge.”)
<range>
Josepe paliu sakatatala, Kamongonya enjele dokome lamaiyamoli pyoo, baame enda doko baanya etanenge joo lanyia.
Lanyiamoaka doko, baame enda dokopa, yonge tole napiambinopaka, wane ane doko mandea. Wane doko mandipiamopa, Josepeme kenge doko Jisasa lea.
Erote baa kiŋi kateamopa, Mariame Jisasa yuu andake Judia, taono Beteleme dokonya mandea. Mandipiamopa, niki pyakaengesa tange, buinya tenge masingi akali mendapuame Jerusalema ipupala,
endakali kateamino dupa lamaiyoo, “Naimame Judamanya kiŋi katapengena latae, wane ŋaŋa dokonya bui doko niki pyakaengesa-kaita, katamo kandatala, baa mambo pyala epelyamanona, anja mandipae silyape?” leami.
Dopa lapae sepala, Kiŋi Erote baa mona kenda kaeya. Dokopa Jerusalema tange endakali longome sepala, mona kenda kaeyamiaka.
Eroteme pitisa mupapi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, dupa pitaka epena lao nyoo elyambu pia. Elyambu petala dokaita tipa pyoo, “Kraisa doko yuu andukunya mandipengepe?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, dokaitame pii yanu pyao, “Goteme propeta mende-kisa lamaiyamo doko, dapa lao pepa pyapae silyamo: 'Nyakama Beteleme tange dupa, nyakamanya yuu taono doko taono waka Judia silyamo, dupanya pundi-pundi naseta. Nyakamanya mandipaenya mandipae, dupanya isingi akali mende pyakalyetamo dokome, nambanya Israele tange endakali dupa setao katakatana' lao pepa pyapae silyamo. Dopa lapae silyamo dokonya, Kraisa doko yuu andake Judia dokonya taono yakane Beteleme mandipengena” leami.
<range>
Dopa lateaminopa, Eroteme akali niki pyakaengesa tange dupa elyakalao epena latala, bui doko gii andukupa katapyape lao tipa pia.
Dopa petala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakama Beteleme pupala, wane doko kutakondape pyoo kutalapape. Kutao kandatala dokopa, nambame apata mambo pyala patoana, langya ipupape” lea.
Dopa lateamopa, kiŋi dokonya pii dupa sepala, nyakama peami. Peaminopa, wamba niki pyakaengesa-kaita bui kateamo kandeamino, dokoaka wambao pao wane mandipae siamo dokonya katea.
Dopa piamopa, nyakamame bui doko kandatala, mona etete auu kaeyami.
Mona auu kaeyao andaka kolandatala, Mariame wane doko kopetae peteamo kandeami. Kandatala dupame luma lakapala, wane doko mambo piami. Mambo pyapala, nyakamanya mandi dupa tangupala, golopi, kena tunduma pingi pautapi, wele epe tunduma pipae mendapu maiyami.
Kuka Goteme akali dokaita Erote kalyamosa-kaita, pilyala naena lao kombea pimaiya. Dopa piamosa, dokaita kaitini waka mendenya-kaita, nyakamanya yuusa pilyiami.
Akali dokaita pateaminopa, kuka Kamongonya enjele mendeme, kombeame Josepe lamaiyoo, “Eroteme wane doko kutao pyao kumasalanya pilyamona, emba sakatatala, wane dokopa endangipa lanyoo, paka Isipi puu. Pupala katatenopa, nambame emba pilya lato gii dokopa pilyetena, emba dokonya mee katapena” lea.
Dopa lamaitiamopa, kuka dokopaka Josepe sakatatala, wane dokopa endangipa lanyoo, Isipi paanya pea.
Pupala Josepe Isipiaka katao, Erote kumiamo gii dokonya tuu lea. Dopa piamo dokome, wamba Kamongome propeta mende-kisa, “Nambanya ikiningi doko Isipi yuu doko yakinatala, nambame epena latona,” leamo doko angi jia.
Niki pyakaengesa tange masingi akali dupame Erote baa minakasetala, pupimi-lumu lao sepala, baa etete imbumi kumia. Imbu kaeyapala baame wamba akali dupa, bui doko gii andukupa kateape lao tipa piamo, doko masia. Masetala Betelemepi, yuu dosa makisa singipi, dupanya pupala, wane ane ee kana laponya anatena patae, dupa pitaka baanya yanda singi dupame, pyao kumasala pena lea.
Dopa piamo dokome, “Taono Rama dokonya, Resolonya wanenge dupanya, wane dupa lao yamataka lao, ee leaminopa, endakali mendeme dupanya mona minao taiyu lasakamaipenge nanjiana” lao, wamba propeta Jeremaeyame leamo doko angi jia.
<range>
Erote kumateamopa, Kamongonya enjele mende Isipi pupala, kombeame Josepe
lamaiyoo, “Wane doko pyalanya piamo akali doko kumatelyamona, embame wane dokopa endangipa lanyoo, Israele pilya” lea.
Dopa lateamopa, Josepeme wane dokopa endangipa lanyoo, Israele pilyia.
Pilyiamoaka doko, Akelesa dokome baanya takange Erotenya panda nyepala, Judia yuu dokonya kiŋi joo kalyamo lapae sepala, Josepe yuu dokaita paanya paka kaeya. Dokopa Goteme kombeame, Judia yuu dokonya nakatape lao lamaiyamo dokonya, baame wane dokopa, endangipa lanyoo Galilea pea.
Pupala taono Nasarete lenge dokonya katea. Dopa piamo dokome, wamba propeta dupame, “Baa Nasarete tangena latamina” leamo pii doko angi jia.
Ee kana mendatupa pateamopa, Jone kaimbu pingi doko Judia yuu dokonya, endakali napalenge mendasa ipao katapala, pii tee pyao lamaiya.
Lamaiyoo pituu, “Gotenya isingi mate doko tengesa ipatelyamona, mona kapilyalapa” lea.
Wamba propeta Aisaiyame Jone kaimbu pingi doko kandao, “Endakali napalenge yuu mendasa akali mendeme katapala wii lao, 'Kamongonya kaitini doko depa lakamaiyepape. Kaitini koeyapae dupa tolasakamaiyepape' lao katatana” lea.
Jone baa yonge pee kamele itimi wasepaepi, matapu bulumakao yanungimi wasepaepi, dupa pyoo katea. Baa paiyombapi, ambulya kakasa lyingipi, dupa nao katea.
Dokopa Jerusalema tangepi, Judia tangepi, endaki Jodane mate dosale tangepi, longo dupa Jone kateamo dokonya peami.
Pupala dupame nyakamanya koo dupa lao panata piaminopa, baame endaki Jodane dokonya kaimbu pyakamaiya.
Dokopa Parasaipi, Sadyusiapi longo mendapu kaimbu pyekena lao epeamino kandatala, baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakama koo kanopatonya mandipae dupa! Gotenya imbu kaeyapae ipatamo doko, apimi langimusa, paka epelyamipi?
Nyakama kini mona kapilyeteamino doko, nyakamanya mana makandepi dupame panasalapape.
Abrakame nyakamanya yumbange dokonyana, nyakama yaka kalyamanona lao masala naeyalapape. Nambame nyakama langilyo: Goteme kapa pao kana silyamo datupa, Abrakamenya wane jina lapyali.
Goteme ita tenge dokonya, wua doko depa lanya setapelyamo. Ita dii epe manja naenge dupa pitaka, pokapala baame itatenya soo yangata.
“Akali maitapyao epelyamo dokonya, pupu lapae dokome namba ita minao. Nambame baanya moko pee dolapo, nyoo minakamaiyanya, namba epe daa. Nambame kaimbu pyekelyo dake, mona kapilyingi doko pyekelyona, baame Oli Spiritapa, itate kaiyepaepame nyakamanya kaimbu pyakata.
Wita angi imbupi pyasoo silyamopa, baame yapenge sapolo doko nyepala, ketae pyasingi. Dopa pingisa, poome imbu umbisa soo kambu pilyamopa, angi isa lapalapa kuiyetaenya ipao singi. Ipao silyamo dupa nyoo baanya nee setenge anda dokonya setapala, imbu dupa ita konjala naenge dokonya soo yangatana” lea.
Gii dokopa Jisasa Galilea yakinatala, endaki Jodane mate dokonya Joneme kaimbu pyekena lao pea.
Pao pyakameamopa, Joneme Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Embame nambanya kaimbu pyakapenge doko, aipuma nambame embanya kaimbu pyakatale lao epelepe?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Nalimbame pyepale lao Goteme masilyamo, dupa apata pimbana pii” lea. Dopa leanya, Joneme baanya pii doko watao minatala, kaimbu pyakamaiya.
Jisasa kaimbu nyepala, endaki ketae pyakalyiamopa, kaiti saa papa laloo petala, Gotenya Oli Spirit doko yaka maiyolee joo lanao ipao, baa-kisa petea.
Dokopa kaiti-kisa katao, pii mende lea dokome lao pituu, “Doo kalyamo doko nambanya Ikiningi, mona setenge doko. Nambame baa etete auu kaengena” lea.
Gii dokopa Sataneme Jisasa minao makande pina lao, Oli Spiritame baa laminao endakali napalenge yuu mendasa pea.
Pupala Jisasa baa yuu gii 40 kuka kotakapi, Gote loma soo, nee nanao katea. Dopa pyoo katapala, baa lopo kaeya.
Dokopa makande pingi akali dokome, baa kateasa ipupala lao pituu, “Emba kini Gote Ikiningi-tamo doko, kana silyamo datupa betesa jina laa” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “'Endakalimi betesa iki nenge dokonya-kaita, saka nakatenge. Goteme pii lelyamo dokonya-kaita, endakali saka katengena,' dopa lao pepa pyapae silyamona” lea.
Dopa lateamopa, Sataneme baa laminao taono epe Jerusalema dokonya pupala, lotuu anda andake ketae dokonya katena lea.
Dopa latala baame Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Gotenya pii dapa lao pepa pyapae silyamo: 'Goteme emba masetala, kaname embanya mokopi mende, koeyatame latala, enjele dupame emba nisoo kopyoo nyina latana' latae silyamo. Dopana, emba kini Gote Ikiningi-tamo doko, ketae dakenya katao isa mangau laa” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “'Embame embanya Kamongo Gote doko minao makande napipi' lao pepa pyapae silyamona” lea.
Sataneme Jisasa deaka laminao, yuu manda etete ketae mendenya pyakalyetala, isa yuu dakenya isingi matepi, oapi epe muni andake pupengepi, dupa baa kandena lea.
Dopa latala, baame Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Embame namba lao luma lakapala, mambo pyateno doko, silyamo dupa pitaka nambame emba ditoana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “'Embame embanya Kamongo Gote doko mambo pyao, baanya iki kalai pyakamaiyoo katape' lao pepa pyapae silyamona, Satane, emba puu” lea.
Dopa lateamopa, Sataneme Jisasa yakinatala pea. Dokopa enjele mendapu ipupala, Jisasa nisiami.
Jone kaimbu pingi doko, anjiami lapae doko sepala, Jisasa baa Galilea pilyia.
Pilyetala taono Nasarete dokonya kuki katapala, taono Kapename dokonya pao katea. Kapename doko Galilea pete lembasa, akali tata Sebyulanepa, Napatalaipanya yuu dokonya singi.
Dopa piamo dokome, wamba propeta Aisaiyame pii leamo dake angi jia:
“Endakali Napatalaipa, Sebyulanepa, dupanya yuu Jodane omotenapa, Galilea lembasapa, dupanya tii pipae andake mende ipatamopa, endakali kamalya katenge dupa-kisa tapyatamo kandatami. Kamalya katenge dupa, yuu iminjetaenya kumapae joo katangema dupa-kisa, tii pipae dokome tii pisetana” lea.
<range>
Gii dokopa pituu, Jisasame endakali dupa pii tee pyao lamaiyoo, “Gotenya isingi mate doko tengesa ipatelyamona, nyakama mona kapilyalapa” lea.
Jisasa Galilea pete lemba dokonya pao kandeamopa, pisa nyingi akali Saimone, kenge mende Pita lenge dokopa, kaiminingi Andruapame umbene nuu mende endaki pete dokonya pyandao, pisa nyoo kateambi.
Jisasame dolapo lamaiyoo, “Nyakambame pisa nyingimbali pyoo, endakali nyalapale mana langitoo, namba watao ipupa” lea.
Gii dokopaka akali dolapome, umbene nuu dupa yakinatala, baa watao peambi.
Umbisale pateaminopa, Jisasame akali Sebedi-pipa, ikiningi Jemesa, Jonepa sipi andaka umbene nuu tambuo peteambino kandatala, epena lea.
Dopa leamopa, nyakambanya takangepa, sipi dokopa yakinatala, Jisasa watao peambi.
Jisasame Galilea yuu doko pitakanya paeyao, endakali dupa Judamanya lotuu anda dupanya mana lamaita, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya lao, wai pii epe doko lamaita pia. Dee baame endakali yaina tata longome pyapae dupa, pitaka mee jeta pyakamaiya.
Baame piamo dupa Siria yuu doko, pitakanya lao taeyami. Dopa piamopa, endakali dupame yaina tata longome pyapaepi, tanda koo nengepi, imambu koo paletapi, mandipaeme nyingipi, papa tambutaepi, dupa pitaka laminao baa kateasa epeami. Dopa piaminopa, Jisasame yaina dupa mee jeta pyakamaiya.
Dokopa endakali kambu longo mendapuame, yuu Galileapi, Dekapolisapi, Jerusalemapi, Judiapi, endaki Jodane yangi-kaitapi, dupanya katao ipupala, Jisasa watao paeyami.
Jisasame endakali kambu longo dupa kandatala, baa yuu manda mendenya pao petea. Peteamo dokonya baanya disaipolo dupa epeami.
Dokopa baame tee pyao, dokaita dapa lao mana lamaiya:
“Endakali imambunya tipya joo katao, Goteme nisipya laka lao masingima dupa, Goteme minao auu pisingi. Auu pisetae dupa Gotenya isingi mate dokonya katatami.
“Endakali ee lao katengema dupa, Goteme minao auu pisingi. Auu pisetae dupa mona yaepao katatami.
“Endakali anasale joo katengema dupa, Goteme minao auu pisingi. Auu pisetae dupa Goteme yuu maituna leamo doko, nyakama nyetami.
“Lopo pilyamopapi, endaki nanu pilyamopapi, napu laka lao putiti kaengeli pyoo, mana tolatae dupa nyepala, watao minapu laka lao putiti kaeyao katenge endakali dupa, Goteme minao auu pisingi. Auu pisetae dupa Goteme maitamopa, nyakama etete yaka jeta.
“Endakali yango kondo kaenge dupa, Goteme minao auu pisingi. Auu pisetae dupa Goteme kondo kaeyata.
“Endakali Gote-kisa iki mona setenge dupa, Goteme minao auu pisingi. Auu pisetae dupame Gote kandatami.
“Endakali mona mendai paliu katamana lao, kyeto joo akema lengema dupa, Goteme minao auu pisingi. Auu pisetae dupa Goteme baanya ikiningina lata.
“Endakali Gotenya mana tolatae minilyamino latala, waka dupame tanda maitaminopa, tanda nenge dupa Goteme minao auu pisingi. Auu pisetae dupa Gotenya isingi mate dokonya katatami.
“Nyakamame namba watao minilyaminosa, endakali dupame nyakama kandao pii koo lao, sambo pii koo longo dupa lao, nyakama minao koeyasilyaminopa, Goteme nyakama auu pisingi.
Wamba propeta kateamino dupa, endakali dupame minao koeyasiamiakana, nyakama minao koeyasetamino dokopa, nyakama walu nalalapape. Yole etete andake doko kaitinya setekelyamona, nyakama eteke kaeyao, mona epe palyoo kalyepape,” Jisasame lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Nyakama yuu dakenya sole jepae kalyamino. Sole tende patamo doko, nyakamame aipa petala dee tende pisetamipi? Sole tende patae dokome mende napingi. Doko soo yakinatala moko katao nepenge.
“Nyakama yuu dakenya tii pipae joo kalyamino. Yuu taono mende manda mendenya silyamo doko, yalo pyoo nasingi. Dopaleaka joo, nyakama-kisa tii pipae doko yalo napipenge.
Endakali mendeme lama kaiyepae mende nyepala, penge mendenya koko pyandala naenge. Daa, baame nyepala, toko ketae dokonya setenge. Dopa pilyamo dokome, endakali andaka pilyamino dupa pitaka tii pingi.
Dopaleaka joo, nyakama-kisa tii pipae silyamo doko, endakali waka dupame kandena lao kalyepape. Dopa pitaminopa, dupame nyakamanya kalai epe pitamino dupa kandatala, nyakamanya Takange kaitinya katenge doko lao mambo pyatamina” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Mosesame loo seteamo dupapi, propeta dupame mana leamino, dupa nambame nyoo nepalanya epeepe lao masala naeyalapape. Dupa nambame nyoo nepalanya naepeo. Dupa angi jisalanya epeo.
Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Yuupi kaitipi dupa etatamopa, loo dupanya kuki etete mendaipi mende alu napita. Dupa alu napitamopaka, pii pepa pyapae silyamo dupa pitaka pyoo etata.
Dopana, endakali mendeme mana setapae dupanya kuki etete mende yalatala, endakali waka dupame dopaka pina lao mana lamaitamo doko, baa Gotenya isingi mate dokonya anasale joo katata. Dopaka doko, endakali mendeme mana setapae dupa watao minatala, endakali waka dupame dopaka pina lao mana lamaitamo doko, baa Gotenya isingi mate dokonya, alyasale joo katata.
Nambame nyakama langilyo: Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, Parasaipi, dupa ita minao nyakamame mana tolatae minala naeyatamino doko, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya napatamina” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “'Embame endakali yango mende tuu pyoo pyao kumasala naeyape. Pyao kumasetamo endakali doko, laminao kote laa pupengena' lao, wamba nyakamanya yumbange dupa lamaiyamino doko, nyakamame siami.
Dopaka doko, nambame nyakama dapa langilyo: Endakali mendeme endakali yango mende imbu kaeyatamo doko, laminao kote laa pupenge. Dee endakali mendeme, endakali yango mende kandao, lamba lao pii koo latamo doko, baa kanjole kambuingi andake doko-kisa laminao pupenge. Dee endakali mendeme mende kandao, kyakaenge mona napalengena latamo doko, baa ita tao katenge ele panda koo dokonya pupenge.
Dopana, embame endakali mende koeyasetala, Gote kundi maiya alta tengesa pao pituu, endakali mende koeyasipu doko imbu kaeyao pilyamo lao masetala,
embanya kundi maipenge doko dosa setapala, embame endakali doko katatasa pupala, lao tolasetala, mona yaepao dee kundi doko Gote maiya pilyepe.
“Dee endakali mendeme emba-pipa kote laanya pia kandeno dokopa, kaitinisa kote laa pao pituu, embame kote langitamo endakali doko mona auu pisakamaipi. Dopa napitino doko, endakali dokome emba laminao pao jasa doko maitamopa, dokome yanda singi dupa maita. Dokopa dupame emba anjinya palyetami.
Anjetae paliu, yanu dutupa pyao etateno dokopaka, emba mokatamina lao, nambame nyakama kiningi langilyona” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “'Embame kepo kolala naeyape' lao, wamba nyakamanya yumbange dupa lamaiyamino doko nyakamame siami.
Dopaka doko, nambame nyakama dapa langilyo: Akali mendeme enda mende lengeme kandatala, nyipu laka lao masilya dokome moname kepo kolenge.
Embanya lenge tolae dokome, koo pyaale lao mapisetamo doko, lukunya nepape. Emba lenge mendai iki tao, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya pupili doko, auu pipyali. Emba lenge lapota tapeta, ele panda ita tao katenge dokonya soo pyandamili doko, auu napipyali.
Embanya kingi tolae dokome, emba koo pyaale lao mapisetamo doko, kepanya nepape. Emba kingi mendai iki kateta, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya pupili doko, auu pipyali. Emba kingi lapota kateta, itate konjala naenge ele panda koo dokonya, pupili doko, auu napipyali.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “'Akali mendeme baanya enda doko yakinao pituu, enda yakinenge pepa doko pyao maipengena' lao, wamba nyakamanya yumbange dupa lamaiyamino doko, nyakamame siami.
Dopaka doko, nambame nyakama dapa langilyo: Enda mendeme kepo kolala naeyatamopa, akalingimi mee yakinatamopa, enda dokome akali waka mende nyetamo doko, akali wambatae doko mambele enda doko kepo kolata. Dee akali mendeme enda yukupae doko, nyetamo kandao doko, akali doko kepoaka kolatana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “'Kamongo dokonya kenge doko latala, embame kiningi etete pituna lateno doko, kaeyala naeyao latenoli pipi' lao, wamba nyakamanya yumbange dupa lamaiyamino doko, nyakamame siami.
Dopaka doko, nambame nyakama dapa langilyo: Embame pii mende lao pituu, kiningi etete lelyona laa naeyape. Salapape! Kaiti doko Gotenya petenge toko dokona, embanya pii lateno dupa kyeto tasalanya, kaitinya kenge latala, pii mende kiningi etete lelyona laa naeyape.
Yuu dake Gotenya moko setenge panda dokona, embame pii lateno dupa kyeto tasalanya, yuu dakenya kenge latala, kiningi etete lelyona laa naeyape. Jerusalema doko Kiŋi Andake dokonya taono dokona, embame pii lateno dupa kyeto tasalanya, Jerusalema kenge latala, kiningi etete lelyona laa naeyape.
Embame iti pumbuti mende kapo jina laa naeyate. Dee kapo mende pumbuti jina laa naeyate. Dopana, embame pii lateno dupa kyeto tasalanya, langalu minatala, kiningi etete lelyona laa naeyape.
Dopana, embame pii mende ŋee lao pituu, ŋee iki lape. Daa lao pituu, daa iki lape. Pii kyeto tasalanya, waipa sinyoo leleno, dupa Sataneme waipa singina” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “'Akali mendeme embanya lenge lukutamopa, itingi lengeaka lukope. Nenge longatamopa, itingi nengeaka longape' lao, wamba nyakamanya yumbange dupa, lamaiyamino doko nyakamame siami.
Dopaka doko, nambame nyakama dapa langilyo: Endakali mendeme emba-kisa koo pitamo doko yanu nanyepe. Endakali mendeme embanya wakena tolae-kaita, kingi kapame pia kandeno doko, yangi-kaita apata pina maipi.
Dee endakali mendeme, embanya yonge pee isa pingi doko, nyotoo lao kote lea kandeno dokopa, yonge pee-kisa pingi doko apata baa maipi.
Dee akali yanda singi mendeme, emba pyalanya petala, pinju soo tengesa umbisale katao mapa lea kandeno dokopa, londatili pao mapape.
Endakali mendeme oapi mende tee latamopa, maipi. Endakali mendeme yanu tee latamopa, maipiaka” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “'Embame embanya patali maki dupa auu kaeyape. Embanya yandapipi dupa imbu kaeyape' lao, wamba nyakamanya yumbange dupa lamaiyamino doko, nyakamame siami.
Dopaka doko, nambame nyakama dapa langilyo: Nyakamame nyakamanya yandapipi dupa auu kaeyao katao, nyakama koeyasilyamino dupa nisoo loma salapape.
Dopa pitamino dokome, nyakamanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokonya, wane joo katatami. Baame niki doko endakali koopi epepi, dupa pitaka-kisa tapina lenge. Baame aiyuu doko, endakali mana tolatae miningipi, mana koo miningipi, dupa pitakanya epena lenge.
Takisa nyingi akali dupame, endakali nyakama auu kaenge dupa, itingi auu kaengema. Dopaleaka joo, nyakamame endakali nyakama auu kaeyatamino dupa, iki auu kaeyatamino doko, dokonya aki yole mende nyetamipi?
Dee kamalya katenge endakali dupame, nyakamanya kaiminingi dupa pii epe lamaingima. Dopaleaka joo, nyakamame nyakamanya kaiminingi dupa, iki pii epe lamaitamino doko, mana aipale mendeme endakali kamalya katenge dupa, ita minatamipi?
Dopana, nyakamanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokome, endakali koopi, epepi dupa pitaka auu kaengena, nyakamame dopaka pyoo, auu kaeyao kalyepape” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Endakali dupame kandamili lao, nyakamame mana tolatae dupa minatamino doko, nyakamanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokome, yole mende nanditana, kandao kalyepape.
“Endakali Gote watao miningi mane-mane pingima dupame, nyakamanya lotuu andapi, kaitini kembopi, dupanya endakali dupame nyakama lalyipimili lao masoo, endakali tipya dupa maingima. Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Dopa pingi endakali dupame nyakamanya yole doko nyepelyaminona, nyakamame dopa napyepape.
Dopana, nyakamame endakali tipya dupa kingi tolae-kaitame nisoo pituu, kingi koeya-kaitame nakandena lao pyepape. Dopa pitamino dokome, endakali mendeme nakandata.
Nyakamame yalo pyoo nisepae maitaminopa, nyakamanya Takange dokome yalo pyoo maitamino doko kandatala, nyakama yole mende ditana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Nyakamame loma setamino gii dokopa, endakali Gote watao miningi, mane-mane pingima dupame, loma singimali pyoo sala naeyalapape. Dupame lotuu andapi, kaitini kembopi, dupanya katao, endakali enombanya loma sipuma laka lao masingima. Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Dopa pingi endakali dupanya yole doko nyepelyamino.
Nyakamame loma salanya pituu, nyakamanya palenge panda dokonya pao, kaita paii lanyetala, nyakamanya Takange yalo pyoo katenge doko lao loma salapape. Dopa pitaminopa, nyakamanya Takange dokome kandatala, nyakama yole mende dita.
“Kamalya katenge endakali dupame, pii tenge nakatenge longo dupa lao, nyakamanya sambo gote dupa lao loma singima. Dokaitame loma londe pyoo singi doko, sambo gote dupame auu kaeyao, sekelyaminona lao masingima.
Nyakama daa jilyamo dupa, tee laa naelyaminopa, wambao nyakamanya Takange Gote dokome masingina, nyakamame kamalya katenge dupame pingimali napyepape.
Nyakamame dapa lao loma salapape: Naimanya Takange ketae kaitinya katenge doko, embanya kenge doko auu pyoo sina lape.
Embanya isingi mate doko epena lape. Ketae kaitinya embanya masingili pingima, dopaka pyoo isa yuu dakenya pyepa lape.
Indupaka natamanoli pyoo, nee dupa dipi.
Naimanya koo pyekelyamino dupanya, yanu dupa kaelyamanona, embame naimanya koo dupanya yanu dupa kaeyape.
Koo pyepa lao makande pingi dupanya, pupa lao yakinala naeyape. Koo dupanya embame naima pyoo nyepe.
Dopana, endakali mendeme nyakama-kisa koo pingitamo dupa, kame setamino doko, nyakamanya Takange ketae kaitinya katenge dokome, nyakamanya koo dupa kameaka sakata.
Nyakamame endakali mendeme, koo pingitamo dupa kame nasetamino doko, Goteme nyakamanya koo dupa kame nasakatakana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Nyakamame Gote loma soo, nee nanao katao, endakali Gote watao miningi, mane-mane pingima dupame pingimali pyoo, enomba kumala naeyalapape. Dokaitame nee nanao kalyamini-lamo lao, endakali dupame nyakama kandena lao, enomba kumao lambalu pyapae paengema. Dopa pingi endakali dupame, nyakamanya yole doko nyepelyaminona lao, nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo.
Nyakamame Gote loma soo, nee nanao katao, endakali dupame nyakama nee nanao kalyaminona lao, masala naena lao, nyakamanya lengelyapi wasa pyapala, iti weleme kai pyapala kalyepape. Dopa pitaminopa, nyakamanya Takange yalo pyoo katenge dokome, iki kandata. Baame nyakamanya yalo pyoo pitamino doko kandatala, nyakama yole mende ditana” lea.
<range>
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Isa yuu dakenya oapi epe setelyamino dupa, kokalyame nao koeyasingi. Dee kaa tao koengeaka. Pake nenge endakali dupame, anda kalupala pake nyingimakana, nyakamame oapi epe dupa isa yuu dakenya nyoo setala naeyalapape.
Kaiti dokonya oapi epe setelyamino dupa, kokalyame nao koeyasala naenge. Dee kaa tao koeyala naengeaka. Pake nenge endakali dupame, anda kalupala, pake nanyingimakana, nyakamame oapi epe dupa kaitinya nyoo setalapape.
Nyakamanya oapi epe dupa setenge panda dokonyaka, nyakamanya mona yukuo setengemana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Lenge doko yongenya kia joo tenge. Embanya lenge doko auu pyoo tao paeyateno doko, embanya yonge doko pitaka etete tii pita.
Dopaka doko, embanya lenge lapota natao paeyateno doko, embanya yonge doko pitaka iminjeta. Emba-kisa kia telyamo doko konjetamopa, emba iminjetae andake mendenya katatena” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Endakali mendeme kamongo lapomanya, kalai pyakamaiya naeyapenge. Lapotanya kalai pyakamaitamo dokome, mende auu kaeyapala, mende doko auu kaeyala naeyata. Dee mende mona setapala, mende doko mona setala naeyata. Dopana, nyakama Gotepa, munipa, lapotanya kalai akali joo, nakatapengena” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Nyakamame nyakama tange auu pyoo, lete katapenge dupanya lao masetala, 'Naima neepi endakipi anja-tae nao katatamape? Yonge pee anja-tae pitamape?' lao masala naeyalapape. Lete katenge angi doko neepi, endakipi, yonge peepi, dopale daa.
Nyakamame yaka dupa kanjepape. Dupame ee pokala naengema. Dupame nee nyoo ipao setenge anda dupanya, mau pyala naengemaka doko, nyakamanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokome dupa nee maingi. Nyakamame yaka dupa etete ita minao kalyamino dokonya, Goteme nyakama nisala naeyatape?
Nyakamanya mendeme auu pyoo katapuli lao masepae longo nyetamo dokome, baanya lete katenge dokonya, ee kana mendatupa waipa setape?
Aipuma nyakamame yonge pee anja-tae pitamape lao, masepae longo nyilyamipi? Palao dii auu pyoo pilyamo dupa kanjepape. Dupa auu pisalanya tangeme kalai mende napingima. Dee yonge peepi mende wasala naengemaka.
Wamba Kiŋi Solomoneme, yati tata epe longo dupa pitaka piamoaka doko, palao dii auu pyoo pilyamo dopale mendeme, baa yati napiana lao, nambame nyakama langilyo.
Aipuma nyakamame Gote tungi kuki pilyamipi? Palao dii epapu telyamo, taita kepao yangapenge dupa, Goteme yati pisingi. Dopa pingi dokome, nyakama yonge pee pipenge dupa, kapa pao ditana lao masala naelyamipi?
Dopana, nyakamame neepi endakipi anja-tae natamape, yonge pee anja-tae pitamape lao masala naeyalapape.
Endakali kamalya katenge dupame, dopale dupa iki kutingi. Dopaka doko, nyakamanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokome, nyakama daa jilyamo dupa kandenge.
Dopana, nyakamame Gotenya isingi mate dokopi, baanya mana tolatae dokopi, dolapo wambao kutalapape. Dopa pitaminopa, Goteme nyakamanya nyepenge dupa dita.
Dopana, nyakamame taitanya lao masepae longo nyala naeyalapape. Taita kenda pipae ipatamo dupa, taita sepenge. Indupa kenda pipae ipatamo dupa, indupaka sepengena” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Nyakamame endakali mende koo epe lao yapala naeyalapape. Dopa pitaminopa, nyakama koo epe lao yapala naeyatamiaka.
Nyakamame endakali mende koo epe lao yapatamino kandao doko, nyakama dopaka pyoo yapatami. Nyakamame endakali mende yapatamino doko, makande mendai dokomeaka nyakama yapatami.
Embanya lengenya ita lyoo andake doko sina latala, mendenya lenge kuni yakane sipya doko, aipa petala kandakamaitipi?
Embanya lengenya ita lyoo andake mende setamopa, aipa petala embame waka mende kandao, 'Embanya lengenya kuni silyamona, nyakaowape' latepe?
Dopa lenge endakali doko, endakali waka dupame, mana tolatae minina lao mana latala, embame mana tolatae doko naminingi. Wambao embanya lengenya ita lyoo andake setamo doko, nyoo nepatala, lenge auu pyoo tao, waka dokonya lenge kuni setamo doko, nyoo nepakamaipi.
“Nyakamame Gotenya latae dupa, yana namaiyepape. Maitamino doko, yana dupame kapilyetala, nyakama natami. Dee nyakamanya mamaku epe dupa mena katataminya pyale nalalapape. Pyale latamino doko, dokaitame dupa moko katao, longao nepatamina” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Gote loma soo tee lelyamino endakali dupa pitaka, Goteme maingi. Kutilyamino endakali dupa pitaka, Goteme laitaka pingi. Anda kaita wata-wata pilyamino endakali dupa, pitakanya Goteme kaita lumbakamaingi. Dopana, nyakamame Gote loma soo tee lapape. Tee lataminopa, Goteme dita. Kutalapape. Kutataminopa, Goteme laitaka pita. Anda kaita wata-wata pyepape. Wata-wata pitaminopa, Goteme kaita lumbakata.
<range>
Waneme takange kandao, betesa natoo latamopa, nyakama apimi wane doko kana mende nena lao maitipi?
Waneme takange kandao, pisa natoo latamopa, nyakama apimi wane doko kanopato mende nena lao maitipi?
Nyakama takange dupa koaka doko, nyakamanya wane dupa, oapi epe maipenge dupa maingima. Nyakamanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokome, nyakama ita minao, baa-kisa tee lelyamino endakali dupa, oapi epe maipenge dupa maingi.
“Dopana, Mosesame loo seteamo dupanyapi, propeta dupame mana leamino dupanya, pii tenge angi lapae silyamo doko dake: Endakali waka dupame, nyakamanya pyakami laka lao masetamino dokoaka, nyakamame dokaitanya pyakamaiyepape” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Koo pandanya koeyala penge lome kaita doko, pee lapae. Kaitini dokonya endakali longo dupa, leke-leke natao pengema. Lete etete katenge panda dokonya penge lome kaita doko, etete yakane. Kaitini dokonya etete tanda nao pupenge. Lome kaita etete yakane dokonya, endakali kukimi kutao kandengema. Dopana, nyakama lome kaita yakane dokonya pupape” lea.
<range>
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Sambo propeta dupame sipisipi yanu nyoo petala, nyakama katatamisa ipatami. Dopa pitaminoaka doko, mona andaka yana kapu jetae ipatamina, wandyuu kalyepape.
Nyakamame dokaitanya mana minatamino dupa kandatala, dupa dopale-lamo lao masetami. Ikililyambu kende dupanya kopi lyingipi? Dee take ita dupanya anga lyingipi?
Ita epe dupame dii koo namandenge. Ita koo dupame dii epe namandengeaka. Ita epe dupa pitakame dii epeaka mandenge. Ita koo dupa pitakame dii koaka mandenge.
<range>
Dii epe namandenge ita dupa pitaka, pokapala itatenya soo yangenge.
Dopana, sambo propeta dupame mana makandepi, minatamino dupa kandatala, nyakamame dopale-lamo lao masetamina” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Namba kandao, mee 'Kamongo Kamongo' lenge endakali dupa pitaka, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya napatami. Nambanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokome, masingili pingima dupa iki patami.
Yuu etatamo gii dokopa, endakali longo dupame namba kandao, 'Kamongo Kamongo, naimame embanya kenge doko lao, wai pii epe doko lamaiyama. Naimame embanya kenge doko lao, imambu koo longo dupa watao piamaka. Naimame embanya kenge doko lao, mirakolo kalai longo dupa piamana' latami.
Gii dokopa nambame dokaita lamaiyoo, 'Nyakama koo pingi dupa, nambame nakandengena pupa' latona” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Nambame mana lalo dutupa sepala, watao minatami endakali dupa pitaka, akali masepae epe palenge mendeme kandatala, yuu kyeto mendenya anda muku minatala, anda piamo dopale.
Baame yuu kyetonya muku minatala, piamo dokonya, poo pupu lao lata, aiyuu ipata, endaki lyoo ipata piamopa, anda doko takyala naeya.
Nambame mana lalo dutupa sepala, watao minala naeyatamino endakali dupa pitaka, akali masepae napalenge mendeme, endaki keanya anda muku minatala, anda piamo dopale.
Baame endaki keanya muku minatala, anda piamo dokonya, poo pupu lao lata, aiyuu ipata, endaki lyoo ipata piamopa, anda doko kaluo koeya dokome, oapi dupa pitaka koeyakana” lea.
Jisasame mana leamo dupa, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali dupame lengemali pyoo nalenya, baa-kisa singi joo mana lea. Tenge dokonya, baame mana dutupa lao etapeamopa, endakali kambu longo peteamino dupame sepala, walu lao paka kaeyami.
<range>
Jisasame yuu manda doko yakinatala, lanao epeamopa, endakali kambu longome baa watao epeami.
Dokopa akali kopetali mendeme, Jisasa kateamo dosa ipao, luma lakapala baa lamaiyoo, “Kamongo, embame nambanya yaina dake mee jakalapo lao maseteno doko, mee jakalapenona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame akali doko kingimi watandatala baa lamaiyoo, “Nambame embanya yaina doko mee jipyali lao masilyona, epapu embanya yaina doko mee jekelyona” lea. Dopa leamopa yaina doko mee julu pia.
Dokopa Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Nambame embanya pyakalo doko, mende lamaiya naenya, pitisa dokome emba kandena puu. Pupala Mosesame wamba mana seteamoli pyoo, dopale mende Gote kundi maitinopa, endakali dupame embanya yaina doko, mee jipya-lamo lao kandenana” lea.
Jisasa Kapename pao pyakameamopa, yanda singi isingi akali mende ipupala, “Akali andake, nambanya kalai akali mende yainame tanda andake nao, andaka takyepae silyamona nisetepe?” lea.
<range>
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Nambame baa saka nyala ipatoana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, yanda singi isingi akali dokome, baanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Akali andake, emba nambanya andaka ipupenge, namba akali epe daana, embame piimi iki latenopa, nambanya kalai akali doko saka paapomo.
Nambanya isingi akali dokonya pundi-pundi namba katenge. Dee yanda singi mendapu, nambanya pundi-pundi katengemaka. Dupanya mende pena lelyopa, baa penge. Mende epena lelyopa, baa epenge. Dee nambanya kalai akali dokome, mende pina lelyopa, baame lelyoli pingina” lea.
Pii leamo doko walu lao sepala, Jisasame endakali baa watao epeamino dupa lamaiyoo, “Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Akali dakeme namba tungi pilyamoli pyoo, Israele tange mendeme, namba tungi pyaminopa nakandapu.
Endakali longo niki pyakaengesa tangepi, niki pambengesa tangepi, dupa ipao Gotenya isingi mate dokonya, Abrakame, Aisake, Jekope-pipa apata nee andake nao pititami.
Dopaka doko, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya katatamina latae endakali dupanya mendatupa, iminjetae panda koo dokonya watao pyandata. Dopa pitamopa, dokonya katao ee lao, yamataka lao, nenge gilyoo katatamina” lea.
Dopa latala baame yanda singi isingi akali doko lamaiyoo, “Embame namba tungi pyatala, tee leeno dokonya, embanya kalai akali doko saka pelyamona, andaka puu” lea. Dopa leamo gii dokopaka, isingi akali dokonya kalai akali doko saka pea.
Jisasa Pitanya andaka peamopa, Pitanya enda imange doko yonge itaita piamopa, yaina siamo kandea.
Kandatala baame enda dokonya kinginya watandeamopa, yonge itaita piamo doko mee jia. Mee jeteamopa, enda dokome sakatatala, Jisasa nee nyoo nena maiya.
Niki landa piamopa, endakali mendapuame imambu koo paleta endakali longo dupa, Jisasa kateasa laminao epeami. Dokopa Jisasame endakali dupa-kisa, imambu koo paleamo dupa, piimi watao pyata, endakali yaina pyapae dupa, pitaka mee jakamaita pia.
Baame dopa piamo dokome, wamba propeta Aisaiyame lao pituu, “Baame naimanya yongenyapi, imambunyapi, yaina dupa mee jakatana” leamo doko angi jia.
Endakali kambu mendeme, Jisasa baa katao kakopeamino kandatala, baanya disaipolo dupa lamaiyoo, “Naima Galilea pete omotena mua” lea.
Dokopa Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali mendeme, Jisasa kateasa ipupala lamaiyoo, “Mana Lenge Akali, emba paeyateli pyoo, namba watao ipatoana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Yana kapu dupanya palenge yuli tombapae dupa singi. Dee yaka dupanya anda katengeaka doko, Akalinya Ikiningi dokonya palenge anda mende nakatengena” lea.
Dokopa dee akali waka Jisasa watao paeyamino, dupanya mendeme baa lamaiyoo, “Kamongo, nambanya takange doko malu petala, emba watao ipatoo paowape?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Endakali kumapae joo kalyamino dupame, kumapae yango dupa malu pina, emba namba watao ipu” lea.
Dopa latala Jisasa baa sipi mendenya pyakalyiamopa, disaipolo dupa sipi dokonya apata pyakalyiami.
Pyakalyetala peaminopa, Jisasa luu palea. Paleamopaka, poo yale mende leamo dokome, endaki buli pyao tandyoo, sipi dokonya kolandea.
Dopa piamopa, disaipolo dupame baa pyale tatala, “Kamongo, naima mangalanya pilyamanona, embame naima nisepoko” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Aipuma nyakama paka kaelyamipi? Nyakama Gote kuki tungi pingima-lamona” lea. Dokopa baame sakatatala, poo leapi, endaki buli piapi, dupa pyalanya leamopa, kuki emapi mende napia.
Dopa piamopa, disaipolo dupame paka kaeyapala lao pituu, “Endakipa poopa dolapome, baanya pii lapyali pilyambino doko, akali dake api laa kanjemape?” leami.
Jisasa Galilea pete omotena, Gadara tangemanya yuu dokaita pao pyakameamopa, akali imambu koo longo palenge lapoma, endakali malu katenge dupanya paliu ipao, Jisasa kandanyiambi. Akali dolapo kapu joo kalyambinosa, endakali mende kaitini dokonya-kaita napaengema.
Dokopa akali dolapome puu lao, “Gote Ikiningi, embame naima aipa piti? Embame tanda andake dipenge gii seteamo doko, ipatala naeyapumupa, embame naima tanda andake wambao dyaanya epelepe?” leambi.
Kuki omosale mena elyambu mendapu nao kateami.
Dokopa imambu koo dupame Jisasa tee lao, “Naima pupale lao pyao watateno doko, mena dokaita-kisa landa pyalapa lapoko” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dupa kandao, “Pupa” lea. Dopa leamopa, imambu koo dupame akali dolapo soo yakinatala, mena dupa-kisa pao landa piami. Landa pyateaminopa, mena elyambu doko pitaka, papatale mendenya-kaita alo pyao pao, endaki pete mendenya mangatala kumiami.
Dokopa mena setao katenge akali dupame, taono dokonya alo pyao pupala, akali imambu koo palenge dolapo-kisa, piamo dupa pitaka lamaiyami.
Dopa leaminopa, taono dokonya palenge endakali dupa pitakame, Jisasa kutao pupala kandanyiami. Kandanyetala dokaitame kyeto joo, “Embame naimanya yuu dake yakinatala puu” leami.
Jisasa sipi dokonya pituu, Galilea pete omotena, baa katenge taono Kapename dokonya pyakamea.
Dokopa akali mendapuame akali papa tambutae mende lapa tokonya soo, baa kateasa epeami. Dopa piaminopa, dokaitame Jisasa baa tungi piamino doko kandatala, akali papa tambutae doko lamaiyoo, “Wane, embanya koo dupa kunao nepekelyona, emba mona yaepa” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali mendapuame, nyakamalapo laloo pyoo, “Akali dakeme Gote lamba lelyamona” leami.
Dopa lao masiamino dupa Jisasame kandatala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Aipuma koo dopale dupa masilyamipi?
Akali dakenya koo dupa kunao nepakamailyona lapu dokopa, nyakamame namba koo kunao nepenge, pupu lapae doko singi-lamo lao nakandelyamino. Dee akali dake lamaiyoo, “Emba sakatatala puu” lato dokopa, namba koo kunao nepenge pupu lapae doko singi-lamo lao kanjamino.
Dopaka doko, Akalinya Ikiningi dokome isa yuu dakenya katao, endakali dupanya koo dupa kunao nepenge pupu lapae doko, baa-kisa singi-lamo lao kanjepalena” lea. Dopa latala baame akali papa tambutae doko lamaiyoo, “Emba sakatatala, embanya lapa toko doko nyoo soo, andaka puu” lea.
Dopa leamopa, akali doko sakatatala andaka pea.
Dopa piamo doko, endakali kambu piamino dupame kandatala, pupu lapae dopale dupa Goteme, akali dake maiya-lamo lao paka kaeyapala, Gote mambo piami.
Jisasame yuu doko yakinao ipupala, akali takisa nyingi Matyu lenge mende, takisa nyingi anda dokonya peteamo kandatala, baa lamaiyoo, “Emba namba watao ipu” lea. Dokopa baa sakatatala, Jisasa watao pea.
Maitakao Matyunya andaka pupala, Jisasa disaipolo dupa-pipa peteaminopa, koo pingipi, takisa nyingipi, longo dupa ipupala, apata nee nao peteami.
Peteamino doko kandatala, Parasai dupame Jisasanya disaipolo dupa tipa pyoo, “Nyakamanya mana lenge akali doko, aipuma koo pingipi, takisa nyingipi, dupa-pipa nee nao pilyape?” leami.
Jisasame pii leamino doko sepala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Endakali yaina napingi dupa dokosa yangyala naenge. Endakali yaina pyapae dupa dokosa yangingi.
Gotenya pii lapae silyamo dake, nyakamame pao mana nyalapape: 'Kundi iki dingi doko, namba Gote dokome auu nakaenge. Endakali yango kondo kaenge doko, namba Gote dokome auu kaengena' lapae silyamo. Nambame endakali tolatae dupa, wii lao lanyalanya naepeo. Endakali koo pingi dupa, wii lao lanyalanya epeona,” Jisasame lea.
Gii dokopa Jone kaimbu pingi dokonya disaipolo dupame, Jisasa kateasa ipupala baa tipa pyoo, “Nee nanao loma singi gii dokonya, naimapi, Parasaipi, dupame Gote loma soo pituu nee nanengena, embanya disaipolo dupame aipuma dopa napingimape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaitanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Akali mendeme enda kelyapala, watapae pyao baanya tata dupa-pipa, apata kalyamino gii dokopa, baanya tata dupa-pipa nee nao, mona yaepao, auu kaeyao katengema. Akali enda kelyenge dopale joo, namba nyakama-pipa apata katao, nee nao kalyamano. Gii mendepa, akali waka mendapuame namba nyokonyoo patataminopa, nambanya disaipolo dupa loma soo, nee nanao katatamina” lea.
Dopa latala kongali pii mendeaka dee Jisasame lao pituu, “Endakali mendeme lapalapa kangupae enenge mendeme, yonge pee atingi mendenya tii telyamo dokonya, kii pimbala naenge. Endakali mendeme lapalapa etete enenge mende, atingi-kisa kii pimbatala wasa pyatamopa, enenge doko inungunyetamo dokome, atingi doko kanguo koeyaseta.
Dopaka pyoo, endakali mendeme waene enenge kamuo, penge meme yanungimi wasepae, atinginya pyandatamo dokome, waene doko bolo lapala, penge atingi doko kangutamopa, waenepa, pengepa, lapota koeyata. Tenge dokonya, waene enenge kamupae doko, penge atinginya kamuo pisala naenge. Waene enenge doko, penge enengenyaka kamuo pisingi, dokome waenepa, pengepa, dolaponya mende koeyala naengena” lea.
Jisasame Jone kaimbu pingi dokonya, disaipolo dupa pii lamaiyoo kateamopa, Judamanya lotuu anda mendenya isingi akali mende, Jisasa kateasa ipao luma lakapala baa lamaiyoo, “Nambanya wanenge doko epapu kumatalamona, dee lenge tena, embame baa-kisa kingi setala ipupoko” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasa disaipolo dupa-pipa sakatatala, akali doko watao peami.
Peaminopa, enda mende ee kana 12 dutupanya, yuu gii dii lao angupae kandenge dokome, Jisasanya maitakaita pupala, Jisasanya yonge peenya watandatopa, nambanya yaina doko mee jakalapomona lao masetala, yonge pee punanya watandea.
<range>
Dopa piamopa, Jisasame kapilyetala, enda doko kandatala, “Wanaku, embame namba tungi pyapino dokome, embanya yaina doko etelyamona, emba mona yaepatala puu” lea. Dopa leamo gii dokopaka, enda dokonya yaina doko etea.
Dokopa Jisasame isingi akali dokonya andaka pao kolandatala kandeamopa, endakali mendapuame kumanda pituu, pulupapu pyao ee wee leami.
Dopa piaminopa, baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Wanaku dake kumala naeyalamo, mee luu palelyamona, nyakama pyoo pupa” lea. Dopa leamopa, endakali dupame baa lamba lao, gii kaeyami.
Dopa piaminopa, Jisasame endakali dupa watao kamanda pyalyetala, baa wanaku kumapae siamo dokonya pea. Pupala wanaku doko kinginya minateamopa, sakatea.
Dopa piamo dokonya atome doko, yuu makisa singi dupa pitakanya taeya.
Jisasame yuu doko yakinatala peamopa, akali lenge monda mendalapome wii lao, “Dapiti Yumbange, embame nalimba kondo kaeyapoko” lao watao peambi.
Jisasa andaka kolandatala peteamopa, akali lenge monda dolapo epeambi. Epeambinopa, baame dolapo tipa pyoo, “Nyakamba nambame yaka nisalapeno lao masilyambipi?” lea. Dopa leamopa, dolapome yanu pyao, “Kamongo, kini embame yaka nisalapenona lao masilyambanona” leambi.
Dokopa Jisasame akali dolaponya lengenya watandatala lamaiyoo, “Nyakambame namba tungi pilyambino dokonya, masilyambinoli pilyamona” lea.
Dopa lalu piamopa, akali dolapo lenge talu piambi. Dokopa Jisasame akali dolapo kyeto joo lamaiyoo, “Nyakamba-kisa pyomo dake, endakali waka mende lamaiya naeyalapape” lea.
Dopa leamoaka doko, Jisasame piamo dupa pitaka, akali dolapome yuu makisa singi dupa pitakanya lao taeyambi.
Akali dolapo puu peteambinopa, endakali mendapuame imambu koo paleta akali muumaa mende, laminao Jisasa kateasa epeami.
Dokopa akali doko-kisa, imambu koo paleamo doko watao piamopa, muumaa doko pii lea. Dopa piamopa, endakali kambu piamino dupame kandatala, walu leami. Walu latala lao pituu, “Wamba naimame Israele tange endakali dupanya, mana dapale mende nakandeamana” leami.
Dopa leaminoaka doko, Parasai dupame lao pituu, “Imambu koo dupanya isingi doko baa-kisa ipao palipya dokome, imambu koo waka dupa watao pilyamona” leami.
Jisasame taono andakepi, yakanepi, dupa pitakanya paeyao, nyakamanya lotuu anda dupanya katao mana lamaita, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya lao wai pii epe doko, lamaita pia. Dee baame endakali yaina tata longome pyapae dupa mee jakamaiya.
Endakali kambu dupa sipisipi setao katenge, daa jepae katao kekeamino kandatala, Jisasame dokaita konda kaeya.
Kondo kaeyapala baame disaipolo dupa lamaiyoo, “Eenya nee longo wambu petelyamoaka doko, endakali mandyuu setapenge etete kuki kalyamino.
Dopana, kalai akali mendatupa apata nee mandyuu, setala pena lape lao, ee tange doko nyakamame loma salapape” lea.
Jisasame baanya 12 disaipolo dutupa epena latala, imambu koo dupa watao pyao, endakali yaina tata longome pyapae dupa mee joo, kalai pina lao, pupu lapae doko, dokaita maiya.
12 aposolo dutupanya kenge dupa, wambao doko Saimone, baanya kenge mende doko Pita, baanya kaiminingi Andru, Sebedi ikiningi Jemesa, baanya kaiminingi Jone,
Pilipa, Batolomyu, Tomasa, takisa nyingi akali Matyu, Alopiasa ikiningi Jemesa, Tadiusa,
Saimone, baanya kenge mende doko Selote, Jisasa enge nyiamo akali doko, Judasa Iskariota, akali dutupa yapao nyia.
Jisasame 12 disaipolo dutupa, kalai pyaa pena latala lamaiyoo, “Endakali kamalya katengemapi, yuu Samaria dokonya taono singipi, dupanya nyakama napupape.
Israele tange sipisipi alu petae joo, kalyamino dupanya pupape.
Pupala, “Gotenya isingi mate doko tengesa ipatelyamona” lao lamaiyepape.
Endakali yaina pyapae dupa saka nyalapape. Kumapae dupa lenge tasalapape. Kopetali dupa mee jakamaiyepape. Imambu koo dupa watao pyakamaiyepape. Nyakamame mee nyilyamino dokonya, meaka maiyepape.
Nyakamame muni mendaipi mende manja naeyao mee pupape.
Akali kalai pilyami dupame, nee toma nengema. Nyakama kalai pyaa patamino yuu dupanya, endakali dupame nyakama nisepengena, nokainapi, moko peepi, pangalipi, yonge pee wakaowapi, mende nyoo napupape.
Nyakama taono andake-tamopi, yakane-tamopi, mendenya pataminopa, endakali mendeme nyakama auu kaeyao lanyeta mende kutao kandatala, doko-pipa iki katao etapala, pupenge gii dokonya, baa yakinatala pupape.
Nyakamame anda dokonya kolandatala, endakali dokonya palenge dupa auu kaeyao, kingi nyepala, “Nyakama Goteme nisalapomona” lapape.
Endakali dupame nyakama auu pyoo lanyetamino doko, nyakamanya pii epe latami doko, dupa-kisa sina kaeyalapape. Dopa napitamino doko, nyakamanya pii epe latami doko tange nyalapape.
Yuu tange mendeme nyakama auu kaeyao lanyala naeyao, nyakamanya pii doko nasoaka pia kandeno doko, andapi, taonopi dupa yakinatala pao pituu, mokonya yuu katatamo dupa lyanda lanya, setapala pupape.
Goteme endakali dupa mokosetamo gii dokopa, taono dokonya kenda pipae ipatamo dokome, taono Sodomo Gomorapanya kenda pipae ipatamo doko, ita minao ipatana lao, nambame nyakama kiningi langilyona” Jisasame lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Nambame nyakama sipisipi jepae dupa, yana kapu dupanya kainanya pupa lelyo. Dopana, nyakama kanopato dupame waa katengeli pyoo, kandao waa katao kalyepape. Yaka maiyolee dupame ema napyoo, mende minao koeyasala naeyoo petengeli pyoo pilyepape.
Nyakama endakali mendapuame nyakamanya lotuu anda dupanya, kote lamana latala, laminao pupala, konjame pyatamina, kandao isoo kalyepape.
Nyakamame namba tungi pyatala, watao paelyamino dokonya, endakali dupame nyakama pyalya lao soo, kiŋipi, gapenapi, dupanya enombanya katasetami. Katasetaminopa, nyakamame wai pii epe doko kiŋipi, gapenapi, endakali kamalya katengepi, dupa panao lamaitami.
Endakali dupame nyakama anjetala laminao, kote anda dupanya pataminopa, nyakamame pii aki lamanape, aipa pyoo lamanape lao masala naeyalapape. Kote lapenge gii dokopa, nyakamame pii lapenge dupa, Goteme dita.
Nyakamame latamino doko, masoo laa naeyatami. Takangenya Oli Spirit dokome, lungu pitamopa latamina” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Akali mendapuame nyakamanya kaiminingi etete dupa, enge nyepala, pyao kumasina lao maitami. Akali mendapuame nyakamanya wane dupa dopaka pitami. Wane mendapuame kandapilyetala, nyakamanya endangi takangepi dupa pyao kumasina lao maitamiaka.
Nyakamame namba watao paeyatamino kandatala, endakali dupa pitakame nyakama etete imbu kaengitami. Dopa pitaminopapi, endakali mendeme kyeto joo katao etatamo doko, baa Goteme pyoo nyeta.
Dopana, endakali dupame taono mendenya, nyakama minao koeyasetamino dokopa, taono doko yakinatala, mendenya paka pupape. Nyakamame Israele yuu dokonya, taono dupa pitakanya kalai pyoo etala naeyataminopa, Akalinya Ikiningi doko ipatana lao, nambame nyakama kiningi langilyona” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Mana nyingi akali mendeme, baanya mana lamaingi akali doko ita naminingi. Kalai akali mendeme baanya isingi akali doko ita naminingiaka.
Endakali dupame mana lenge akali doko, mana maitaminoliaka pyoo, mana nyingi akali doko mana maitami. Isingi akali doko mana maitaminoliaka pyoo, kalai akali doko mana maitami. Dopana, endakali dupame namba isingi akali doko kandao, kenge koo Belesabulu ditamino dokonya, nyakama nambanya tata dupa kandao, kenge etete koo mendapu ditamiakana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Sanga pyatae silyamo dupa pitaka tenda lopalyeta. Yalo petae silyamo dupa tenda panaseta. Dopana, nyakamame Gotenya yalo petae dupa panao lamaitaminopa, endakali dupame nyakama minao koeyasetamino lao paka nakaeyalapape
Nambame pii elyakalao langilyo dupa, panao lamaiyepape. Pii kakateme langilyo dupa, yuu manda dupanya katao wii lao lamaiyepape.
Yonge doko pyao kumasetamino dupame, imambu doko pyao kumasala naeyatamina, paka nakaeyalapape. Yongepi, imambupi, lapota pyao koeyasetala, ele panda koo dokonya pyandatamo akali doko, paka kaeyalapape.
Endakali dupame 10 toeame iki, yaka pimbinakae lapoma sambamili. Dopaka doko, Takange Gote dokome yaka dupanya mendaipi mende kumala naena lao, masilyamo doko, dupanya mende isa mangatala, kumala naengema.
Dopaka pyoo, Goteme nyakamanya aiyomba iti dupa pitaka, mendai-mendai lao itaki pingi.
Nyakamame yaka pimbinakae dupa ita minao kalyaminona, paka nakaeyalapape” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Endakali mendeme endakali waka dupanya enombanya, namba Kraisa tatana latamo doko, nambame nambanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokonya enombanya, baa namba tatakana lato.
Dopaka doko, endakali mendeme endakali waka dupanya enombanya, namba Kraisa tata daana latamo doko, nambame nambanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokonya enombanya, baa namba tata daakana latona” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Nambame isa yuu dakenya, endakali dupa mona setao katena epeena lao masala naeyalapape. Daa, endakali dupa mona setao katena lao naepeo. Wakale pyoloo pingi mana doko, sakatasala epeo.
Ikiningipa takangepa wakale pyoloo pingipi, wanengepa endangipa wakale pyoloo pingipi, aeyangepa wakale pyoloo pingipi, nambame mana doko, mapisala epeo.
Tenge dokonya, endakali mendenya taiyoko etete dupame, baa yandapipili jetami.
“Endakali mendeme baanya endangipi, takangepi, ikiningipi, wanengepi, mende moname etete auu kaeyapala, namba mee yongeme auu kaeyatamo doko, baa kapa pao namba tata joo nakatata.
Dee endakali mendeme, baanya poko ita doko tange nyoo soo, namba watao naipatamo doko, baa kapa pao namba tata joo nakatataka.
Endakali mendeme namba yakinatala, baa tange auu pyoo katapuli lao masetamo doko, baa koeyata. Endakali mendeme namba lao masetala, baa tange kame setamo doko, baa auu pyoo katatana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Endakali mendeme nyakama lanyetamo dokome, namba lanyeta. Namba lanyetamo dokome, namba puu leamo akali doko lanyetaka.
Endakali mendeme propeta mende baa propeta-lamona latala, lanyetamo doko, propeta dupa Goteme yole maitamoliaka pyoo, maita. Dee endakali mendeme akali mende tolatae-lamona latala, lanyetamo doko, akali tolatae dupa Goteme yole maitamoliaka pyoo, maita.
Dee endakali mendeme endakali tipya datupanya mende, namba watao paenge-lamona latala, endaki iki kamuo maitamo doko, baa tenda Goteme yole mende maitana lao, nambame nyakama kiningi langilyona” lea.
Jisasame baanya 12 disaipolo dutupa, mana lamaiyoo etapala, baa kateamo panda doko yakinatala, Galilea taono waka singi dupanya, wai pii epe doko mana lamaiyanya pea.
Jone kaimbu pingi doko anjetae paliu, Kraisame kalai pupu lapae dupa pilyamo lapae sepala, baanya disaipolo mendatupame Kraisa kateasa pupala, “Emba akali naima pyoo nyala ipatana latae singi dokope, pande naimame akali waka mende malisemape?” lao, tipa pyoo sala pena lea.
<range>
Dupame Jisasa kateamo dokonya pupala, baa tipa piaminopa, Jisasame dokaitanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Nyakama pilyetala, kandelyaminopi, silyaminopi, dupa Jone lamaiyepape.
Lenge monda dupa dee lenge telyamino. Moko koo dupa kaita paelyamino. Endakali kopetali dupa mee jakamailyamo. Kaleketa dupame pii silyamino. Endakali kumapae dupa sakatatala paelyamino. Endakali tipya dupame wai pii epe doko silyamino.
Dee akali mendeme namba maka kaeyapala, mona lapo palyala naenge doko, Goteme auu pisetae kalyamona lao Jone lamaiyepape” lea.
Jonenya disaipolo dutupa pilyoo pateaminopa, endakali kambu dupa Jone kaimbu pingi dokonya lao, Jisasame pii mendapu lamaiyoo, “Wamba nyakamame endakali napalenge yuu dokonya, aki mende kanja peami? Kembo yokopi mende poome ema-ema piamo kanja peamipi,
pande akali mende yonge pee yati pipae epe mendapu pyoo kateamosa, kanja peamipi? Daa, akali yonge pee yati pipae epe pingi dupa, kiŋi dupanya andaka katengema.
Nyakama peamino doko, propeta mende kateamo kanja peami. Propeta doko baa mee ambe propeta mende daa.
Akali doko kandao, Goteme dapa lea: 'Salapape! Nambame nambanya wai akali doko, wambao pena latopa, Mesaeya dokonya kaitini doko depa lakamaitana' lao pepa pyapae silyamo.
Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Yuunya endakali dupa pitaka, Jone kaimbu pingi dokome ita minao katea. Dopaka doko, endakali mende Gotenya isingi mate dokonya, anasale joo kalyamo dokome, Jone ita minilyamo.
Jone kaimbu pingi dokome, pii lamaiyoo kateamo gii dokonya pituu, indupa tuu lao, endakali longo dupame Gotenya isingi mate doko, nyakamanya pupumi nyepala, isemana lelyamino.
Joneme pii tee pyao lamaitala naeyamopa, Mosesame loo seteamo dupapi, propeta dupame mana leamino dupapimi, Gotenya isingi mate doko ipatana leami.
Nyakamame dake kiningi-lumuna lao masetamino doko, dake salapape: Ilaija ipatana lao pii pepa pyapae singi doko, Jone kaimbu pingi doko kandao latae singi.
Nyakama kalekaita singi dupame, pii doko auu pyoo salapape.
“Endakali indupa gii dakepa kalyamino dupa, aki mendepa nambame makande pyuape? Nyakama wane kole dupame, kamapusa kambu lapoma pyapala, mumu lao wii laloo pingi dopale. Wane kole dupame dapa lengema: 'Naimame nyakamanya pulupapunya wee pyakamanopa, dokonya danisa laa naeyalamino. Naimame kondo kaeyao ee wee lenge doko lapumanopa, nyakamame ee laa naeyalamino.'
<range>
“Dopaleaka joo, endakali dupame Jone kandao, betesa waenepi dupa nanao kateamopa, mumu lao baa-kisa imambu koo mende palelyamona leami.
Dopaka doko, endakali dupame Akalinya Ikiningi doko kandao betesa waenepi, longo lao napumupa, mumu lao baa nee tiaka nakaeyao nenge-lamona lelyamino. Endakali koo pingipi, takisa nyingipi, dupa kaita minao apata kalyamona' lelyamino. Dopaka doko, Gotenya masepae epe nyilyami dupa watao minilyaminopa, masepae epe dokome kalai tolatae pipenge dupa, pipae singina,” Jisasame lea.
Jisasame mirakolo kalai longo piamo taono dupanya tange endakali dupa, mona kapilyala naeyaminosa, baame pyalanya lao pituu,
“Taono Korasina tangepi, Betsaida tangepi, dupa nyakama koeyatamina, kandao kalyepape. Mirakolo kalai nyakamanya taono dupanya, pio dupa, taono Saidone tangepi, Taeya tangepi, dupame kandeamili doko, nyakamame yonge pee pumbuti dupa petala, yonge lindi pyapala, wamba mona kapilyiamili.
Goteme endakali mokosetamo gii dokopa, Taeyapi, Saidonepi, dupa-kisa tenge andake setataka doko, nyakama Korasina tangepi, Betsaida tangepi, dupa-kisa Goteme tenge eteteaka andake setata.
Dee nyakama taono Kapename tange dupa, kapa pao kaiti-kisa patama lao masilyamipi? Daa, Goteme nyakama ele panda koo dokonya, watao pyandata. Mirakolo kalai nyakamanya yuu dupanya pio dupa, Sodomo tange dupame kandeamili doko, mona kapilyiaminopa, yuu doko koeyala naeyali.
Goteme endakali mokosetamo gii dokopa, Sodomo tange dupa-kisa, tenge andake setataka doko, nyakama Kapename tange dupa-kisa, Goteme tenge eteteaka andake setatana” lea.
Gii dokopa Jisasame lao pituu, “Apane, emba yuupi, kaitipi, dupa pitakanya Kamongo. Mana longo kandenge endakalipi, mana longo nyepae endakalipi, dupame nakandena lao yalo piino dupa, wane ŋaŋa joo katengema endakali dupame, kandena lao embame panasino dokonya, nambame emba lao mambo pilyo.
Kini Apane, embame pituna lao auu kaengeme masinoli pyoo pii-lamo.
Nambanya Takangeme dupa pitaka nambame isepe lao, namba-kisa setea. Endakali mendeme Ikiningi doko angi nakandenge. Takangeme iki kandenge. Dee endakali mendeme Takange doko angi nakandengeaka. Ikiningimi iki kandenge. Dee Ikiningi dokome, Takange doko endakali mendeme kandena lao masetala, laitaka petelyamopa, endakali dokome Takange doko-lamo lao kandenge.
Nyakamame kenda pipae longo dupa soo, popo tandapi neami kandeno doko, namba katatosa soo ipupape. Nambame nisotopa, nyakama imambu nyetami.
Namba akali andiki pipae mende, namba anasale joo katenge. Nyakamame nambanya pii doko watao minao, namba-kisa mana nyala ipupape. Nyepala dokopa, nyakama imambu setami.
Nambanya kaitini dokonya paenge endakali dupa, leke-leke natao paengema. Nambame dopale mende salapale lao dilyo doko, kenda napingina” Jisasame lea.
Sambata gii mendenya, Jisasapi baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa, wita ee kaina mendenya kaita pao pituu, baanya disaipolo dupame lopo kaeyapala, wita dii kii lanyetala tambao neami.
Dopa piaminopa, Parasai dupame kandatala Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Embanya disaipolo dupame Sambata gii dokonya, daa latae singi mana doko minilyamino kanda” leami.
Dokopa Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Dapitimi piamo doko nyakamame pepanya itaki napiamipi? Dapitipi, akali apata kateamino dupa lopo kaeyami. Lopo kaeyapala Dapitimi Gotenya lotuu andaka kolandatala, betesa Gote opa maitae, pitisa dupame iki napenge siamo dupa nyepala, akali dupa maiyoo nea.
<range>
Dee Sambata gii dupanya, pitisa dupame lotuu anda andake dokonya, Gotenya enombanya koeyala naeyao, kalai pingimana lao pepa pyapae singi doko, itaki napiamipi?
Akali asa kalyamo dokome, lotuu anda andake doko ita minao kalyamona lao, nambame nyakama langilyo.
Gotenya pii mende dapa lao pepa pyapae singi: 'Endakalimi namba kundi iki dingima mana doko, nambame auu nakaenge. Endakali yango kondo kaenge mana doko, nambame auu kaenge.' Pii dakenya tenge dupa nyakamame siamili doko, endakali tenge nakatenge dupa-kisa, tenge setala naeyamili.
Akalinya Ikiningi dokome, Sambata gii dokonya apata isoo kalyamoakana,” Jisasame lea.
Dokopa Jisasame ee doko yakinatala, Judamanya lotuu anda dokonya andakote pea.
Peamopa, akali kingi yangi talyanga mende peteamo doko, Jisasame tolasakamaitamopa, Parasai dupame Jisasa kote lamana lao masetala, baa tipa pyoo, “Sambata gii dupanya endakali yaina pyapae dupa, mee jakamaipengepe, daape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Sambata gii mendenya, nyakamanya sipisipi mende yulinya mangatamopa, tange pao kopyoo nanyetamipi?
Sipisipi dupa endakalimi ita minao kalyamino. Dopana, Sambata gii dokonya naimame kalai epe pyoo, endakali dupa nisepengena” lea.
Dopa latala baame akali kingi yangi talyanga doko lamaiyoo, “Embanya kingi doko tinoka” lea. Tinokateamopa, kingi epe yangi dopaleaka jia.
Dopa piamopa, Parasai dupame lotuu anda doko yakinatala, Jisasa pyao kumasemana latala, kamaka pao kambuiyami.
Kambuiyamino kandatala, Jisasame yuu doko yakinatala pea. Dokopa endakali longo dupame baa watao peamino dupanya, endakali yaina pyapae dupa pitaka mee jakamaiya.
Jisasame yaina mee jakamaiyamo dokaita, kyeto joo lamaiyoo, “Nambame dopa pyakalamona lao, mende lamaiya naeyalapape” lea.
Dopa piamo dokome, Goteme propeta Aisaiya-kisa pii lea mende, angi paneamo doko dake:
“Dake nambanya kalai akali, nambame baa yapao nyio doko. Baa nambanya etete mona setenge doko. Namba tange baa etete auu kaenge. Nambanya Spirit doko baa maitupa, baame nambanya mana tolatae doko, akali tata dupa pitaka panao lamaita.
Baame kaitinisa katao, pii yanda pyoo, pii puu lao latamopa nasetami.
Kembo maitange tambapae mende, baame etete lakanyala naeyata. Ita langa konjalanya kii lao seta mende, baame etete konjesala naeyata. Dopaka pyoo, baame endakali dupa kondo kaeyao, baanya mana tolatae dokome, koo dupa pitaka ita minata.
Akali tata dupa pitakame, baame tanga pyoo nyala ipatana lao, malisoo katatamina” lapae silyamo.
Gii dokopa endakali mendapuame, akali lenge monda, muumaa imambu koo paleta mende laminao, Jisasa kateasa epeami. Jisasame akali doko auu pyoo niseteamopa, baa pii lao, lenge tao pia.
Baame piamo dupa kandatala, endakali kambu piamino dupa pitakame walu latala, “Akali dake Dapiti Yumbange dokope?” leami.
Parasai dupame pii doko sepala lao pituu, “Baa-kisa imambu koo dupanya isingi, Belesabulu doko ipao palipya dokome, imambu koo waka dupa watao pilyamona” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame masiamino dupa kandatala, dokaita lamaiyoo, “Kiŋi mendenya tata doko pyaloo petala, nyakama wakale pitamino doko, pitaka koeyatami. Dee taono mendenya tangepi, akali mendenya enda wanepi, dupa wakale pyoloo petala, nyakama yangolapo pyaloo pitamino doko, nyakama saa latami.
Dopaka pyoo, Satane tata doko pyaloo petala, nyakama wakale pitamino doko, baame aipa petala ita minatape?
Belesabulu dokome namba pupu lapae dilyamopa, imambu koo dupa watao pingina lelyamino. Dopa lelyamino doko, nyakamanya disaipolo dupa apimi pupu lapae mailyamopa, imambu koo dupa watao pingina lelyamipi? Nyakamanya disaipolo dupameaka, nyakamame kopeta lapimi-lamona latami.
Goteme Oli Spirit dokonya pupu lapae doko, namba ditamopa, imambu koo dupa watao pyato doko, Gotenya isingi mate doko nyakama-kisa ipao setamosa pita.
Akali mendeme akali pupu lapae mendenya, andaka kolandatala, baanya pinju dupa pake nyalanya-tamo doko, wambao kendeme baa yaki pinya setapala nyeta.
Endakali mende namba tata joo nakalyamo, doko nambanya yandapipi. Dee endakali mendeme namba nisoo, endakali dupa Goteme nisina lao nyoo kambu pyala naelyamo, dokome endakali dupa Gotenya isingi mate dokonya, watao pingi.
Tenge dokonya, nambame nyakama langilyo: Goteme endakali dupanya koo pingipi, lamba lengepi, dupa pitaka kunao nepakamaita. Dopaka doko, endakali mendeme Oli Spirit doko kandao, lamba latamo doko, Goteme baanya koo doko, kunao nepakamaiya naeyata.
Endakali mendeme Akalinya Ikiningi doko kandao, lamba latamo doko, Goteme baanya koo doko kunao nepakamaita. Dopaka doko, endakali mendeme Oli Spirit doko kandao, lamba latamo doko, Goteme baanya koo doko kunao nepakamaiya naeyatamopa, baa-kisa tanga tangapi sulu setana,” Jisasame lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Ita epe dupame dii epeaka mandenge. Ita koo dupame dii koaka mandenge. Ita mendenya dii mandelyamo dupa, wambao kandatala, ita angi doko dopale-lamo lao masingima.
Nyakama koo kanopatonya mandipae dupame, aipa petala pii epe mende latamipi? Endakalinya monanya paliu tumbilyamo dokoaka, kambunya pyakalyingi.
Endakali mendenya monanya epe palelyamo dokoaka, kambunya pyakalyingi. Dee endakali mendenya monanya koo palelyamo dokoaka, kambunya pyakalyingi.
Nambame nyakama dapa langilyo: Tanga Goteme mokosetamo gii dokopa, embanya pii koo lateno dutupanyaka, Goteme emba aipuma leepe lao tipa petala mokoseta.
Emba tangenya pii dokonyaka, Goteme emba-kisa tenge mende nasilyamona lata. Daa-tamo doko, emba tangenya pii dokonyaka, Goteme tenge emba-kisa silyamona, latana” lea.
Gii dokopa Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, Parasaipi, mendapuame Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Embame kalai pilino doko, Gote-kisa katao pilini-lamo lao kandamana, mirakolo mende pii” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaitanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Endakali Gote yakinao, koo pingi palelyamino dupame mirakolo mende nyakama kandamana lao tee lelyaminoaka doko, nambame mirakolo mende kanjepale napyakatoo. Goteme kongali mende, propeta Jonaa-kisa piamo mendai dokoaka, nyakama kandataminopa dita.
Wamba Jonaa doko kotaka gii tepo, kuka gii tepoaka, pisa andake mendenya ingi koko paleamoliaka pyoo, Akalinya Ikiningi doko, kotaka gii tepo, kuka gii tepoaka, malunya palita.
Wamba Jonaa dokome yuu Ninipe tange dupa, pii panao lamaiyamopa, dokaitame sepala, mona kapilyiami. Indupa akali mende kalyamo dokome, Jonaa nyoo ana pyandao katamupa, nyakamame baanya pii doko sepala, mona kapilyala naelyamino. Tenge dokonya, Goteme endakali mokosetamo gii dokopa, endakali Ninipe tange dupame sakatatala, nyakama Parasaipi, endakali epapu pii silyamino, dupa-kisa tenge setatami.
Wamba kuini enda Seba tange dokome, yuu londati waka pituu, Kiŋi Solomonenya masepae epe dupanya pii yandaita dupa, nyotoo lao epea. Indupa akali mende kalyamo dokome, Kiŋi Solomone nyoo ana pyandao katamupa, nyakamame baanya masepae epe dupanya, pii yandaita dupa nanyilyamino. Tenge dokonya, Goteme endakali mokosetamo gii dokopa, kuini enda Seba tange dokome, sakatatala nyakama Parasaipi, endakali epapu pii silyamino dupa-kisa, tenge setatana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Imambu koo mendeme endakali mende yakinatala, yuu sapu dupanya katapenge panda kutingi. Kutao kaeyapala
lao pituu, 'Nambame anda wamba yakineo dokonya, dee pilyotoo' lenge. Dopa latala baa pilyetala kandelyamopa, anda dokonya mende napaliu, auu pyoo tolasetae kalyamo kandenge.
Dopa petae kalyamo kandatala, baa pao imambu etete koo 7-pela apata lanyepala, anda dokonya dee pilyetala katengema. Wamba akali doko kopeta kateamoaka doko, imambu koo dupa baa-kisa ipao paleaminopa, baa etete kopeta katea. Dopa piana, gii dakepa nyakama endakali etete koeyapae palelyamino dupa, mona kapilyala naeyatamino kandao doko, koeyatami iki-lamona” lea.
Jisasame endakali kambu dupa pii lamaiyoo kateamopa, baanya endangipi, kaiminingipi dupa ipao, baa pii lamaimana lao, kamaka kateami.
Dopa piaminopa, akali mendeme Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Embanya endangipi kaiminingipi kamaka katapala, emba pii langimana lelyaminona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame akali dokonya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Nambanya endangi doko apipi? Nambanya kaiminingi dupa apitupape?” lea.
Dopa latala baanya kingi kondeme, endakali baa watao epeamino dutupa laitaka petae katao, “Pii soo pilyamino datupa, nambanya endangipi kaiminingipina kanjepa.
Nambanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokonya masingili pingima, endakali dupa nambanya kaiminingipi, pimalengepi, endangipina” lea.
Gii dokopaka Jisasame anda doko yakinatala pao, Galilea pete lembasa petea.
Peteamo dokonya endakali etete longo mendapu ipao, kambu piaminosa, baa sipi mendenya pyakalyetala petea. Dokopa endakali kambu doko pitaka, endaki pete lemba dokonya kateami.
Kateaminopa, Jisasame kongali lao endakali dupa, mana lamaiyoo dapa lea: “Akali mendeme ee wai lyandala pea-pyaa.
Lyandeamopa, ee wai yangi kaitininya pea. Peamo dupa pitaka yaka dupame nyoo neami.
Yangi kana-kisa yuu kuki singi dupanya peamo dupa, pupae langa lea.
Langa leamoaka doko, pingi auu pyoo napiamosa, niki teamo dokome kumasia.
Yangi yuu ikililyambu nenge-nenge katapae tenge palenge, dupanya pea. Peamo dupa langa leamoaka doko, ikililyambu tambe-tambe andapala, kui pyambea.
Ee wai yangi lyandeamo dupa, yuu epenya pupala, andao dii mandea. Yangimi 100 mandea, yangimi 60 mandea, yangimi 30 lao dii mandea.
Nyakama kalekaita singi dupame, pii doko auu pyoo salapapena” lea.
Maitakao disaipolo dupame Jisasa kateasa ipupala, baa tipa pyoo, “Embame endakali dupa kongaliaka lao pii lamaiyoo kalyeno doko, aipuma pilipi?” leami.
Baame nyakamanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Gotenya isingi mate dokonya, pii tenge yalo petae palelyamo doko, nambame nyakama panao langitoo. Dopaka doko, endakali waka dupa panao lamaiya naeyato.
Endakali mende-kisa Gotenya pii setamo doko, baa konda pyoo maita. Dopaka doko, Gotenya pii nasingi mende-kisa kuki setamopa, sekelyamo lao masetamo doko, dutupa tange nyokonyeta.
Endakali dupame lengeme kandelyaminoaka doko, tenge angi doko nakandelyamino. Kaleme silyaminoaka doko, tenge angi doko nyala naelyamino. Tenge dokonya, nambame endakali dupa kongali pii lao lamaingi.
Goteme propeta Aisaiya-kisa pii dapa lea: 'Nyakamame pii kaleme setamiaka doko, tenge angi doko soo nanyetami. Nyakamame lengeme kandatamiaka doko, tenge angi doko kandao nanyetami.
Endakali dakaitanya mona pyakilyia dokome, kale poeyamosa pii nasoo, lenge iminjiamosa kanja naeyao pilyamino. Dee kaleme sepala, lengeme kandatala, mona tii pitamopa, mona aloo petala, namba tungi pyamili doko, nambame pyoo nyipuli.
Dopaka doko, nyakama nambanya pii singi dupa, Goteme auu pisimupa, nyakamame lengeme angi kandao, kaleme angi pii soaka pilyamino.
Nyakamame kandelyamino dupa propeta longopi, endakali tolatae longopi, dupame kandatamana lao, nea kaeyao malisiaminoaka doko, angi nakandeami. Dee dupame setamana lao, nea kaeyao malisiaminoaka doko, angi nasiamina lao, nambame nyakama kiningi langilyona” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Akali mendeme ee wai lyandea dokonya, tenge doko dakena salapape.
Ee wai yangi kaitinisa peamo dopaleaka joo, endakalimi Gotenya isingi mate dokonya, pii doko sepala, tenge doko nanyilyaminopa, Sataneme ipupala, monanya nasina lao, pii doko nyoo nepenge.
Ee wai yangi kana-kisa pao, langa leamo dopaleaka joo, endakali yangimi wai pii epe doko sepala, auu kaeyao yapa nyingima.
Ee wai kana-kisa pingi napiamosa, kumiamo dopaleaka joo, endakali dupame, wai pii epe doko auu pyoo nyepelyaminopa, pii doko nyakama-kisa silyamo dokonya, pundu kendapi longo epelyamopa, wai pii epe doko pupae yakinengema.
Ee wai yangi yuu ikililyambu tenge palenge dupanya peamo dopaleaka joo, endakali yangi dupame wai pii epe doko singima. Singimaka doko, yuunya munipi, pinju longo nyoo setao katapu laka lao, putiti kaengepi, nea kaengepi, mana dupame, wai pii epe doko kui pilyamosa, dii namandengema.
Ee wai yangi lyandeamo dupa, yuu epenya peamo dopaleaka joo, wai pii epe dokonya tenge angi doko soo nyepala, endakali yangimi dii 100 mandenge, yangimi 60 mandenge, yangimi 30 lao dii mandengena” lea.
Jisasame dee kongali pii mende dokaita lamaiyoo, “Gotenya isingi mate doko, akali mendeme baanya eenya wita wai epe lyandeamo dopale.
Kuka gii mendepa, endakali dupa pitaka palipiaminopa, akali dokonya yandapipi mendeme ipupala, wita wai lyandatae kaina dupanya, wita jepae koo tanu mende lyandatala pea.
Maitakao wita dupa langa latala, andao dii manjanya piamopa, koo tanu dupa apata kateamo kandeami.
Dokopa akali ee tange dokonya, kalai akali dupame baa peteasa ipupala, tipa pyoo, 'Akali andake, embame embanya ee dokonya wita wai epe lyandeno doko, koo tanu kalyamo dupa anja-tae kalyape?' leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baame dokaita lamaiyoo, 'Doko akali yandapipi mendeme lyandao piana' lea. Dopa leamopa, kalai akali dupame baa lamaiyoo, 'Naimame dupa yukuo nepala pumili lao masilipi?' leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baame dokaita lamaiyoo, 'Daana, koo tanu dupa yukuatiti, wita dupa apata yukutamina, lapota pyasoo andena kaeyalapa. Wambu pitamo gii dokopa, nambame nee mandyuu mau pingi akali dupa lamaiyoo, “Wambao nyakamame koo tanu dupa, itatenya soo yangapengena, yukuo yaki pyepape. Dopa petala wita dupa elyambu petala, nambanya nee setenge anda dokonya, setalapape” latona' leana,” Jisasame lea.
<range>
Jisasame dee kongali pii mende dokaita lamaiyoo, “Gotenya isingi mate doko, akali mendeme ee wai mastet lenge mende, baanya eenya lyandeamo dopale.
Ee wai dupa pitakanya mastet wai doko, etete yakaneaka doko, lyandataesa langa latala andao, ee wai pokatae waka dupa pitaka ita miningi. Andao yale jilyamopa, wangya dupanya yaka dupame ipao anda pingimana” lea.
Jisasame dee kongali pii mende dokaita lamaiyoo, “Gotenya isingi mate doko, yisa mendalapo enda mendeme nyoo, palao longo-pipa pyasoo endaki minilyamopa, yisa dokome palao doko pitakanya taeyapala, andasingi dopalena” lea.
Jisasame endakali kambu andake doko, pii lamaiyamo dutupa pitakanya, mende mee lamaiya naeyao, kongaliaka lao lamaiya.
Baame kongaliaka lao lamaiyamo dokome, wamba Goteme propeta mende-kisa, “Yuupi kaitipi tee piamo dokonya pituu, indupa tuu lao, yalo petae dupa nambame kongaliaka lao, endakali dupa lamaituna” leamo doko angi jia.
Dokopa, Jisasame endakali kambu andake doko yakinatala, baa andaka kolandateamopa, disaipolo dupa ipupala baa lamaiyoo, “Koo tanupa makande pyoo, kongali laleno dokonya tenge dupa naima langi” leami.
Jisasame yanu pyao, “Ee wai epe lyandeamo doko, Akalinya Ikiningi doko kandao lea.
Ee doko isa yuu dake kandao lea. Ee wai epe lyandeamo dupa, Gotenya isingi matenya katenge endakali dupa kandao lea. Dee koo tanu dupa, Satanenya endakali katenge dupa kandao lea.
Koo tanu lyandeamo yandapipi doko, Satane kandao lea. Wambu piamo gii doko, tanga gii etatamo doko kandao lea. Nee mandyuu mau pingima akali dupa, enjele dupa kandao lea.
Koo tanu dupa yukuo elyambu petala, itatenya soo yangeamino doko, gii etatamo dokopa, endakali koo dupa ele panda koo dokonya, soo yangata doko kandao lea.
Akalinya Ikiningi dokome baanya enjele dupa pena latamopa, dupame pupala koo pina lao mapisingipi, tanga lao koo pingi endakalipi, dupa baanya isingi mate dokonya nakatena lao yukuo nepatami.
Yukuo nepatamino dupa, itate andake dokonya soo pyandataminopa, dokonya katao endakali koo pingi dupa, ee lao nenge gilyoo yamataka latami.
Dokopa endakali tolatae dupa, nyakamanya Takangenya isingi mate dokonya, tii pyoo niki joo tao katatami. Nyakama kalekaita singi dupame, pii doko auu pyoo salapapena,” Jisasame lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Gotenya isingi mate doko, bokosa muni ee mendenya yalo petae kateamo dopale. Yalo petae kateamo doko akali mendeme kandasetala, dee sanga pyambea. Dopa petala baa auu kaeyao andaka pupala, baanya oapi singi dupa pitakame muni nyepala, ee doko pao sambeana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Gotenya isingi mate doko, akali bisnis pingi mendeme, mamaku epe mendapu sambalanya kutao paenge dopale.
Akali dokome mamaku eteteaka epe, muni andake pupenge mende kutao kandatala, andaka pupala, baanya oapi singi dupa pitakame muni nyepala, mamaku epe doko sambao nyingina” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Gotenya isingi mate doko, akali dupame umbene nuu mende, endaki petenya pyandatala, pisa tata longo dupa nyingi dopale.
Pisa umbene nuunya tumbatelyamopa, pisa nyingi akali dupame pyalya lao lembasa nyepala, isa pituu yapengema. Yapapala epe dupa nyoo mandipala, koo dupa nepengema.
Dopaka pyoo, gii etatamo dokopa, enjele dupa ipupala, endakali koo pingipi, mana tolatae miningipi, dupa yapao mokosetami.
Endakali koo dupa, itate andake dokonya watao pyandataminopa, dokonya katao ee lao nenge gilyoo, yamataka latamina” lea.
Jisasame disaipolo dupa tipa pyoo, “Nyakamame pii datupanya tenge dupa nyilyamipi?” lea. Dopa leamopa, dokaitame yanu pyao, “Naimame tenge dupa nyepelyamanona” leami.
Dokopa baame dokaita kandao, “Anda tange mendeme baanya oapi enengepi, wambataepi, epe andaka setenge dupa, kalai pipenge jetamoli pyoo minao kalai pita. Dopaka pyoo, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali mendeme, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya mana nyepala, mana enenge dokopi, wambatae dokopi, lapota baame minao kalai pipenge jetamoli pyoo, pitana” lea.
Jisasame pii kongali dutupa lamaiyoo etapala, yuu doko yakinatala pea.
Baanya yuu tenge dokonya pupala, endakali dupa nyakamanya lotuu anda dokonya mana lamaiyamopa, walu latala, “Akali dakeme masepae epepi, mirakolo kalaipi, dupa pitaka anja-tae nyiape?
Akali dake kapenda dokonya ikiningi daape? Baanya endangi doko Maria daape? Baanya kaiminingi dupa Jemesapi, Josepepi, Saimonepi, Judasapi dutupa daape?
Baanya pimalenge dupa pitaka, ae naima-pipa apata napilyamape? Baame pilyamo datupa pitaka, anja mana nyiape?” leami.
Dopa latala dupame baa kandao, mona koo palyiami. Dopa piaminosa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Propeta mende yuu waka dupanya kalyamo doko, endakali dupame baa andanda semaingima. Dopaka doko, propeta mende baanya yuu tenge dokonya kalyamo doko, baanya palupi, tatapi dupame baanya pii sepala, andanda semaiya naengemana” lea.
Dupame baa tungi napiaminosa, baame mirakolo kalai longo yuu dokonya napia.
Gii dokopa Galilea tange isingi akali, Erote Antipasa lenge dokome, Jisasame pilyamo lapae dupa sia.
Sepala baanya kalai akali dupa lamaiyoo, “Akali doko Jone kaimbu pingi doko. Baa malunya sakatatala, mirakolo kalai dapale dupa pyoo kalyamona” lea.
Wamba Eroteme baanya kaiminingi Pilipa, etanenge Erodiasa lenge doko baa tondao nyia. Dopa piamosa, Jone kaimbu pingi dokome Erote lamaiyoo, “Embame enda tondao nyilino doko, kopeta pilinona” lea. Dopa lati siamosa, Eroteme Jone anjinya pyandea.
<range>
Anjinya pyandatala baame Jone pyao kumasotoo lao masiamoaka doko, Juda dupame Jone baa propetana lao masiaminosa, paka kaeyapala yakinea.
Erotenya mandenge gii doko epeamopa, gii doko kandao nyoo, endakali longo peteami. Dopa piaminopa, kaina dokonya Erodiasa wanenge doko ipao, danisa lea. Danisa leamo doko kandatala, Eroteme etete auu kaeyapala, wanaku doko lamaiyoo, “Nambame kiningi etete lelyo. Embame dopale mende dii lateno doko, lateliaka pyoo dyaapona” lea.
<range>
Dokopa wanaku doko endangi peteasa pupala, aipa laowape lea. Dopa leamopa, endangi dokome, “Jone kaimbu pingi dokonya aiyombo doko, pelesanya setapala dina lamaiya puu” lea. Dokopa wanaku doko Erote peteasa pupala, endangimi leamo dutupa lamaiya.
Pii dutupa sepala, Erote mona kenda kaeyamoaka doko, wamba baame endakali enombanya, kiningi etete mende ditoana leamo doko masetala,
baame yanda singi mendeme anjetae andaka pupala, Jonenya aiyomba doko kepao nyala pena lea.
Pena lateamopa, Jonenya aiyomba doko kepanyetala, pelesa mendenya setapala, wanaku doko minao ipao maiya. Maitiamopa, wanaku dokome nyepala endangi pao maiya.
Maitiamopa, Jonenya disaipolo dupa ipupala, baanya yonge doko nyoo, malu piami. Malu petala, Jisasa pao lamaiyami.
Jisasame Jone malu pimi lapae doko sepala, baame yuu doko yakinatala, sipi mendenya pituu, Galilea pete omotena endakali napalenge yuu mendakaita, mendeme nakandena lao baa pea. Baa pelyamo lapae endakali dupame sepala, nyakamanya taono dupanya katao, baa watao kaitini peami.
Jisasa Galilea pete omotena pao pyakamatala, endakali kambu andake mende kateamino kandea. Kandatala baame endakali dokaita kondo kaeyapala, yaina pyapae dupa mee jakamaiya.
Niki landa piamopa, disaipolo dupa ipupala Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Endakali napalenge panda dakenya, yuu kuiyalanya pilyamona, embame endakali kambu dake maketa seta dupanya, tange nee sambao nala pena laa” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Daa, dokaita napena, nyakamame nee maiyepa” lea.
Dopa leamopa, dupame baa lamaiyoo, “Naimanya nee longo nasilyamo. 5-pela betesa-pipa, pisa lapo-pipa iki silyamona” leami.
Dokopa baame lao pituu, “Dutupa nyoo minao ae ipupa” lea.
Dopa latala baame endakali dupa tanu dupanya petena lea. Petena latala, 5-pela betesa-pipa, pisa lapoma-pipa nyepala, kaiti-kisa kandalyetae katao, yaka pilino lea. Dopa latala betesa dutupa konjepala, baanya disaipolo dupa maiyamopa, dupame endakali dupa mokosoo maiyami.
Endakali dupa pitakame nao tiaka kaeyateaminopa, kakana siamo dupa disaipolo dupame nyoo, 12 baseketa tumbasiami.
Enda wanepi itaki napyao, akali iki 5 tausenepi mendeme, nee neami.
Dokopa Jisasame baanya disaipolo dupa, sipinya pyakalyetala, Galilea pete omotena wambao pena lea. Baame endakali kambu dupa, andaka pena latala kandao katea.
Dokaita pateaminopa, baa iki loma sala, yuu manda mendenya pea. Yuu kuiyala peamopa, baa iki dokonya katea.
Dokopa disaipolo dupa sipi dokonya pituu, endaki pete kainanya peaminopa, poo andake mende paanya peamino dokaita-kaita pituu, laeyao lao ipupala, endaki doko buli piamo dokome, sipi doko nyoo yangi pyasa-pyasa pia.
Yuu yongao pukiamopa, Jisasa baa endaki pete dokonya moko katao, disaipolo dupa sipinya peamino dokonya pea.
Disaipolo dupame baa endaki pete dokonya moko katao epeamo kandatala, “Timango mende epelyamona” latala, paka kaeyao ae leami.
Dopa piaminopa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Namba epelyona, nyakama paka nakaeyalapa” lea.
Dokopa Pitame baa lamaiyoo, “Kamongo, kini emba-tamo doko, embame namba endakinya moko katao ipu laa” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame, “Emba ipu” lea. Dokopa Pitame sipi doko yakinatala, endakinya moko katao, Jisasa kateamo dokonya pea.
Pao pituu kandeamopa, poo andake mende leamosa, baa paka kaeya. Dokopa baa endakimi nyoo landa piamopa, baame ae lao, “Kamongo, namba nisa!” lea.
