Dopa leamopa, Jisasame yapa kingi pyale latala, Pita kii nyokonyetala, “Aipuma emba mona lapo palipala, namba kuki tungi pyalepe?” lea.
Dokopa nyakamba sipinya pyakalyiambinopa, poo doko yatu lea.
Yatu leamo doko kandatala, disaipolo sipinya peteamino dupame, “Kiningi etete, emba Gote Ikiningi-lamona” lao mambo piami.
Jisasa disaipolo dupa-pipa, Galilea pete dokonya yangi-kaita, Genesarete yuu dokonya pao pyakameami.
Yuu dokaita tange endakali dupame, Jisasa-lamo lao kandatala, yuu dosa singi dupa pitakanya wai leaminopa, yaina pyapae dupa pitaka soo epeami.
Endakali soo epeamino dupame, baanya yonge pee punanya, yaina pyapae dupame watandena lao, Jisasa tee leami. Watandeamino endakali dupa pitakanya, yaina dupa mee jeta pia.
Gii dokopa Parasaipi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, mendapuame Jerusalema katao, Jisasa kateasa ipupala tipa pyoo,
“Embanya disaipolo dupame mana wambatae naimanya, yumbangeme seteamino dupa, aipuma yalengemape? Dupame nee nalanya dokopa, kingi wasa pingili pyoo napingima-lamo” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dupanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Nyakamame aipuma yumbangenya mana wambatae dupa, watao minama latala, Gotenya mana kyeto setapae dupa yalengemape?
Wamba Goteme lao pituu, 'Embanya endangi takangepi dolapo, andanda semaiyoo katape” lea. Dee Goteme, “Endakali mendeme baanya endangi takangepi mende kandao, pii koo latamo doko, baa pyao kumasepengena' lea.
Dopa leamoka doko, nyakamame mana waka mende miningima-lamo. Akali mendeme endangi takangepi lamaiyoo pituu, 'Nambame nyakamba oapi dipenge dupa pitaka, Gote maitalona' latamo kandao doko, nyakamame kapana lao mana lengema-lamo. Lelyamino dokome, endangi takangepi nisepengena lao, Gotenya loo seteamo doko mee joo nepengema.
<range>
Nyakama Gote watao miningi mane-mane pingima dupa, propeta Aisaiyame dapa lao makande pyokondape pia:
'Endakali tata dakeme, kambumi namba mambo pyapala, nyakamanya moname namba angi mambo napingima.
Dupame endakalinya mana setapae dupa mana lao pituu, “Dake Gotenya mana setapaena” lengema. Nyakamame kambumi namba mambo pilyaminopa, nambame nasingina' lapae silyamo.”
Dokopa Jisasame endakali kambu doko epena latala lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame pii dake sepala, masokondape pyepape:
Endakali mendeme nee mende nelyamo dokome, baa koeyasala naenge. Endakali mendenya nengekaita pii koo epelyamo dokome, baa koeyasingina” lea.
Gii dokopa disaipolo dupame ipupala baa lamaiyoo, “Parasai dupame embanya pii doko sepala, imbu kaelyamino doko embame kandelepe?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Nambanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokome, ee waingi pokala naeyamo dupa pitaka, pingitaka yukuta.
Dopa pitana, nyakamame Parasai dupa katena kaeyapala, watala naeyalapape. Parasai lenge monda dupame, endakali yango dupa kii miningima. Akali lenge monda mendeme, lenge monda yango mende kii minilyamo doko, lapota yulinya pyakengembana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Pitame baa lamaiyoo, “Nee nenge dokome, endakali mende koeyasala naengena lao, embame kongali laleno dokonya, tenge doko naima langi” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame lao pituu, “Nyakamame apata nongo pyapala, pii tenge doko nanyilyamipi?
Kamanda singi mende nengekaita pelyamo doko, inginya soo kamanda epenge, doko nyakamame masala naelyamipi?
Endakalinya monanya palenge mende, nengekaitanya epenge dokome, endakali dupa koeyasingi.
Monanya paliu pyakalyingi dupa, masingi koopi, endakali pyao kumasingipi, kepo kolengepi, enda akalipi nyele-nyele paengepi, pake nengepi, sambo pii lengepi, lamba lengepi,
dopale dupame endakali koeyasingi. Dopaka doko, endakali mendeme kingi wasa napinya, mee nee nyoo nelyamo dokome, baa koeyasala naengena” Jisasame lea.
Jisasame yuu doko yakinatala, taono Taeyapa, Saidonepanya yuu siamo dupanya pea.
Peamopa, enda Kenane tange mendeme ipupala, puu lao, “Akali Andake, emba Dapiti Yumbange. Imambu koo mendeme nambanya wanenge doko, etete koeyasilyamona embame namba kondo kaeyao nisepoko” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame pii mende yanu pyao, baa lamaiya naeya. Dokopa baanya disaipolo dupame ipupala, kongo lao baa lamaiyoo, “Enda dakeme wii latae katao, naima watao epelyamona, embame baa pena laa” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dupanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Goteme namba Israele tange, sipisipi alu petae joo kalyamino, dupanya iki puu leana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, enda dokome ipao baa kateamo dosa luma lakapala, “Akali Andake, embame namba nisepoko” lao tee lea.
Dokopa Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Wanenya nee dupa nyepala, pyale lao yana dupa maitamopa, auu napitana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, enda dokome baa lamaiyoo, “Akali andake, wane dupame nee nelyaminopa, kuku-kakanapi isa pelyamo dupa, yana toko pundi-pundi kalyamino dupame nyoo nengemakana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Enda, embame namba kini tungi pyatala, nambame pyakalapenona lao masilinoli, pyekelyona” lea. Dopa leamo gii dokopaka, wanaku doko-kisa imambu koo paleamo doko, yakinatala pea.
Jisasame yuu doko yakinatala, Galilea pete tengesa dosale, manda mendenya lalyoo pupala petea.
Peteamopa, endakali kambu longo dupame, endakali moko koopi, lenge mondapi, papa tambutaepi, muumaapi, waka yainame pyapaepi, longo dupa laminao baa peteamo dosa epeaminopa, yaina dupa pitaka mee jakamaiya.
Yaina mee jakamaiyamo dupa kandatala, endakali kambu dupame walu leami. Muumaa dupame pii lao, papa tambutae dupa tolao, moko koo dupa kaita paeyao, lenge monda dupa lenge tao piaminosa, Israelemanya Gote doko lao mambo piami.
Dokopa Jisasame baanya disaipolo dupa epena latala lamaiyoo, “Endakali dakaita yuu gii tepoma, namba-pipa katapuma. Indupa nee etalame-lamo dokonya, nambame dakaita kondo kaelyo. Nee nanao andaka pena latopa, kaitinisa laowambe lapae setamina” lea.
Dokopa disaipolo dupame baa lamaiyoo, “Endakali napalenge yuu dakenya, naimame betesa anja-tae nyepala, endakali kambu andake dake nena maimape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, “Nyakamanya betesa akipate silyape?” Jisasame lea. “7-pela betesa-pipa, pisa yakane kuki mendalapo-pipa, silyamona” leami.
Dokopa Jisasame endakali dupa isa petena lea.
Dopa latala, 7-pela betesapi, pisapi, dutupa nyepala, Gote lao yaka pilino latala konjia. Konjepala, baanya disaipolo dupa maiyamopa, dupame endakali dupa mokosoo maiyami.
Maiyaminopa, pitakame nao tiaka kaeyami. Kakana siamo dupa disaipolo dupame, 7-pela baseketa tumbasiami.
Enda wanepi itaki napyao, akali tausene kitomendeme neami.
Napeaminopa, Jisasame endakali dupa pena latala, baa sipi mendenya pyakalyetala, yuu Magadana pea.
Dokopa Parasaipi, Sadyusiapi, mendapuame ipupala Jisasa minao makande pyoo, “Embame kalai pilino doko, Gote-kisa katao pilini-lamo lao kandamanana, mirakolo mende pii” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baame dokaitanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Niki landa pilyamopa, kaiti kate pilyamo kandatala, nyakamame taita paina pita-lamo lengema.
Yuu yongao pituu, kaiti kate pilyamo kandatala, aiyuu ipata-lamo lengema. Nyakamame kaiti doko kandatala, taita dopa pita-lamo lao lengemaka doko, indupa gii dakepa mana makandepi, aloo pipae epelyamo dupa, nyakamame yapao nakandelyamipi?
Endakali indupa palelyamino dupame, Gote yakinatala, koo pyaanya auu kaelyamino. Nyakamame mirakolo mende kandamana lelyaminoaka doko, mirakolo mende napyakatoo. Goteme Jonaa-kisa mirakolo piamo, dokoaka makande petae setana” lea. Dopa latala baame dupa yakinatala pea.
Disaipolo dupame endaki pete dokonya yangitena pyakamatala, betesa nanyoo ipamane-lamo lao, kandeami.
Dokopa Jisasame dokaita kongalimi lamaiyoo, “Parasaipi, Sadyusiapi dupanya yisa dupame, nyakama koeyasetamina kandao kalyepape” lea.
Dopa leamopa, nyakamalapo laloo pyoo, “Naimame betesa nanyoo ipamano dokonya lelyamona” leami.
Dopa leamino doko Jisasame kandatala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakama Gote tungi napingi dupame, aipuma betesa nasilyamo lao nyakamalapo lelyamipi?
Nyakamame namba apipi lao masala naelyamiakape? Nambame 5-pela betesa, akali 5 tausene dupanya konjakamaiyo, doko nao kakana siamo dupa, baseketa longo tumbasiamino doko, kame silyamipi?
Dee nambame 7-pela betesa, akali 4 tausene dupanya konjakamaiyo doko, nao kakana siamo baseketa longo tumbasiamino, doko kame silyamipi?
Nambame betesanya iki lao nalalo doko, nasalamipi? Parasaipi, Sadyusiapi, dupanya yisa dupame koeyasetamina kandao kalyepape” lea.
Dopa lateamopa, yisa doko palaonya taelyamopa, betesa doko andengeli pyoo, Parasaipi, Sadyusiapinya mana koeyapae dupa taenge. Taelyamo dokome, endakali longo dupa-kisa andinyilyamopa, koengemana lao yisa-pipa, Jisasame makande pyoo lalame-lamo lao, disaipolo dupame masiami.
Jisasa baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa, taono Sisaria Pilipae pupala, baanya disaipolo dupa tipa pyoo, “Endakali dupame Akalinya Ikiningi doko kandao, apina lelyamipi?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, dupame yanu pyao, “Yangimi emba kandao Jone kaimbu pingi dokona lelyamino. Yangimi emba propeta Ilaijana lelyamino. Yangimi emba propeta Jeremaeyana lelyamino. Yangimi propeta waka wamba kateamino dupanya mendena, lelyaminona” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita tipa pyoo, “Endakali dupame dopa lalumino doko, nyakamame namba kandao apina lelyamipi?” lea.
Dokopa Saimone Pitame Jisasa kandao, “Emba Kraisa, Gote saka katenge dokonya Ikiningi dokona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Saimone, Jonaa ikiningi, embame pii leleno doko, endakali mendeme langya naelyamo. Nambanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokome, emba auu pisetala langipumupa leleno.
Nambame emba kandao dapa langilyo: Pita, emba kana kyeto dokona, nambanya siosa doko kana kyeto dake-kisa pitupa, Satanenya pupu lapae dokome, siosa doko ita minala naeyata.
Nambame Gotenya isingi mate dokonya, kii dupa emba ditu. Embame isa yuu dakenya, endakali mendenya kaita lyokateno doko, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya lyokataeyaka katata. Embame isa yuu dakenya endakali mendenya, kaita lumbateno doko, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya lumbapaeyaka setana” lea.
Dopa latala baame disaipolo dupa kyeto joo lamaiyoo, “Namba Kraisa dokona lao, mendaipi mende lamaiya naeyalapape” lea.
Gii dokopa pituu, Jisasame baanya disaipolo dupa panao dapa lamaiya: “Namba Jerusalema pupenge. Patopa, Judamanya isingi akalipi, pitisa mupapi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, dupame namba tanda longo ditala, pyao kumasetataminopa, yuu gii tepo dokonya Goteme namba dee sakatasetana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Pitame Jisasa laminao umbisale pupala pyalanya lao, “Kamongo, embame leleno doko, dopa napinana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame kandapilyetala Pita lamaiyoo, “Satane emba puu! Embame Gotenya masingili pyoo nalenya, endakalinya masingili pyoo leeno dokome, nambanya kaita lyokekelenona” lea.
Dokopa Jisasame baanya disaipolo dupa lamaiyoo, “Endakali mendeme namba watao ipatoo lao masetamo doko, baa tange kame sepala, baanya poko ita doko nyoo soo, namba watao ipupenge.
Endakali mendeme namba watatosa, tanda natona lao masetala, wanditamo doko baa alu pita. Dopaka doko, endakali mendeme namba lao masetala, baa tange kame setamo doko, baame lete etete katenge doko nyeta.
Endakali mendeme namba yakinatala, yuunya oapi dupa pitaka nyoo setao katapala, baa alu pitamo doko, oapi dupame tanga baa aipa petala nisetape? Aki mende Gote maitala, baanya lete etete katenge doko tange sambao nyetape?
Akalinya Ikiningi doko baanya enjele dupa-pipa, baanya Takangenya tii pipae dokonya ipata. Ipupala endakali mendai-mendai lao, mana minataminoli pyoo, yole maita.
Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Endakali ae kalyamino datupanya mendapu, kumala naeyataminopa, Akalinya Ikiningi doko, baanya isingi mate dokonya pupu lapae doko-pipa, ipatamopa kandatamina” Jisasame lea.
Yuu gii 6-pela pateamopa, Jisasame Pita, Jemesa, Jemesa kaiminingi Jonepi, dutupa laminao yuu manda ketae mendenya pupala, nyakama iki kateami.
Kateaminopa dutupanya enombanya Jisasa waka jia. Baanya lengelyapi doko tii pyoo, niki tele pia. Dee baanya yonge pee dupa, kyoo lao pole-pole pia.
Dokopa Mosesa, Ilaija, Jisasa-pipa pii lao kalyu piaminopa kandeami.
Kandatala Pitame Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Kamongo, naima dakenya katapumanopa auu pyuumuna, embame kapana lao maseteno doko, nambame dakenya sele anda tepoma pitoo. Mende embanya, mende Mosesanya, mende Ilaijanyana” lea.
Pitame dopa lao kateamopa, kopa tii pipae mendeme ipupala, dokaita sanga pia. Dopa piamopa, kopa tambe-tambe dokonya pii mende lea dokome, “Doo kalyamo doko nambanya Ikiningi, mona setenge doko. Nambame baa etete auu kaengena, nyakamame baanya pii doko sakamaiyepape” lea.
Dokopa disaipolo dutupame pii doko sepala, etete paka kaeyapala, tombauli siami.
Dopa piaminopa, Jisasame ipao dutupa watandatala, “Nyakama paka nakaenya sakatalapa” lea.
Dopa leamopa, dutupame kandeaminopa, Jisasa baa iki katea.
Dokaitame yuu manda dokonya katao lanao pituu, Jisasame kyeto joo, “Nyakamame kanjimino doko mende lamaiya naeyalapape. Tanga Akalinya Ikiningi doko, kumapala sakatatamopa, endakali dupa lamaitamina” lea.
Dokopa disaipolo dupame Jisasa tipa pyoo, “Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali dupame, aipuma 'Ilaija wambao ipatatamopa, Kraisa ipupengena' lengemape?” leami.
Jisasame dutupanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Kini, dupa pitaka depa lasalanya, Ilaija wambao ipupenge.
Dopaka doko, Ilaija ipateana lao nambame nyakama langilyo. Ilaija baaka epeamopa, endakali dupame kandao nanyepala, masiamili pyoo baa minao koeyasiami. Dopaka pyoo, Akalinya Ikiningi doko tanda maitamina” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jone kaimbu pingi doko kandao, lelyamona lao disaipolo dupame masiami.
Endakali kambu pyao kateamino dokonya, Jisasapi baanya disaipolo tepo dutupa-pipa ipateaminopa, akali mendeme Jisasa kateasa ipao, baa lao luma lakapala
lamaiyoo, “Akali Andake, nambanya wane dake mandipaeme, itatenya nyoo yangao, endakinya nyoo pyandao pilyamopa, baa tanda longo nao katengena, embame baa kondo kaeyao nisakapoko.
Nambame baa laminao, embanya disaipolo dupa katamisa ipupupa, dupame baanya yaina doko kapa pao, mee jisala naeyalaminona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame lao pituu, “Indupa endakali palelyamino dupame, koteaka lao pii tanga lao, Gote tungi napilyamino doko, namba oo koto doko, nyakama-pipaka tole katatope? Nyakama nongo pilyamino doko, andukupa tolataminopa lao nambame malisoo kataowape? Wane doko laminao asa ipupa” lea.
Lanyoo ipateaminopa, Jisasame imambu koo doko pyalanya latala, wane doko yakinatala pena leamopa pea. Puu piamopa, wane dokonya yaina doko mee jia.
Maitakao Jisasa iki peteamopa, disaipolo dupame ipupala baa tipa pyoo, “Aipuma naimame imambu koo doko, kapa pao watao napyalamape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame Gote kuki tungi pilyamino dokonya, imambu koo doko kapa pao watao pyala naeyalamino. Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Nyakamanya Gote tungi pingi doko, yakane mastet dii dopale-pili, dokome yuu manda dake lamaiyoo, 'Emba sakatatala, omosale puu' lapinopa, pupyaliakana” lea.
<range>
Jisasa baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa, Galilea yuu dokonya kambu pyatala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Akali mendeme Akalinya Ikiningi doko, enge nyepala, endakali waka dupa laitaka pyaanya pilyamo.
Laitaka petatamopa, dupame baa pyao kumasetami. Kumasetataminopa, yuu gii tepo dokonya, Goteme baa dee sakatasetana” lea. Dopa leamo sepala, disaipolo dupa mona etete kenda kaeyami.
Jisasa baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa, taono Kapename dokonya pyakameaminopa, lotuu anda andakenya takisa nyingi akali dupame, ipupala Pita tipa pyoo, “Nyakamanya mana lenge akali dokome, lotuu anda andakenya takisa doko maingipi?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Pitame yanu pyao, “Kini maingina” lea. Dopa latala baa andaka pao kolandatala, pii mende latala naeyamopa, Jisasame tipa pyoo, “Saimone, embame aipa lao masili? Yuu dakenya kiŋi dupame nyakamanya ikiningi dupa-kisa takisa nyingimape, pande endakali yuu tenge tange dupa-kisa takisa nyingimape?” lea.
Pitame yanu pyao, “Endakali yuu tenge tange dupa-kisa nyingimana” lea. Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Dopa-tamo doko, kiŋi ikiningi dupame takisa namaipenge.
Dopaka doko, naimame akali dokaita kenda pisala naeyamana, embame endaki pete dokonya pupala, uku mende pyandatala, pisa wambao nyeteno dokonya nengekaita angapu lakyepala, dokonya konde mende palyapomona nyepe. Nyepala pao lotuu anda andake dokonya, nalimbanya takisa maipi” lea.
Gii dokopa disaipolo dupame Jisasa tipa pyoo, “Gotenya isingi mate dokonya api alyasale joo katatape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame wane koo mende epena latala, dokaitanya kainanya katasetala
lamaiyoo, “Nyakamanya mana doko aloo petala, anasale jetala wane koo joo nakatatamino doko, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya, napatamina lao nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo.
Endakali mendeme baa tange anasale jetala, wane koo dapale jetamo doko, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya alyasale joo katata.
Endakali mendeme namba lao masetala, wane koo dapale mende lanyilyamo dokome, namba lanyingiakana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Namba tungi pingi wane koo mende, endakali mendeme koo pina lao mapisetamo doko, kana andake mende baanya mangenya kende katatala, soo solowatanya pyandamili doko, auu pipyali.
Isa yuu dakenya, koo pina lao mapisingi dupa singi-lamo. Dopana endakali dupa pitaka-kisa makande pingi ipatana, kandao kalyepape. Kini makande pingi dupa ipatamoaka doko, endakali mendeme koo pina lao mapisetamo doko, baa koeyata-lamo!
Embanya kingi mokopi mendeme, emba koo pyaale lao mapisetamo doko, kepanya nepape. Emba kingi mokopi mendai iki kateta, lete etete katenge dokonya pupili doko, auu pipyali. Kingi mokopi lapota kateta itate konjala naenge dokonya, soo pyandamili doko, auu napipyali.
Embanya lenge mendeme koo pyaale lao mapisetamo doko, lukunya nepape. Emba lenge mendai iki tao, lete etete katenge dokonya pupili doko, auu pipyali. Emba lenge lapota tapeta, ele panda koo ita tao katenge dokonya, soo pyandamili doko, auu napipyali” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Wane koo dupanya isingi enjele dupa, nambanya Takange kaitinya katenge doko-pipa, apata katengema. Dopana, nyakamame dupa kandanya palyala naeyalapape.
<range>
Nyakamame aipa lao masilyami? Akali mendenya 100 sipisipi katatamo dokonya, mendai alu pitamopa, baame aipa pitape? Baame 99 sipisipi dutupa, pau manda mendenya katena latala, mendai alu pitamo doko kutala naeyatape?
Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Sipisipi 99 katatamino dutupa, auu kaeyatamoaka doko, baame mendai alu pitamo doko kutao nyepala, etete auu kaeyata.
Dopaka pyoo, nyakamanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokome, wane koo dupanya mende alu napipya laka lao, masingina” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Embanya kaiminingi mendeme emba koo pingitamo doko, baa katatasa emba pupala, nyakamba iki pitipala, baanya koo pitamo doko, lao panasoo lamaipi. Lamaitinopa, baame embanya pii setamo doko, embanya kaiminingi doko dee pilyoo nyete.
Baame embanya pii nasetamo doko, pii pepa pyapae singili pyoo, mendai lapopi mende lanyepala, nyakambanya pii latambino dupa sina, laminao deaka lamaiya pupape.
Baame dutupanya pii nasetamo doko, embame siosanya endakali kambu pyatae dupa lamaipi. Dee baame siosanya apata pii nasetamo doko, baa kamalya katenge endakalipi, takisa nyingi akalipi, dopale-lamo lao kandatala, wandyuu kalyepape.
“Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Nyakamame isa yuu dakenya endakali mendenya, kaita lyokatamino doko, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya lyokataeyaka katata. Nyakamame isa yuu dakenya, endakali mendenya kaita lumbatamino doko, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya lumbataeyaka seta.
Nambanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokome, mende pyekena lao, nyakamanya mendalapome mona mendai palyetala, tee latambinopa, baame latambiliaka pyakata.
Endakali lapo tepopi mendatupame, namba lao masetala, mendasa kambu pyao pitatamino dokonya, namba kainanya apata katatona lao, nambame nyakama langilyona” lea.
Dokopa Pitame Jisasa tipa pyoo, “Kamongo, nambanya kaiminingi mendeme koo petae katao pingitamopa, nambame baanya koo dupa, paa 7-pela kame sakamaipengepe, pande akipatesape?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame yanu pyao, “Paa 7-pela iki daa. Paa 77 pyoo, koo pitamo dupa kame sakamaipengena lao lelyo.
Dopana, Gotenya isingi mate doko kiŋi mendeme, baanya kalai akali dupa-kisa, yanu maiyamo dupa tolasekena, latoo lao masiamo dopale.
Kiŋi dokome tee pyao yanu dupa, pyekena lao kateamopa, kalai akali yanu singi dupanya mende, laminao epeamino doko-kisa, 10 milion kina yanu sakamaiya.
Akali dokome yanu andake doko, kapa pao pyapenge nanjiamosa, kiŋi dokome baanya kalai akali dupa lamaiyoo, 'Nyakamame akali dakepi, baanya enda wanepi, dee oapi dupa pitakame muni nyepala, yanu doko pyekena lamaiyepape' lea.
Dopa leamopa, kalai akali dokome kiŋi dokonya enombanya, pao luma lakapala tee lao, 'Nambame embanya yanu dupa pitaka pyakatona, embame namba kondo kaeyapala, gii dipoko' lea.
Dopa leamopa, kiŋi dokome baa kondo kaeyapala, baanya yanu dupa kaeyapala yakinea.
Dopa peteamopa, kalai akali dokome pupala, baanya kalai akali yango mende-kisa, 100 kina baanya yanu sakamaingi doko kandanyia. Kandanyetala kalai akali yango dokonya, mangenya puu lao minatala, 'Nambanya yanu dutupa yapa pyaka' lea.
Dopa leamopa, kalai akali yango dokome tombauli sepala tee lao, 'Nambame embanya yanu dupa pitaka pyakatona, embame namba kondo kaeyapala, gii dipoko' lea.
Dopa leamoaka doko, baame daa latala, kalai akali yango dokome, yanu dutupa etao pyatakala ipatana, anjoo pyandatala pena lea.
Dokopa baanya kalai akali yango dupame, piamo doko kandatala, kondo kaeyao maka kaeyapala, kiŋi doko pao lamaiyami.
Lamaiyaminopa, kiŋi dokome kalai akali doko epena latala lamaiyoo, 'Emba kalai akali koo-lamo! Nambame emba kondo kaeyao, nisepoko lao tee lapino dokonya, nambanya yanu emba-kisa sipumu dutupa pitaka kaeyapu.
Nambame emba kondo kaeyapu dopaka pyoo, embanya kalai akali yango doko kondo kaeyateno!” lao pyalanya lea.
Dopa latala, kiŋi dokome imbu kaeyapala, kalai akali doko anjoo, tanda maina lao, anjingi andaka isingi akali dupanya kingilyaka maiyoo pituu, 'Akali dakeme nambanya yanu dutupa, etao pyatakala ipatana, anjoo soo pupa' lea-pyaa.
Dopana, nyakamanya kaiminingi mendeme koo pingitamo dupa, kiningi etete monanya katao kame nasetamino doko, nambanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokome, nyakamanya koo pitamino dupa, kame nasakatakana” lea.
Jisasame pii lao etapala, Galilea yuu doko yakinatala, Judia yuu dokonya endaki Jodane yangitena pea.
Dokopa endakali kambu longome Jisasa watao epeaminopa, baame dokaitanya yaina dupa mee jakamaiya.
Dopa piamopa, Parasai mendapuame ipupala, baa minao makande pyoo, “Akali mendeme baanya enda doko-kisa, tenge mee mende-tamopi, angi mende-tamopi, setapala yakinatamo doko, loome daa latae singi doko yalatape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baame yanu pyao, “Nyakamame pii dake itaki napiamipi? 'Tee piamo dokopa, Goteme enda akalipa lao wasia.
Tenge dokonya, akalimi baanya endangi takangepa yakinatala, baanya etanengepa tole pyao, yonge mendai joo pititambina' lao pyapae silyamo.
Tenge dokonya, dolapo lapoma joo napetenya, yonge mendai joo pititambi. Goteme nyoo pyasetae doko, endakalimi wakale pyoloo napipengena” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Parasai dupame baa tipa pyoo, “Dopa-tamo doko, Mosesame loo seteamo dokonya, 'Akali mendeme baanya enda doko yakinao pituu, enda yakinapenge pepa mende maitala pena lapengena' lao, aipuma seteape?” leami.
Dokopa Jisasame pii yanu pyao, “Nyakamanya yumbange dupa tuu-tuu piaminosa, Mosesame loo doko pepa pyanya setea-pyaa. Dopaka doko, wamba tee piamo dokopa, Goteme loo doko setala naeya.
Dopana, nambame nyakama dapa langilyo: Akali mendenya etanenge dokome, kepo kolala naeyatamopa, baame mee yakinatala, enda waka mende nyetamo doko, akali dokome kepo kolatana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, baanya disaipolo dupame baa lamaiyoo, “Enda akalipa tole pyao petenge mana doko, dopale-tamo doko, akalimi enda lanyala naeyao katataminopa, auu pitana” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Akali pitakame kapa pao, enda lanyala naeyao mee nakatatami. Goteme kyeto maitamo mendapuame, iki kapa pao enda nanyoo mee katatami.
Akali mendapu enda nanyepenge jepae mandeami dupame, enda nanyoo mee katengema. Akali mendapu lakapo nyepae, enda lanyala naengema. Dee mendapuame Gotenya isingi mate dokonya kalai doko pitoo lao masetala, enda lanyala naengemaka. Tenge dokonya minao, akali mendeme enda lanyala naeyao katatoo lao masetamo doko, yakana” Jisasame lea.
Dokopa endakali mendapuame Jisasa kateamo dokonya, wane wanakupi dupa Jisasame kingi, aiyombanya setapala, loma sakamaina lao laminao epeaminopa, disaipolo dupame endangi takangepi dupa pyalanya leami.
Pyalanya leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Gotenya isingi mate doko, wane wanakupi koo dapale dupanyana, epekena kaita lyokala naeyalapa” lea.
Dopa latala baame dokaita-kisa kingi setao loma sepala, baa yuu doko yakinatala pea.
Gii mendepa akali mende Jisasa kateasa ipupala, “Mana Lenge Akali, mana epe aipale mende minatala, tanga namba lete etete katenge doko nyotope?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Aipuma embame mana epe dupanya lao namba tipa pilipi? Gote iki baa epe kalyamo. Emba lete etete katenge doko nyotoo lao maseteno doko, Gotenya loo dupa watao minape” lea.
Dopa lateamopa, akali dokome baa tipa pyoo, “Loo dupa andutupape?” lea. Dokopa Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Embame endakali pyao kumasala naeyape. Kepo kolala naeyape. Pake nala naeyape. Endakali mende sambo lao minakasala naeyape.
Embame embanya endangi takangepa dolapo, andanda semaiyoo katape. Dee embame emba tange auu kaengeli pyoo, endakali yango dupa auu kaeyao katapena” lea.
Dokopa akali patange dokome pii yanu pyao, “Loo dutupa pitaka nambame watao miningina, dee nambame aki mende apata pipengepe?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Embame Gotenya mana tolatae dupanya katapu laka lao maseteno doko, emba pupala, embanya oapi dupa pitakame muni nyepala, endakali daa jepae dupa maitala, namba watao ipupi. Dopa pitinopa, tanga embanya epe dupa kaitinya sakatana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, akali patange dokome sepala, baanya oapi etete longo singi dokonyana, mona kenda kaeyapala, baa yakinatala pea.
Dokopa Jisasame disaipolo dupa lamaiyoo, “Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Yuunya kamongo dupa Gotenya isingi mate dokonya paanya, leke-leke tatamina” lea.
Dee mende nyakama langilyo: Kamele mendeme kepo tii mendenya leke-leke tao kolandapyaliaka doko, yuunya kamongo mendeme, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya paanya, eteteaka leke-leke tapyalina” lea.
Dokopa disaipolo dupame pii dutupa soo etete walu latala, “Dopa-tamo doko, endakali apimi Gotenya isingi mate dokonya patape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita lengeme kandatae katao lamaiyoo, “Endakalimi nyakamanya pupu lapae dokome, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya napupenge. Endakalimi kapa pao napipenge dupa pitaka, Goteme kapa pao pingina” lea.
Dokopa Pitame baa lamaiyoo, “Naimanya tatapi, pinjupi, dupa pitaka yakinatala, emba watao epelyamano dokonya, tanga naimame aki mende nyetamape?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Tenda Goteme yuu kaitipi enenge jetamo gii dokopa, Akalinya Ikiningi doko, baanya kiŋi petenge toko dokonya, tii pipae-pipa pitita. Gii dokopa nyakama, nambanya disaipolo dupa kiŋi petenge toko, 12-pela dutupanya pititami. Dokonya pituu, Israele tata 12-pela dutupanya pii lao tolasakamaiyoo pititami.
Endakali mendeme namba lao masetala, ee andapi, takange endangipi, kaiminingi pimalengepi, wane wanakupi dupanya mende yakinatamo dokome, dee wakao 100 lao nyeta. Dee lete etete katenge doko apata nyetaka.
Salapape! Epapu endakali longo mendapu, wambao kalyamino dupa tanga maita pyatami. Maitapyao kalyamino dupa, tanga wambatamina” Jisasame lea.
Jisasame kongali pii mende lao pituu, “Gotenya isingi mate doko, akali mendeme yongama wamba sakatatala, baanya waene ee dokonya kalai pyekena lao, kalai akali mendapu lanyala peamo dopale.
Pupala ee tange dokome, akali mendatupa yuu gii mendainya, 1 kiname yole pingili pyoo pitoana, waene eenya kalai pyakala pena lea.
Pena latala 9 kilokopi mendenya, maketanya pupala kandeamopa, akali mendatupa mee kateami.
Kateamino kandatala baame dupa lamaiyoo, 'Nambame nyakama yole pipengeli pyoo pitoana, nyakama apata nambanya waene ee dokonya kalai pyakala pupa' lea.
Dopa lateamopa, akali dupa kalai pyakamaiya peami. Dutupa pateaminopa, 12 kilokopi, 3 kilokopinya baame deaka maketanya pupala, kalai akali mendatupa lanyepala, waene eenya kalai pyakala pena lea.
Deaka 5 kilokopi mendenya pupala, baame akali mendatupa mee kateamino kandatala dupa lamaiyoo, 'Aipuma nyakama indupa gii dake, pitaka mee dakenya katalamipi?' lea.
Dopa leamopa, dupame yanu pyao, 'Akali mendeme naima kalai nandipyasa, naima mee katalamanona' leami. Dokopa baame dokaita lamaiyoo, 'Nyakama apata nambanya waene ee dokonya, kalai pyakala pupa' lea.
Yuu kuiyalanya piamopa, akali ee tange dokome, ee isingi akali doko lamaiyoo, 'Embame kalai akali dupa epena latala, yole pipi. Yole pyoo pituu, kalai akali 5 kilokonya ipamino dupa, wambao yole pima-pima pyoo, yongama wamba ipamino dutupanya tuu lapena' lea.
Dokopa kalai akali 5 kilokonya, kalai tee piamino dupa ipupala, 1 kina lao nyiami.
Dopa pyoo nyiaminosa, kalai akali yongama wamba kalai tee piamino, dupame nyakama muni mendalapo, apata wakao nyalamano lao masiaminoaka doko, nyakama apata 1 kina laowaka nyiami.
Dopa pyoo nyepala, akali ee tange doko imbu kaeyapala, mumu leami.
Dopa latala akali ee tange doko lamaiyoo, 'Kalai akali 5 kilokonya ipamino datupame, awa mendai iki kalai pimino. Naima indupa gii dake pitaka, niki yale mende tapumupa, leke-leke tao kalai pyemano doko, embame dupa naima-pipa kapa-kapa lao, yole pilino doko, auu napilyamona' leami.
Dopa leaminopa, akali ee tange dokome kalai akali dupanya mende lamaiyoo, 'Kaimia, nambame emba minakasala naeyalo. Emba 1 kina nyotoana lapinopa, nalimba pii lao yaki pyaa naeyalambape?
Kalai akali maitapyao ipamino dupa, emba yole pilyo dopaka pyoo, dutupa nambanya auu kaengeme yole pyoo. Nambanya muni dokome, mendita mende pitoo lao masotoli pyoo napitupi? Nambame kalai akali maitapyao ipamino dupa, nambanya kondo kaengeme, 1 kina laowaka maiyo dokonya, embame dokaita-pipa tilya nyala naenya, embanya yole doko nyoo puu' lea-pyaa.
<range>
Dopana, epapu endakali mendapu wambao kalyamino dupa, tanga maita pyatami. Maitapyao kalyamino dupa, tanga wambatamina” Jisasame lea.
Jisasa Jerusalema pao pituu, baanya 12 disaipolo dutupa iki laminao, umbisale pupala lamaiyoo,
“Salapape! Naima indupa Jerusalema pelyamano. Dokonya akali mendeme, Akalinya Ikiningi doko enge nyepala, pitisa mupapi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, dupa laitaka pitamopa, dupame baa kote latala pyao kumasina latami.
Dopa latala dupame baa akali kamalya katenge dupanya, kingilyaka maitaminopa, dokaitame baa kandao lamba latala, konjame pyapala, poko itanya pyao yukutami. Dopa petataminopa, yuu gii tepo dokonya, Goteme dee sakatasetana” lea.
Jemesa, Jonepanya endangi dokome, Jisasa-kisa dopale mende tee latoo lao masetala, nyakamba-pipa apata ipao, Jisasanya enombanya baa luma lakea.
Dokopa Jisasame baa tipa pyoo, “Nambame embanya aipa pyakaowape?” lea. Dopa leamopa, enda dokome baa lamaiyoo, “Embanya isingi mate dokonya, kiŋi joo pititinopa, nambanya wane dalaponya mende, embanya kingi tolae-kaita petena lakape, mende embanya kingi koeya-kaita petena lakape” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Embame masala naeyao lelenona” lea. Dopa latala, wane dolapo lamaiyoo, “Nambame kenda pipae salapo-lamo doko, nyakambame kapa pao setambipi?” lea. Dokopa dolapome yanu pyao, “Nalimbame kenda pipae dupa, kapa pao setambakana” leambi.
Dopa leambinopa, Jisasame dolapo lamaiyoo, “Kini nyakambame kende pipae dupa setambiaka. Dopaka doko, nambanya kingi tolae-kaita petena lapengepi, koeya-kaita petena lapengepi, doko nambanya kalai daa. Nambanya Takangeme pititamina lao, yapao nyiamo endakali dupa pititamina” lea.
Pii doko sepala, 10-pela disaipolo dutupame Jemesa Jonepa imbu kaeyami.
Dopa piaminopa, Jisasame dokaita pitaka epena latala lamaiyoo, “Akali kantri waka isingi, Gote tungi napingi dupame, nyakamanya endakali isingi dupa kandanya palyetala, nyakama alyasale joo katengema, doko nyakamame kandengema. Kantri dupanya akali andake dupame, nyakamanya pii watao minekena lao kandatae paengema, mana doko nyakamame kandengemaka.
Nyakamame dopa napyepape. Nyakamanya mende akali andake joo katapuli lao masetamo dokome, nyakamanya kalai akali joo katapenge.
Dee nyakamanya mende alyasale joo katapuli lao masetamo dokome, nyakamanya kendemane joo katapenge.
Dopaka pyoo, Akalinya Ikiningi dokome baanya kalai pyekena lao naepea. Baame endakali longo dupa nisoo, kii tamao nyalanya, baa tangeme kumala epeana” lea.
Jisasa baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa, taono Jereko doko yakinatala peaminopa, endakali kambu andake mendeme baa watao peami.
Dokopa, akali lenge monda lapoma kaitinisa peteambi. Akali dolapome Jisasa epelyamo leamino sepala, wii lao, “Dapiti Yumbange! Kamongo! Embame nalimba kondo kaeyapoko” leambi.
Dopa leambinopa, endakali dupame pii kaena lao pyalanya leami. Dopa leaminoaka doko, akali dolapome dee puu lao wii lao, “Dapiti Yumbange! Kamongo! Embame nalimba kondo kaeyapoko” leambi.
Dopa leambinopa, Jisasa baa katapala, akali dolapo epena latala lamaiyoo pituu, “Nambame nyakambanya aipa pyakapili lao masilyambipi?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, akali dolapome baa lamaiyoo, “Kamongo, nalimba dee lenge tao kandambana, embame nalimba nisepoko” leambi.
Dopa leambinopa, Jisasame dolapo kondo kaeyapala, baanya kingimi dolaponya lengenya watandalu piamopa, nyakamba lapota lenge talu piambi. Dopa petakamaiyamopa, nyakamba baa watao peambi.
Jisasa disaipolo dupa-pipa Jerusalema tengesa, Olipimanda dokonya taono Betepasa peami. Pao pituu, Jisasame disaipolo lapoma wambao pena latala
lamaiyoo, “Taono yakane silyamo omonya pupala, dongi matakai mende, yakane-pipa anjetae kalyamona, lapota tata lao minao ipupape.
Endakali mendeme nyakamba kandao pii mende lea kandeno doko, nyakambame baa lamaiyoo, 'Kamongome dongi dalapo minao, kalai mende pipenge jilyamo laamona' lapape. Dokopa baame yapa dyaapomona” lea.
Dopa piamo dokome, propeta mendeme pii leamo dake angi jia:
“Jerusalema tange dupa lamaiyoo, 'Nyakamanya kiŋi doko, dongi yakane mendenya maitanya pituu, akali kenge nasingi joo, nisala epelyamona kanjepape' lao, lamaiyepape” lea-pyaa.
Dokopa disaipolo dolapome pupala, Jisasame leamoli piambi.
Dopa petala dolapome, dongi matakai doko yakane-pipa minao epeambi. Ipupala nyakambanya yonge pee ketae pingi dolapo, dongi dolaponya maitanya seteambinopa, Jisasa pyakalyetala, pituu pea.
Peamopa, endakali kambu andake mendeme, nyakamanya yonge pee ketae pingi dupa, kaitini dokonya kuiyami. Yangi dupame ita yoko dupa lakao, kaitini dokonya kuiyamiaka.
Dokopa endakali dupa wambata, maita pyata pyoo pao pituu, puu lao wii lao, “Dapiti Yumbange doko epelyamo dokonya, naimanya Gote doko lao mambo pilyamano! Kamongonya kengenya akali epelyamo dake, Goteme auu pisetae! Gote Ketae Kaitinya Katenge doko lao mambo pilyamano!” leami.
Jisasa Jerusalema pao pyakameamopa, endakali dupa pitakame walu latala, “Akali epelyamo dake apipi?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, endakali kambu Jisasa-pipa apata peamino dupame, “Akali epelyamano dake kenge Jisasa lenge. Baa yuu andake Galilea taono Nasarete, tange propeta dokona” leami.
Jisasa lotuu anda andake kame dokonya kolandatala, endakali maketa setao kateamipi, sambao kateamipi, dupa kandatala imbu kaeya. Imbu kaeyapala, toko ketae muni aloo piamino dupapi, yaka maiyolee maketa setao petenge toko dupa minalyetala, kaii lao nepatala watao pia.
Dopa petala baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Pii pepa pyapae singi dokonya, 'Gotenya lotuu anda andake doko, loma singi anda latamina' lapae silyamo. Dopaka doko, nyakamame anda dake, pake nengemanya anda jinya nepelyaminona” lea.
Endakali lenge mondapi, moko koopi, dupa Jisasa kateasa lotuu anda andake dokonya, kame andakote epeaminopa, baame yaina dupa mee jakamaiya.
Dopa piamopa, wane koo dupame, lotuu anda andake dokonya kame andakote katao, wee lao, “Naimame Gote lao Dapiti Yumbange, doko mambo pilyamano!” leami. Wee leamino dupa sepa, Jisasanya kalai pupu lapae piamo dupa kandata petala, pitisa mupapi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, dupame imbu kaeyami.
Imbu kaeyapala dokaitame Jisasa tipa pyoo, “Wane koo dupame wee lelyamino dupa embame silipi?” leami. Dopa leaminopa, baame yanu pyao, “Kini nambame silyo. 'Wane koo dupame, kambumi Gote lao mambo pyatamina' lao, pepa pyapae silyamo doko nyakamame itaki napiamipi?” lea.
Dopa latala baame dokaita yakinatala, Betani pao palea.
Oo yongama wamba, Jisasa dee Jerusalema pilyoo pituu, baa lopo kaeya.
Lopo kaeyapala baame piki ita mende kaitini lembasa kateamo kandatala, dokonya dii lyilyape lao kanja pea. Pao kandeamopa, dii nalyoo yoko iki pyoo katea. Dokopa baame piki ita doko kandao, “Embame tanga tangapi dee dii mende namanditina” lea. Dopa lalu piamopa, piki ita doko sapuiya.
Disaipolo dupame piamo doko kandatala walu leami. Walu latala tipa pyoo, “Piki ita dake aipa petala pupae lao sapuilyape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaitanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Nyakamame mona lapo palya naenya, Gote tungi pyatamino doko, nambame piki ita dake pilyoliaka nyakamame pitami. Dee nyakamanya mendeme, yuu manda dake sakatatala, solowatanya pyakala pena latamino doko, kini dopaka pita.
Nyakamame Gote tungi pyatala, dopale mende nyemana lao loma soo, tee latamino dupa pitaka, Goteme ditana” lea.
Jisasa lotuu anda andake dokonya, kamenya andakote pilyetala, endakali dupa mana lamaiyoo kateamopa, pitisa mupapi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, dupame ipupala baa tipa pyoo, “Emba apimi kalai andake dupa pii lapumupa pilipi?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaitanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Nambame nyakama tipa mende pitoaka, nyakamame yanu pyatamino doko, nambame kalai dupa akali dokome pii lapumupa pilyona lao, nyakama langitoaka.
Joneme kaimbu piamo mana doko, apimi pina leamopa piape? Goteme pina leape, pande akalimi pina leamipi?” lea. Dopa leamopa, dokaitame pii doko sepala, nyakamalapo laloo pyoo, “Naimame 'Joneme kaimbu piamo mana doko, Goteme pina leana' latamano doko, 'Aipuma nyakamame baanya pii doko, kiningina lao masala naelyamipi?' laapome-lumu.
Dopaka doko, endakali kambu dakeme, Jone baa propeta kiningina lao masingima dokonya, naimame, 'Akalimi pina leamina,' laanya paka pyuumuna” leami.
Dopa latala dupame Jisasanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Apimi Joneme kaimbu pina leape lao, naimame masala naelyamanona” leami. Dokopa Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Dopa-tamo doko, nambame kalai dupa akali dokome, pii lapumupa pilyona lao, nyakama langya naeyatoakana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Akali mendeme wane lapoma mandea-pyaa. Takangeme wane mupa doko lamaiyoo, 'Emba indupa waene ee dokonya kalai pyaa puu' lea.
Dopa leamopa, wane mupa dokome yanu pyao, 'Namba napatoana,' leamoaka doko, maitakao mona aloo petala pea.
Dokopa takange dokome wane kole doko, kateasa pao dopaka lamaiya. Dopa lamaiyamopa, 'Apane, yakalumuna' latala, angi napea.
Dopa latala, “Wane dolaponya andukumi, takangenya masiamoli piape?” lao, Jisasame pitisa mupapi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, dupa tipa pia. Dokopa dokaitame yanu pyao, “Wane mupa dokomena” leami. Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame lamaiyoo, “Jone kaimbu pingi dokome, mana epe tolatae dupa leamopa, nyakamame kiningina lao masala naeyami. Dopaka doko, takisa nyingi akalipi, 2 kina endapi, dupame kiningina lao masiamino dokonya, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya, wambao puminopa, nyakama mona aloo napilyamino dokonya, nyakama napelyaminona lao kiningi langilyona” lea.
<range>
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Kongali pii dake salapape. Akali yuu andake singi mendeme, waene ee mende kame petala pokea-pyaa. Pokatala dii lyao waene ipange nyalanya, takyoo indyapenge yuli mende tombao wasia. Wasetala ee doko kandao isoo pitipenge, anda ketae mende pia. Petala akali mendapu-pipa, propeta mokosetamanopa latala, ee doko isoo bisnis pyoo katekena latala, baa yuu londati mendakaita pao katea.
Waene wambu pingi gii doko epeamopa, baanya kalai akali mendapuame, ee isakamaingi akali dupa kateamisa pupala, waene baa nyepenge dupa peekena nyala pena lea.
Leamo dokonya pateaminopa, ee isakamaingi akali dupame baanya kalai akali dupa minatala, mende pyao indyepa, mende pyao kumaseta, mende kaname pyapa piami.
Dopa peteaminopa, akali ee tange dokome, dee kalai akali longo pena lea. Ee dokonya pateaminopa, ee isakamaingi dupame, wamba peamino dupa-kisa piaminoliaka piami.
Dopa peteaminopa, akali dokonya ikiningi doko, andanda semaiyamino lao masetala, baa etao pena lea.
Wane doko epeamo kandatala, ee isakamaingi dupame nyakamalapo laloo pyoo, 'Wane dakeme takangenya moeya dupa nyepengena, baa pyao kumasetamano doko, baanya moeya nyepenge dupa naima nyetamana' leami.
Dopa latala wane doko minatala, ee dokonya kamalya pyale latala, pyao kumasiamina” Jisasame lea.
Dopa latala Jisasame dokaita tipa pyoo, “Dopa piami-lumu dokonya, akali ee tange dokome ipupala, ee isakamaingi dupa aipa pitape?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, dokaitame yanu pyao, “Akali ee tange dokome, akali koo dokaita tanda maiyoo, pyao kumaseta. Dopa petala akali waka, waene dii lyao tange maiyakamaipenge, mendapuame ee doko isoo katekena lao, laitaka pitana” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame pii pepa pyapae silyamo dake, itaki pyala naeyamipi? 'Kapenda dupame, anda pipenge kana mende kandao, koeyapae-lamo latala yakineamino doko, kana mupa jetelyamo. Kana mupa jetelyamo doko, Kamongome pipya-lamo dokonya, naimame eteteaka auu kaeyao, sani kandelyamano'” lapae silyamo.
Dopana, ee tange dokome baanya ee doko, akali waka mendapuame, isoo katekena leamoli pyoo, Goteme nyakama daa latala, baanya isingi mate doko, akali waka mendapuame isoo katekena lata.
Endakali mendeme kana dokonya pao lombapae setamo doko, baa indyuu koeyata. Dee kana doko kolimbatala pyatamo doko, baa indyuu koeyatakana” lea.
Jisasame dopa leamopa, Parasaipi, pitisa mupapi dupame pii kongali dupa, nyakama kandao lalumuna lao sepala,
baa anjemana lao kaita kutiami. Kutiaminoaka doko, endakali kambu kateamino dupame, Jisasa baa propetana lao masiaminosa, paka kaeyapala baa yakineami.
Jisasame kongali pii mende deaka dokaita lamaiyoo, “Gotenya isingi mate doko dapale mende: Kiŋi mendenya ikiningi doko, enda keleamopa, takangeme nee andake mende yangakamaiya-pyaa.
<range>
Kiŋi dokome baanya kalai akali dupame, endakali nee napenge latae dupa lanyala pena lea. Dopa lateamopa, nyakama pupala, nee nala epena lamaiyaminopa, dokaitame nyakama naipumanana leami.
Dopa piaminosa, baame kalai akali mendatupa pena lao pituu, 'Endakali nee napenge latae dupa kandao, “Bulumakao maipapi, bulumakao andapaepi, dupa pyapalamo. Dupa pitaka depa latae sepelyamona, nyakama dokonya nala ipupa” lapape' lea.
Dokopa kalai akali dupame pao lamaiyaminoaka doko, endakali nee napenge latae dupame, pii nepatala, nyakamanya masiaminoli pyoo, mende baanya eenya pea, mende baanya bisnis pyaa pea.
Dee yangimi kalai akali dupa minatala, mana koo minao pyao kumasiami.
Dopa piamino doko, kiŋi dokome sepala, imbu kaeya. Imbu kaeyapala baanya yanda singi dupame, kalai akali pyao kumasiamino dupa pyao kumasetala, dupanya taono doko yangala pena lea.
Dokopa kiŋi dokome baanya kalai akali dupa lamaiyoo, 'Nambanya nee andake doko depa latae sepelyamoaka doko, nee napenge latae endakali dupa mana epe naminingima, dokonyana nee nala naepena daa lelyo.
Dopana, nyakamame endakali kambu pingi panda dupanya pupala, endakali kandatamino dupa pitaka, nee andake dakenya nala epena lamaiyepape' lea.
Dopa lateamopa, kalai akali dokaitame kaitini dupanya pupala, endakali koopi epepi kandeamino dupa pitaka laminao, ipao kambu piaminopa, nee andake napenge panda doko, tumbiami.
Peteamino dokonya kiŋi dokome ipupala, endakali dokaita kandeamopa, akali mende yonge pee, enda kelyengesa pingi doko napyoo peteamo kandea.
Kandatala kiŋi dokome baa lamaiyoo, 'Kaimia, aipuma embanya yonge pee, enda kelyengesa pingi doko napyoo dakenya epepe?' lea. Dopa leamopa, akali doko ema napia.
Dokopa kiŋi dokome baanya kalai akali dupa lamaiyoo, 'Akali dake kingi mokopi yaki petala, kamalya iminjetae, endakali ee lao, yamataka lao, nenge gilyoo katenge dokonya soo pyale lapa' lea.
Dopana, Goteme endakali longo dupa epena lengeaka doko, baame endakali kuki yapao nyingina,” Jisasame lea.
Dokopa Parasai dupame pupala, Jisasame pii mende kopeta latamo dokonya, baa mangenya minamana latala, pii lao kambuiyami.
Dopa petala Parasai dupame, nyakamanya disaipolo mendapuapi, Erote Antipasa tata mendapuapi, dupa Jisasa kateasa pena leami. Dupame pupala Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Mana Lenge Akali, embame akali andake dupa paka nakaeyao, kiningi pii doko tolao lenge. Endakali dupame pipimili lao Goteme masilyamo, dokonya-kaita embame tolao mana lenge.
Dopana, embame aipa lao masili? Gapomane andake Sisa doko, naimame takisa maipengepe, daape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame baa minao koeyasalanya, makande pilyamini-lamo lao kandatala, dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakama Gote watao miningi mane-mane pingima dupame, aipuma namba minao makande pilyamipi?
Takisa maipenge muni konde mende, kandatoo nyoo dyepa” lea. Dokopa muni konde mende maitiaminopa,
Jisasame dokaita tipa pyoo, “Muni konde dakenya, apinya lengelyapi, kengepi kalyape?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, dokaitame yanu pyao, “Sisanya kalyamona” leami. Dopa leaminopa, baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Sisanya dupa Sisa tange maiyakamaiyepape. Gotenya dupa Gote tange maiyakamaiyepape” lea.
Pii yanu pyao leamo doko sepala, dokaitame paka kaeyapala, baa yakinatala peami.
Sadyusi dupame, endakali kumapae dupa sakatala naeyatana lengema. Gii dokopaka, dopa lengema dupa, Jisasa kateasa ipupala baa lamaiyoo,
“Mana Lenge Akali, wamba Mosesame mana leamo dokonya, 'Akali mendeme enda nyepala, wane manja naeyao kumatamopa, baanya kaiminingi dokome enda walyakae doko piseta. Baapa enda walyakae dokopa, wane mupa manditambino doko, kaiminingi kumia dokonya lao, manjakamaitana' lapae silyamo.
Gii mendepa akali mendenya, ikiningi 7-pela naima-pipa kateamano dokonya, mupa dokome enda nyepala, wane manja naeyao kumia. Kumateamopa, kaiminingi lapo dokome enda walyakae doko pisia.
Pisiamoaka doko, wane namandeamopa, akali doko kumia. Kaiminingi teponge dokome, dopaka pia. Dopaka pyoo, kaiminingi 7-pela dutupa pitakame, enda dokoaka nyepala, wane manja naeyaowaka kumiami.
Dokaita kumao ete dokonya, enda doko kumia.
Akali kaiminingi 7-pela dutupa pitakame, enda mendai dokoaka nyiamino dokonya, tanga endakali sakatatamino gii dokopa, enda doko apinya jetape?” lao tipa piami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame yanu pyao, “Nyakamame pii pepa pyapae singi doko, masala naeyao, Gotenya pupu lapae, doko masala naeyaowaka pingima dokonya, nyakamame kopeta lelyamino.
Endakali kumapae dupa dee sakatatamino gii dokopa, akali enda nyala naeyao, enda akali napao, kaitinya enjele dupa katengemali pyoo katatami.
Endakali kumapae dupa, dee sakatatamino dokonya, Goteme pii lanya seteamo dake, itaki napiamipi?
Goteme 'Namba Abrakame, Aisake, Jekopepinya Gotena' lea. Baa kumapae dupanya Gote daa. Baa saka katenge dupanya Gote. Abrakame, Aisake, Jekopepi dee tanga sakatao katatamina lao, Goteme masala naeyali doko, baa dutupanya Gote laa naeyalina” lea.
Dopa leamopa, endakali kambu piamino dupame baanya mana leamo dupa sepala, walu lao paka kaeyami.
Jisasame Sadyusi dupa pii nalena lao, etete auu pyoo yanu pyakamaiyamo sepala, Parasai dupa Jisasa kateasa ipao kapeami.
Kapeamino dupanya, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali mendeme, Jisasa minao makande pyoo,
“Mana Lenge Akali, Mosesanya loo dupanya anduku mupa joo silyape?” lao, tipa pia.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “'Embame embanya Kamongo Gote doko, embanya monapi, imambupi, masingipi, dutupa pitakame auu kaeyape.'
Doko loo mupa doko.
Loo lapo doko dake: 'Embame emba tange auu kaengeli pyoo, embanya endakali yango dupa auu kaeyape.'
Mosesanya loo setapaepi, propeta dupame pepa piamipi, dupa pitaka loo lapoma dolaponya, koko palelyamona” lea.
Parasai dupa kapatae kateaminopa, Jisasame dokaita tipa pyoo,
“Nyakamame Mesaeya dokonya yumbange doko, apina lao masilyamipi?” leamopa, “Baa Dapitinya yumbangena” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dupa lamaiyoo, “Oli Spiritame lungu piamopa, Dapitimi dapa lea: 'Goteme nambanya Kamongo Mesaeya doko lamaiyoo, “Emba nambanya kingi tolae-kaita piti. Dokonya pititinopa, nambame embanya yandapipi dupa ita minatakala, embanya moko pundi-pundi katena latona' lao, pyapae silyamo.” Dopa latala Jisasame dokaita tipa pyoo, “Dapitimi Mesaeya doko kandao, baanya Kamongona lea-lumu doko, kaitini andukunya-kaita, Mesaeya doko baanya yumbangena leape? Mesaeya doko baa Dapitinya yumbange iki daa. Baanya Kamongo dokona lao, nyakamame masala naelyamipi?” lea.
<range>
<range>
Dopa lateamopa, akali mendeme Jisasanya pii doko kapa pao, yanu pyapenge nanjia. Gii dokonya pituu, akali mendaipi mendeme, baa tipa pyaanya paka kaeyami.
Jisasame endakali kambu andake piamipi, baanya disaipolopi, dupa lamaiyoo,
“Loo mana nyepae akalipi, Parasaipi, dupame Mosesanya panda nyoo mana lengema.
Dopana, dupame nyakama langitamino dupa pitaka pyepape. Dopaka doko, dupame mana lelyaminoli pyoo, nyakama tange watao minala naengemana, nyakamame dopa napyepape.
Dee dupame kenda pipae dupa, endakali dupanya lataiyanya nyoo sakamaitala, nyakamame kukipi mende nisoo sala naengema.
Nyakama alyasale joo kalyamano lao masetala, pilyamino dupa pitaka, endakali dupame kandamili laka lao sakao pingima. Dupame Gotenya pii dokonya mendatupa, pepa pyanya bokosa yakane mendenya mandipala, langalunya angatatenge joo petala, mende kinginya kitambu joo pisetala, endakalimi kandamili lao paengema. Dee nyakamanya yonge pee ketae pingi punanya, yati pipae londe dupa, anjinya pyandatala paengemaka.
Dee Judamanya lotuu lelyamipi, nee andake nelyamipi, dupanya nyakama enomba nyoaka pitipumali laka lao masingima.
Dee kamapu dupanya endakali dupame, mana lenge akali lao, kingi nyoo, mambo pilyaminopa, dopaka pipimi laka lao masingima.
Dopa pingimaka doko, nyakamanya Mana Lenge Akali mendai iki kalyamo, dokonya nyakama kaiminingiaka kalyaminona, endakali dupame nyakama kandao, mana lenge akali lena nalalapape.
Gote kaitinya katenge doko iki, nyakamanya Takangena, nyakamame isa yuu dakenya endakali mende, lalyoo takange laa naeyalapape.
Nyakamanya Akali Andake mendai iki kalyamo, doko baa Kraisana, endakali dupame nyakama kandao, akali andake lena nalalapape.
Nyakamanya mendeme akali andake joo katapuli lao, masetamo doko baa, nyakamanya kalai akali joo katapenge.
Endakali mendeme tange kenge minalyoo katatamo doko, baa kenge anasale joo seta. Dee endakali mendeme tange kenge minanao katatamo doko, baa kenge alyasale joo seta.
“Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, Parasaipi, nyakama Gote watao miningi mane-mane pingima dupa, koeyatamina kandao kalyepape. Nyakama Gotenya isingi mate dokonya napenge dupame, endakali paanya pipimi dupanya kaita lyokelyamino.
<range>
“Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, Parasaipi, nyakama Gote watao miningi mane-mane pingima dupa, koeyatamina kandao kalyepape. Nyakamame disaipolo mende nyemana lao kutao, solowata yangitena pata, yuu waka dupanya pata pingima. Dokopa endakali mende nyilyamino doko, nyakamanya mana koeyapae dupa lamailyaminopa, baa etete koenge.
“Akali lenge monda dupame, endakali waka dupa kii miningima-lamo dupa, nyakama koeyatamina kandao kalyepape. Nyakamame endakali dupa mana lamaiyoo pituu, 'Endakali mendeme lotuu anda andake dokonya kenge latala, kiningi etete mende pituna latala, napitamo doko yakaka. Dopaka doko, endakali mendeme lotuu anda andake dokonya golome wasepae, setamo dupanya kenge latala, kiningi etete mende pituna latamo dokome, kaeyala naeyao, latamoli pipengena' lengema.
Nyakama lenge monda kyakaenge! Lotuu anda andake dokome, golome wasepae andakote silyamo dupa, Gote maitaena lao auu pisingi. Tenge dokonya, golome wasepae andakote silyamo dupame, lotuu anda andake doko ita naminingi. Lotuu anda andake dokome, golome wasepae andakote silyamo dupa, ita miningi.
Dee nyakamame endakali dupa mana lamaiyoo pituu, 'Endakali mendeme lotuu anda andake dokonya, alta dokonya kenge latala, kiningi etete mende pituna latala, napitamo doko yakaka. Dopaka doko, endakali mendeme opa alta ketae setamo dokonya, kenge latala, kiningi etete mende pituna latamo dokome, kaeyala naeyao latamoli pipengena' lengema.
Nyakama lenge monda daape! Alta dokome opa ketae silyamo dupa, Gote maitaena lao auu pisingi. Tenge dokonya, opa alta ketae silyamo dupame, alta doko ita naminingi. Alta dokome opa, alta ketae silyamo dupa ita miningi.
Dopana, endakali mendeme alta dokonya kenge latala, kiningi etete mende pituna latamo doko, opa alta ketae setamo dupa, apata kandao lata.
Dee endakali mendeme lotuu anda andake dokonya, kenge latala, kiningi etete mende pituna latamo dokome, lotuu anda andake dokonya katenge Gote doko, apata kandao lata.
Dee endakali mendeme, kaiti dokonya kenge latala, kiningi etete mende pituna latamo dokome, Gotenya petenge toko dokopa, toko dokonya petenge Gote dokopa, apata kandao lata.
“Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, Parasaipi, nyakama Gote watao miningi mane-mane pingima dupa, koeyatamina kandao kalyepape. Nyakama lenge monda dupame, endakali waka dupa kii miningima-lamo. Nyakamame takaepi, mondaipi, itamaiyapi, dupa malu 10-pela mokosoo setapala, dutupanya malu mendai Gote maingima. Dopa pingimaka doko, mana epeme endakali tolasingipi, kondo kaengepi, Gote tungi pingipi, loo andake dutupa nyakamame watao naminingima-lamo. Nyakamame loo yakane dupa watao miningimali pyoo, loo andake dupa apata watao minalapape. Dopa napitamino doko, nyakamanya kapo mendenya pongena mende, koko setamo doko, nyoo nepatala, kamele mende nyoo nengekaita goe lapimili dopale-lamo.
<range>
“Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, Parasaipi, nyakama Gote watao miningi mane-mane pingima dupa, koeyatamina kandao kalyepape. Endakali mendeme kapopi, pelesapi, ketaetena iki wasa pyatala, koko wasa napingili pyoo, nyakamanya yongeme Gote watao miningi mane-mane petala, nyakama iki lao masingipi, putiti kaengepi, mana dopaleme mona andaka tumbatae kalyamo.
Nyakama Parasai dupa lenge monda! Nyakamame kapopi, pelesapi, kaimala pipae dupa koko wambao wasa pyapenge. Pyataminopa, ketaetena wasa pyatae katata.
“Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, Parasaipi, nyakama Gote watao miningi mane-mane pingima dupa, koeyatamina kandao kalyepape. Endakali malu yati petae katengeli pyoo, nyakama kalyamino. Malu ketae yatimi auu pilyamopa, malu koko tamuo, endakali kuli akipi aimi koenge dopale joo nyakama kalyamino.
Dokaita joo, nyakamanya yongeme tolatae mane-mane pilyaminopa, mona andaka endakali yango minakasoo, koeyapae mana miningi dupa tumbatae kalyamo.
“Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, Parasaipi, nyakama Gote watao miningi mane-mane pingima dupa, koeyatamina kandao kalyepape. Nyakamame propeta kumiami dupanya, malu-kisa anda epe dupa petala, endakali tolatae kumilyami dupanya, malu dupa yati pisingima.
Dopa pyoo pituu, 'Wamba naimanya yumbange kateamino gii dokopa, naima kateamali doko, yumbange dupame propeta dupa pyao kumasiaminopa, naimame yumbange dupa nisala naeyamalina' lengema.
Nyakamame dopa lelyamino dokome, nyakama propeta dupa pyao kumasiamino, akali dupanya mandipaena lao panelyamo.
Dopana, nyakamanya yumbange dupame kalai piamino doko, nyakamame indupa pyoo etasalapape.
Nyakama koo kanopatonya mandipae dupa, Goteme ele panda koo dokonya watao pyandatamo doko, aipa petala wanditamipi?
Nambame propetapi, masepae singi akalipi, mana lenge akalipi, dupa nyakamanya kainanya epena lato. Dopa pitupa, nyakamame dupanya yangi dupa pyao kumasetami. Yangi dupa pyao poko itanya yukutami. Yangi dupa nyakamanya lotuu anda dupanya konjame pyatami. Yangi dupa nyakamame taono mendenya pituu, mendenya watao paeyao pyatami.
Nyakamame dopa pitaminosa, wamba akali tolatae kateamino dupa pitaka pyao kumasiami dokonya, tenge doko nyakama-kisa seta. Akali tolatae Abele lenge doko, pyao kumasiami dokonya pituu, Berekia ikiningi Sakaraeya, lotuu anda andakepa, altapa, dolaponya kainanya pyanya seteami, dokonya tuu lao tenge doko, nyakama-kisa seta.
Dopa piamino dupa pitakanya, yanu doko endakali indupa palelyamino dupa-kisa, ipatana lao nambame nyakama kiningi langilyona” lea.
Jisasame Jerusalema tange dupa kondo kaeyao, “O Jerusalema Jerusalema! Nyakamame propeta dupa pyao kumasoo, Goteme epena latae akali dupa, kaname pyao kumasoaka katengema. Paa longosa, nambame nyakama nyoo kambu pyatala, yaka matakaimi yakane dupa, papa pundi-pundi, yapu nengeli pitoo lao masipupa, nyakamame tanga lelyamino.
Goteme nyakamanya lotuu anda andake doko yakinatamopa, anda doko mee katata.
Nyakamame 'Akali mende, Goteme epena lapumupa, epelyamo doko Goteme auu pisetaena' latamino dokopa, nyakamame namba dee kandatamina lao, nambame nyakama langilyona” Jisasame lea.
Jisasame lotuu anda andake, kame doko yakinatala peamopa, disaipolo dupame ipupala baa lamaiyoo, “Lotuu anda andake dakenya makisa, anda auu petae kalyamo datupa kanda” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Anda kana soo namba-namba pyoo petae kalyamo, kandelyamino datupa, tanga dopaka petae nakatata. Pitaka pyao kaluo nepatamina” lea.
Jisasa Olipimanda peteamopa, disaipolo dupa elyakalao ipupala baa tipa pyoo, “Embame laleno dutupa, gii andukupa dopa pitape? Gii etatamo dokopi, emba ipateno gii dokopi, dolaponya kongali aipale mende pitamopa kandatamape? Naima langi” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame yanu pyao, “Endakali mendeme nyakama minao kyakasetana, kandao kalyepape.
Endakali longome nambanya kengenya ipupala, 'Namba Kraisa dokona' lao, endakali longo minao kyakasetami.
Yanda pilyamino lapaepi, yanda ingingi lapaepi, dupa sepala, nyakama walu nalalapape. Kenda pipae andake dopale dupa pitaka ipatamoaka doko, yuu etapenge gii doko maitapyao ipata.
Kantri mendeme kantri mende yanda pimaita, kiŋi mendeme kiŋi mende yanda pimaita pitami. Dee yuu wakale-wakale dupanya, titiwali dupa minata, lopo andake dupa sepa pita.
Dopa pitamo doko, enda wane manjanya maita pingi dopale joo pita.
“Gii dokopa nyakama namba tata joo katataminosa, akali tata dupa pitakame, nyakama etete imbu kaengitami. Dopa petala, nyakama anjetala, pyao tanda ditala kumasetami.
Dokopa endakali longome, namba tungi pingima doko yakinatala, nyakamalapo imbu kaeyao pyaloo petala, mende enge nyaa-nyaa pitami.
Dee sambo propeta longo mendapuame ipupala, endakali longo dupa minao kyakasetami.
Luiyao koo pingi mana doko andatamopa, endakali longo dupame, endakali yango auu kaenge mana doko yakinatami.
Dopa pitaminopapi, endakali mende kyeto joo katao etatamo doko, baa Goteme pyoo nyeta.
Gotenya isingi mate dokonya lao, wai pii epe doko endakali dupa pitaka, sina lao lamaitami. Endakali dupa pitaka pii lamaiyoo kapa petataminopa, yuu etapenge gii doko ipatana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “'Gii mendepa akali mendeme myuku pipae mende, lotuu anda andake andakote nyoo setatamopa kandatala, endakali dupame lotuu anda andake doko yakinatami. Dokonya lao wamba propeta Danieleme leamo doko, angi jetamo kandatala, endakali Judia katatamino dupa, paka yuu manda dupanya pupenge jetana” lea. (Pii dake itaki pyateno dokome, tenge doko kutao nyepe.)
<range>
Gii dokopa endakali mende, baanya anda patakisa katatamo dokome, baanya oapi andakote setamo dupa nyalanya, andakote pupenge nanjeta.
Dee endakali mende eesa katatamo dokome, baanya yonge pee ketae pingi doko nyalanya, pilyala naeyapengeaka jeta.
Enda wane tongatapi, enda wane andu nengepi, dupa gii dokopa etete kondo pita.
Koo kana palitamopapi, Sambata gii palitamopapi, paka napataminopana, nyakama loma soo kalyepape.
Goteme yuu kaitipi wasiamo dokonya pituu, indupa tuu lao, kenda pipae epelyamo dupa pitaka, kenda pipae ene ipatamo dokome ita minata. Dee kenda pipae dopale mende tanga tangapi naipata.
Goteme yuu gii dupa muu pisala naeyatamo doko, endakali mendaipi mende nakatata. Dopaka doko, baanya endakali yapao nyepae dupa lao masetala, kenda pipaepi, yuu giipi, dupa minao muu piseta.
Gii dokopa Gotenya yapao nyepae endakali dupa lanyoo, lemba pyalanya, sambo Kraisa mane-mane pipaepi, sambo propetapi, dupame ipupala, kongalipi, mirakolo kalaipi, dupa pitami. Dopana, endakali mendeme nyakama langyoo, 'Kraisa doko asa kalyamo kanjepa, amasa kalyamo kanjepa' lea kandeno doko, kiningi lelyamona lao masala naeyalapape.
<range>
Nambame enesa tanga pitamo dupa langilyona, nyakama kandao kalyepape.
Paa mendai, yuu-wapaka pilyamopa, tii pipae doko niki pyakaengesa pituu, niki pambengesa tuu lenge. Dopa pilyamopa, endakali dupa pitakame kandengema. Dopaka pyoo, Akalinya Ikiningi doko ipatamopa, endakali pitakame kandatami. Dopana, endakali mendeme nyakama langyoo, 'Kraisa doko endakali napalenge yuu dokonya kalyamona, kanja pupa' lea kandeno doko, kanja napupape. Dee endakali mendeme, 'Kraisa doko anda dakenya andakote pilyamona' lea kandeno doko, kiningi lelyamona lao masala naeyalapape.
<range>
Yaka lakepame buu minilyamopa, konaiyapi mende kumapae salame-lamo lao kandengema. Dopaka pyoo, kenda pipae dopale dupa ipatamopa, Akalinya Ikiningi doko ipanya tengesa pilyamona lao, kandatamina” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Kenda pipae andake dupa etalu dokonya, kaitinya singi dupa pitaka ema-ema pita. Dopa pitamopa, niki doko iminjoo, kana doko tii napyoo, kaitinya bui dupa kondao isa ipao pita.
Dokopa Akalinya Ikiningi doko ipanya, kongali mende kaitinya pitamopa, yuunya akali tata dupa pitakame kandatala, yako lao ee latami. Dokopa Akalinya Ikiningi doko baanya pupu lapaepi, tii pipaepi, dupanya pituu kopa tambe-tambe ipata.
Dokopa beto mende puu lao latamopa, yuu lemba dupa pitakanya pituu, enjele dupame endakali yapao nyepae dupa pitaka, lanyoo kambu pina latana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Nyakamame piki ita dokonya mana mende nyalapape. Nyakamame piki ita mange popo pyoo, alulyamo doko kandatala, paina pyaanya pilyamona lengema.
Dokaita joo, pitamo dutupa pitaka nyakamame kandatala, Akalinya Ikiningi doko ipanya tengesa petelyamona lao masalapape.
Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Endakali indupa palelyamino dupa, kumao etala naeyataminopa, lelyo dupa pitaka pita.
Yuupi kaitipi dupa pitaka, alu pitaka doko, nambanya pii doko tanga tangapi alu napitana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Endakali mendeme Akalinya Ikiningi ipupenge gii doko masala naengema. Kaitinya enjele dupame masala naengemaka. Ikiningi dokome apata masala naengeaka. Takange dokome iki masingi.
Wamba Noa kateamo gii dokopa, endakali dupame mana minao kateaminoliaka pyoo katataminopa, Akalinya Ikiningi doko dee ipata.
Endakimi napiamopa, endakali dupame nee endakipi dupa nao, akali dupame enda lanyoo, wanaku dupa akali nyala pena lao maiyoo kateami. Dopa pyoaka kateaminopa, Noa sipi andaka kolandeamo, gii doko epea.
Dupame aipa pitape lao masala naeyao nao kateaminopa, endaki andake dokome ipupala, dokaita pitaka pyambea. Dopa piana, tanga endakali dupa dopaka pyoo katataminopa, Akalinya Ikiningi doko tanda lao ipata.
Ipatamo gii dokopa, akali lapoma eenya katatambinopa, dolaponya mende yakinatala, mende enjele dupame lanyoo patami.
Dee enda lapomame palao wasalanya, wita dii takyoo indyuu pititambinopa, dolaponya mende enjele dupame yakinatala, mende lanyoo patami.
Dopa pitamina, nyakamanya Kamongo doko andukupa ipatape lao, masala naelyaminona, kandao isoo kalyepape.
Pii dake salapape: Anda tange mendeme pake nenge akali mende, andukupa ipatape lao masala naenge dokonya, baanya anda doko kalukatamina latala, kandao isoo katenge.
Dopaka pyoo, Akalinya Ikiningi doko andukupa ipatape lao nyakama masala naelyaminona, kandao isoo kalyepape” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Kalai akali pii watao miningi, masepae singi mendeme, baanya akali andake dokonya pii seta. Baanya akali andake dokome kalai akali waka dupa isina latala, yuu tependa mendakaita patamopa, baame dokaita isoo katao pituu, nee napenge gii dokonya, nee mokosoo maiyoo katata.
Katatamopa, akali andake doko pilyetala, kalai akali dokome dopa pyoo katatamo doko kandatala, baa minao auu piseta.
Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Akali andake dokome baanya oapi dupa pitaka, kalai akali dokomeaka isakao katena lata.
Dopaka doko, kalai akali koo mendeme, baanya akali andake doko tanga waka ipata-lamona lao masetala,
baanya kalai akali yango dupa pyapapu, bia nao, kyakao paenge dupa-pipa neepi, biapi nao katatami.
Dopa pyoo katao, baanya akali andake doko naipapomo lao masoo katatamo gii mendepa, walu lao ipata.
Ipupala akali andake dokome, kalai akali koo doko pyao indyepala, Gote watao miningi mane-mane pipae, dupa-pipa katena lao, ele panda koo dokonya watao pyandata. Dokonya, nyakama ee lao yamataka lao, nenge gilyoo katatamina” Jisasame lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Gotenya isingi mate doko dapale: Gii mendepa akali mendeme, baanya enda watapae pyala ipatoo lateamopa, enda mapukae 10-pela dutupame, nyakamanya lama kaiyoo minao, kandanyemana latala malisoo peteami.
Enda dutupanya 5-pela masepae nasingi. Yangi 5-pela dutupa masepae singi.
Enda masepae nasingi dutupame, nyakamanya lama dupanya katasini tumbasetala minao peaminoaka doko, wakao kamuo namandeami.
Enda masepae singi dutupame, nyakamanya lama dutupanya katasini tumbasetala, wakao kamuo minaowaka peami.
Pupala akali enda watapae pyapenge doko, yapa naepeamosa, enda dutupa lemonguti leami.
Lemonguti latala paleaminopa, kuka andatombe dokonya, wii mende epeamo dokome, 'Akali enda watapae pyapenge doko, ae epelyamona, nyakama kandanyalapale ipupa' lea.
Dopa leamopa, enda mapukae dutupa pitaka sakatatala, nyakamanya lama dupa depa leami.
Dokopa enda masepae nasingi dutupame, enda masepae singi dutupa lamaiyoo, 'Naimanya lama datupa konjalanya pilyamona, nyakamanya katasini dupanya mendatupa dyepa' leami.
Dopa leaminopa, enda masepae singi dutupame pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, 'Katasini datupame naimapi, nyakamapi, pitaka kapa napapome-lamona, stoa andaka pupala, nyakama waka sambala pupa' leami.
Dokopa enda dutupa stoa andaka pateaminopa, enda watapae piamo akali doko epea. Epeamopa, enda depa latae peteamino dutupa, baa-pipa enda watapae dokonya, nee nalanya andaka kolandeami. Kolandateaminopa, kaitini doko paii lanyiami.
Maitakao enda mapukae masepae nasingi dutupame ipupala, 'Akali andake! Akali andake! Naimanya kaitini lumbakapoko' leami.
Dokopa baame dokaita lamaiyoo, 'Nyakama kiningi etete langilyo: Nyakama nambame nakandengena' lea.
Dopana, Akalinya Ikiningi doko andukupa ipatape lao, nyakamame masala naelyaminona, kandao isoo kalyepape,” Jisasame lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Gotenya isingi mate doko, akali mende baa yuu londati mendakaita patoo latala, baanya kalai akali dupa wii lanyetala, oapi dupa pitaka kandao isoo katekena leamo dopale.
Akali dokome baanya kalai akali dupame, mana kandengemali pyoo, kalai pyaamino lao masetala, muni mokosoo maiya. Mende 5 tausene kina maiya. Mende 2 tausene kina maiya. Mende 1 tausene kina maiya. Dopa petala baa paanya piamo dokonya pea.
Pateamopa, akali 5 tausene kina nyiamo dokome, ongopaka pao, muni dutupame minao kalai petala, dee 5 tausene kina konda pyoo nyia.
Dopaka pyoo, akali 2 tausene kina nyiamo dokome, minao kalai petala, 2 tausene kina konda pyoo nyia.
Akali 1 tausene kina nyiamo dokome, pupala baanya akali andake dokonya muni dutupa yuli pia.
Yuu gii longo pateamopa, akali andake doko dee pilyetala, muni maiyamo dutupanya baanya kalai akali dupa-pipa, pii lao wasalanya epea.
Ipateamopa, akali 5 tausene kina nyiamo dokome, 5 tausene kina dee konda pyoo minao ipupala, 'Akali Andake, embame namba 5 tausene kina diino dokonya, nambame 5 tausene kina konda pyoo nyekeona kanda' lea.
Dopa leamopa, baanya akali andake dokome baa lamaiyoo, 'Embame yaka pyekee-lamo! Emba akali epe dokomena, nambame leoli pyoo pii-lamo! Embame kalai kuki dutupa, nambame leoli pyoo auu pyoo, isii-lamo dokonya, nambame emba longo dupa isoo kata latoo. Embapa nambapa, mona setao katambana ipu' lea.
Dokopa akali 2 tausene kina nyiamo doko, apata ipupala, 'Akali Andake, embame namba 2 tausene kina diino dokonya, nambame 2 tausene kina konda pyoo nyekeona kanda' lea.
Dopa leamopa, baanya akali andake dokome baa lamaiyoo, 'Embame yaka pyekee-lamo! Emba akali epe dokomena, nambame leoli pyoo pii-lamo! Embame kalai kuki dutupa, nambame leoli pyoo auu pyoo isii-lamo dokonya, nambame emba longo dupa isoo kata latoo. Embapa nambapa mona setao katambana ipu' lea.
Dokopa akali 1 tausene kina nyiamo doko, apata ipupala, 'Akali Andake, emba akali tomba nenge, nambame kandenge. Embame wakamanya ee waingi pokatae, dupanya nee yukuo mandenge. Dee wakamanya ee waingi lyandatae, dupanya dii lyao mandengeaka.
Dopa pingi dokonya, nambame paka kaeyapala, embanya muni dutupa pao yuli piona, embame muni namba diino, dutupa datupakana kanda' lea.
Dopa leamopa, akali andake dokome baa lamaiyoo, 'Emba kalai akali koo, maka-maka kaeyapae-lamona, nambame wakamanya ee waingi pokatae, dupanya nee yukuo mandyuu, wakamanya ee waingi lyandatae dupanya, dii lyao mandengeaka-lumu doko,
nambanya muni dutupame, propeta mendatupa mandekena, beŋenya setakateno! Embame dopa pyekeeli kandao doko, nambanya muni dutupanya, wakao mendatupa apata nyipulina” lea.
Dopa latala, baanya kalai akali yangi dokaita lamaiyoo, “1 tausene kina doko nyepala, akali 10 tausene kina singi doko maiyepa.
Endakali mende-kisa longo setamo kandao doko, baa longoaka konda pyoo maita. Maitamopa, baa-kisa longoaka seta. Endakali nasingi mende-kisa, kuki setamo dutupa, baa-kisa nasina lao tange nyokonyeta.
Dopana, nyakamame kalai akali koo dake, kamalya iminjetae endakali ee lao yamataka lao, nenge gilyoo katenge dokonya, soo pyale lapa' leana” lao, Jisasame lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Tanga Akalinya Ikiningi doko, baanya tii pipae-pipa, enjele dupa pitaka-pipa, apata ipao, baanya kiŋi petenge toko dokonya pitita.
Dokopa endakali paliu pelyamo dupa pitaka, baanya enombanya nyoo kambu pyatami. Dopa pitaminopa, sipisipi setao katenge mendeme, sipisipi memepi yapao wakale pyoloo pingili pyoo, endakali dupa yapao mokoseta.
Mokosoo pituu, baame sipisipi dupa baanya kingi tolae-kaita katena lata. Meme dupa baanya kingi koeya-kaita katena lata.
Dokopa kiŋi dokome kingi tolae-kaita katatamino dokaita lamaiyoo, 'Nyakama nambanya Takangeme auu pisetae. Yuu kaitipi tee piamo dokopa, baanya moeya doko nyakama nyetamina latala, baanya isingi mate dokonya, depa lanya setekeamo doko nyala ipupa.
Wamba namba lopo kaeyopa, nyakamame namba nee diami. Endaki nanu kaeyopa, namba endaki kamuo diami. Opone joo epeopa, namba nyoo setao paleami.
Yonge pee napyoo kateopa, namba yonge pee diami. Yaina siopa, namba kandao nisiami. Anjetae paleopa, namba kanja epeamina' lata.
Dopa latamopa, endakali tolatae dupame yanu pyao, 'Akali Andake, naimame andukupa lopo kaeyenopa, emba nee diamape? Andukupa endaki nanu kaeyenopa, emba endaki kamuo diamape?
Andukupa opone joo epenopa, emba nyoo setao paleamape? Andukupa yonge pee napyoo katenopa, emba yonge pee diamape?
Andukupa yaina siinopa, emba kandao nisiamape? Andukupa anjetae palenopa, emba kanja epeamape?' latami.
Dopa lataminopa, kiŋi dokome dokaita lamaiyoo, 'Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Nambanya kaiminingi datupanya, koo kenge nasingi mende nisiamino dokome, namba nisiamiakana' lata.
“Dopa latala, baame kingi koeya-kaita katatamino dokaita lamaiyoo, 'Nyakama watao pyatae dupa namba yakinatala, Satanepi, Satanenya enjele koopi, dupanya itate konjala naenge, setakamaiyamo dokonya pupa.
Wamba lopo kaeyopa, nyakamame namba nee nandiami. Endaki nanu kaeyopa, nyakamame namba endaki kamuo nandiami.
Opone joo epeopa, nyakamame namba nyoo setao napaleami. Yonge pee napyoo kateopa, nyakamame namba yonge pee nandiami. Yaina siopa, nyakamame namba kandao nisala naeyami. Anjetae paleopa, nyakamame namba kanja naepeamina' lata.
Dopa latamopa, dokaitame yanu pyao, 'Akali Andake, andukupa emba lopo kaeyenopapi, endaki nanu kaeyenopapi, opone joo epenopapi, yonge pee napyoo katenopapi, yaina siinopapi, anjetae palenopapi, naimame kandatala, nisala naeyamape?' latami.
Dopa lataminopa, kiŋi dokome dokaita lamaiyoo, 'Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Nyakamame endakali datupanya, koo kenge nasingi mende, nisala naeyamino dokome, namba nisala naeyamiakana' latana,” Jisasame lea.
Dopa latala, Jisasame endakali pii soo kateamino dupa lamaiyoo, “Endakali kingi koeya-kaita katatamino, dokaita tanda nao, leke-leke tao, etete katatami. Dopaka doko, endakali tolatae dupa, lete etete katenge doko nyetamina,” Jisasame lea.
Jisasame pii manapi dokaita pitaka lamaiyoo etapala, baanya disaipolo dupa lamaiyoo,
“Napinya Kaeyamo Pasopa gii doko ene ipanya pimupa, yuu gii lapoma silyamo doko, nyakamame masilyamino. Gii dokopa, Akalinya Ikiningi doko poko itanya pyao yukuina lao, yanda singi dupanya kingilyaka maitana” lea.
Gii dokopaka pitisa mupapi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, dupa pitisa mupa dupanya, aiyomba Kaeyapasa lenge dokonya, andaka pii lao kambuiyami.
Kambuingi dokonya pituu, nyakamame aipa petala Jisasa waa katao, anjoo nyepala pyao kumasemape lao, kaita kutiami.
Kutapala lao pituu, “Aopyoo latala endakali dupame pyao pitamina, gii epe dokonya dopa napimana” leami.
Jisasa baa taono Betani dokonya, akali kopetali Saimone lenge dokonya andaka, nee nao petea.
Peteamopa, enda mendeme penge yakane mendenya, wele tunduma pipae, muni andake pupenge tumbatae mende minao epea. Ipupala Jisasanya aiyombanya, wele doko kaii lakamaiya.
Kaii lakamaiyamo doko kandatala, “Wele dake endakalimi sambaminopa, muni andake nyepala, endakali daa jepae dupa maipumalina, aipuma wele dake baame mee pyoo nepelyape?” lao, disaipolo dupame imbu kaeyami.
<range>
Dopa leamino doko Jisasame sepala, dokaita lamaiyoo, “Baame namba-kisa kalai epe etete mende pilyamona, aipuma nyakamame enda dakenya mona kenda pisakamailyamipi?
Endakali daa jepae dupa koteaka lao nyakama-pipa apata katatamiaka doko, namba nyakama-pipa gii longo mende, kalya naeyalamano.
Enda dakeme wele tunduma pipae, kaii lakalamo dokome, nambanya yonge doko malu pipenge dokonya depa lasoo pyakalamo.
Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Yuu dupa pitakanya, wai pii epe doko lao taeyatamino gii dokopa, enda dakeme pilyamo dupa apata masina lao, taeyatamina” lea.
Judasa Iskariota lenge doko, 12 disaipolo dutupanya mende, baa pitisa mupa dupa kateamisa pupala,
dokaita tipa pyoo, “Nambame Jisasa nyakama laitaka pitoo, nyakamame namba aki mende ditamipi?” lea. Dopa leamopa, dokaitame baa silipa muni 30 maiyami.
Gii dokopa pituu, Judasame pitisa dokaita Jisasa laitaka pyaanya, kaitini kutia.
Israele tange dupame betesa yisa napalenge nengema, yuu gii tee pyao dokonya, disaipolo dupame Jisasa kateasa ipupala baa lamaiyoo, “Napinya Kaeyamo Pasopa nee doko, naimame anja depa lamape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame Jerusalema pupala, akali mende kanjaminona, doko lamaiyoo, 'Mana Lenge Akali dokome, baanya gii doko tengesa petelyamona, Napinya Kaeyamo Pasopa nee doko, baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa, embanya andaka natoo lalamona' lao lamaiyepape” lea.
Dokopa disaipolo dupame Jisasame leamoli pyoo, nee akipi depa leami.
Yuu kuiyala peamopa, Jisasa baanya 12 disaipolo dutupa-pipa, nee nao peteami.
Nee nao pituu, baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Nyakamanya mendeme, namba enge nyipumu dokome, namba pyao kumasepenge akali dupa laitaka pyaapomona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, nyakama mona etete kenda kaeyapala, baa tipa pyoo, “Kamongo, doko namba kandao leepe?” lao laa-laa peami.
Dopa leaminopa Jisasame yanu pyao, “Nee disanya poeyanyoo nao, apata pilyamano dakenya mendeme, dopa pyaapomo.
Akalinya Ikiningi doko kumatana lao, pepa pyapae singi dokonya, dopaka pita-lamo. Dopaka doko, akali enge nyetamo doko, koeyata-lamo. Endangimi baa namandeali, doko yaka jialina” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasa enge nyiamo akali Judasa dokome, baa lamaiyoo, “Mana Lenge Akali, embame leeno doko, namba lao leepe?” lea. Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Emba tangeme leleno dokoakana” lea.
Nyakama nee nao pituu, Jisasame betesa mende nyepala, Gote lao yaka pilino latala konjia. Konjepala baanya disaipolo dupa maiyoo pituu, “Dake nambanya yonge dokona, nyoo nalapa” lea.
Dopa latala baame kapo waene peteta mende nyepala, Gote lao yaka pilino latala, dokaita maiyoo pituu, “Nambanya taiyoko kaii lelyo dakeme, endakali longo dupa pitakanya, koo dupa kunao nepao, Goteme pii enenge mende lao setekelyamona, nyakama pitakame nyoo nalapa.
<range>
Nambame nyakama langilyo: Namba dee waene nala naeyaowaka katao, tanga nambanya Takangenya isingi mate dokonya, waene enenge doko nyakama-pipa apata natamana” lea.
Dopa lateamopa, dokaitame wee mende latala, kamaka pyakalyetala, Olipimanda peami.
Dokopa Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Goteme dapa lea: 'Sipisipi setao katenge doko pyatopa, sipisipi dupa wakale saa latamina' lao, pii pepa pyapae silyamo. Lapae silyamoliaka pyoo, indupa kuka gii dakepa, kenda pipae namba-kisa ipatamo kandatala, nyakama pitakame namba soo yakinalamino.
Dopaka doko, Goteme namba dee sakatasetatamopa, nyakama Galilea paa naeyataminopa, namba wambao patona” lea.
Dokopa Pitame Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Disaipolo dupa pitakame emba soo yakinatala pataminopa, nambame emba yakinala naeyatona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Nambame emba kiningi langilyo: Indupa kuka gii dakenya, yaka pauli pii ene laanya pitamopa, paa tepomasa embame namba nakandengena laapenona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Pitame baa lamaiyoo, “Nambame emba yakinala naeyato. Emba kumateno dokonya namba apataka kumatambana” lea. Dokopa disaipolo yangi dupa pitakame dopaka leami.
Dopa lateaminopa, Jisasa baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa, Gesemani ee dokonya peami. Pupala baame dupa lamaiyoo, “Namba omosale loma sala pelyona, nyakama asa pilyepa” lea.
Dokopa Jisasa baa mona kenda kaeyapala, Pitapi, Sebedi ikiningi dolapopi laminao umbisale pea.
Pupala dutupa lamaiyoo, “Nambanya mona doko etete kenda pipaeme putukupala, kumapenge julumuna, nyakama asa kandao katamana kalyepape” lea.
Dopa latala baa kuki umbisale pao, yuunya tombauli sepala, loma soo pituu, “Apane, embame namba-kisa kenda pipae silyamo dake, nyoo nepakapenge jia kandeno doko, nyoo nepakape. Embame namba-kisa kenda pipae silyamo dake, nyoo nepaka lapuliaka doko, nambame masilyo dokonya-kaita napipi. Embame masilino dokonya-kaita pipi” lea.
Dopa lao loma sepala ipao kandeamopa, disaipolo dutupa luu palyasiamisa, baame Pita lamaiyoo, “Nyakama aipuma namba-pipa, awa mendai iki dokonya kandao isoo nakatalamipi?
Kiningi etete, nyakamanya moname pyuani kaeyapumupa, yongeme papa tambulyamona, makande pingi dupanya nyakama pao koeyatamina, loma soo kandao isoo kalyepape” lea.
Dopa latala Jisasa paa lapo pyoo loma sala pea. Loma soo pituu, “Apane, kenda pipae epelyamo dake, namba-kisa epena lao kaeya kandeno doko, embame masilino dokonya-kaita pipi” lea.
Loma sepala dee ipao kandeamopa, disaipolo dutupa lemonguti kaeyapala, luu paliu siami.
Paliu sina latala, baa paa tepo pyoo loma sala pea. Pupala wamba loma siamo dutupaka sia.
Loma sepala dee ipao disaipolo dutupa lamaiyoo, “Nyakama mee luaka paliu silyamipi? Namba enge nyipumu akali doko ipatelyamo. Akalinya Ikiningi doko, koo pingi endakali dupa laitaka pyaapomo, gii doko ipatelyamona, mona sakatalapa” lea.
<range>
Jisasame dopa lao kateamopa, baanya 12 disaipolo dutupanya mende, Judasa lenge doko epea. Epeamo dokonya, endakali kambu andake mende, konja-wua, kolyepepi dupa minao, baa apata epeami. Dupa pitisa mupapi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, dupame pena leaminosa epeami.
Jisasa enge nyiamo akali dokome, wambao endakali kambu doko lamaiyoo, “Nambame akali mende nunu pitu dokona, nyakamame baa minatala anjalapape” lea.
Dopa lamaitala ipao baa Jisasa kateasa tolao pupala, “Mana Lenge Akali, kuakama!” lea. Dopa latala baa nunu pia.
Dopa piamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Kaimia, embame pyaanya epeno doko pipoko” lea. Dokopa endakali kambu dokome, Jisasa minatala anjiami.
Anjeteaminopa, Jisasa-pipa apata kateamino dupanya mendeme, baanya konja-wua doko kolanyetala, pitisa mupa dupanya aiyomba dokonya, kalai akali mendenya kale lyanya nepea.
Dopa piamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Embanya konja-wua doko palenge andanda dokonya, mandi. Konja-wua miningi dupa, konja-wuameaka kumingi.
Nambame nambanya Takangeme, namba nisina lao wii lalu pipupa, baame enjele 72 tausenepi mende, epena lapyalina lao masala naelepe?
