Namba nisina lapuli doko, kenda pipae dake namba-kisa, dopa pyoo ipupengena lao, pii pepa pyapae singi doko dii manja naeyapyalina,” Jisasame lea.
Dopa latala, baame endakali kambu doko lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame pake nenge mende, anjala epele lao konja-wuapi, kolyepepi, dupa minao namba anjala epelyamipi? Nambame koteaka lao lotuu anda andake dokonya, endakali dupa mana lamaiyoo kateo dokopa, nyakamame namba anjala naeyami.
Dopaka doko, wamba propeta dupame pii pepa piami dupa, angi jina lao, dutupa pitaka pilyamona” lea. Dokopa disaipolo dupa pitakame Jisasa yakinatala, paka pyakao peami.
Dokopa Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, dupa pitisa mupa Kaeyapasa kateasa ipao kambu piami. Kambu piamino dokonya, Jisasa anjoo laminao epeami.
Dokopa Pita waa katao, maitanya Jisasa watao pea. Pupala pitisa mupa dupanya aiyomba dokonya, anda kamapusa kolamatala, aipa pilyamipi lao kandatoo latala, yanda singi dupa-pipa petea.
Pitisa mupapi, kanjole kambuingi andake dokomepi, Jisasa pyao kumasemana latala, akali mendapuame baa-kisa sambo pii setao, kote lena lao kutiami.
Dokopa akali longo ipupala, Jisasa-kisa sambo pii setao, kote leami. Dopa leaminoaka doko, baa pyao kumasepenge tenge mende kandao nanyiami. Etao dokonya, akali lapoma ipupala
lao pituu, “Akali dakeme, 'Gotenya lotuu anda andake doko, kapa pao lakyepala, yuu gii teponya pituna' leana” leambi.
Dokopa pitisa mupa dupanya, aiyomba dokome toeya katapala Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Pii emba-kisa tenge setao lelyambino dake, aipuma yanu napilipi?” lea.
Dopa leamoaka doko, Jisasa ema napia. Dopa piamosa, pitisa mupa dupanya aiyomba dokome, dee baa lamaiyoo, “Gote saka katenge dokome kandao kalyamona, embame pii tolao kiningi doko naima langi. Emba Gote Ikiningi, Kraisa dokope?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Embame leleno dokoakana, nambame nyakama dapa langilyo: Akalinya Ikiningi doko, Gote etete pupu lapae dokonya kingi tolae dokonya pituu, tanga kaitinya kopa tambe-tambe ipatamopa, nyakamame kandatamina” lea.
Dopa leamo sepala, pitisa mupa dupanya aiyomba dokome, baa tangenya yonge pee dupa minao lapyepala, lao pituu, “Baame Gote lamba lao pii lelyamo doko, nyakamame sepelyamino. Aipuma endakali mendapuanya pii deaka nyemanape?
Nyakamame aipa pimana lao masilyamipi?” lea. Dopa leamopa dupame, “Baa pyao kumasepengena” leami.
Dopa latala, baanya lengelyapinya sopokalimi pyapa, kimiame pyapa piami. Dee mendapuame baa kingi kapame pyao pituu,
“Emba kini propeta-tamo doko, emba akali dokome pyalumu lao naima langi” leami.
Pita anda kamapusa peteamopa, pitisa mupa dupanya aiyomba dokonya, kalai pyakamaiyoo petenge wanaku mendeme ipupala, baa lamaiyoo, “Emba Galilea tange Jisasa dokopa apata katengembana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Pitame endakali kateamino dupanya enombanya tanga lao, “Embame leleno doko namba nakandengena” lea.
Dopa latala baa lome kambusa peamopa, kalai wanaku waka mendeme kandatala, endakali dosa kateamino dupa lamaiyoo, “Akali dake Nasarete tange Jisasa dokopa, apata katengembana” lea.
Dokopa Pitame deaka tanga lao, “Goteme namba kandao katamupa lelyo. Akali leeno doko nakandenge daana” lea.
Gii kuki pateamopa, akali dosa kateamino dupame ipupala, Pita kandao, “Embanya pii dokome panalumuna, kiningi etete emba akali dupanya mendeaka-lamona” leami.
Dopa lateaminopa, Pitame lao pituu, “Namba akali doko nakandengena, sambo lato doko, Goteme namba pinana” lea. Dopa lalu piamopa, yaka pauli pii mende lea.
“Yaka pauli pii ene laanya pitamopa, embame paa tepomasa, namba nakandengena laapenona,” Jisasame leamo dutupa masetala, Pita kamaka pyakalyetala, putukuo ee lea.
Oo yongama wamba, pitisa mupapi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, dupa pitakame Jisasa pyao kumasemana latala, lao kambuiyami.
Dopa petala dupame Jisasa anjetala, laminao pao, Gapena Pondiasa Pailate maiyami.
Jisasa pyao kumasemana leamino doko kandatala, Jisasa enge nyiamo akali Judasa doko mona kenda kaeyapala, silipa muni 30 nyiamo dutupa minao pupala, pitisa mupapi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, dupa tange maiyakamaiya.
Maiyakamaiyoo pituu, “Akali tenge nakatenge mende, nambame enge nyipu doko, nambame kopeta pipu-lamona” lea. Dopa lamaiyamopa dokaitame, “Doko embanya kalai. Naimanya kalai mende daana” leami.
Dokopa Judasame muni dutupa, lotuu anda andake dokonya kainanya pyale latala pea. Pupala baa tange mangenya kende katatala, yukutae katao kumia.
Pitisa mupa dupame silipa muni dutupa yapao nyepala, “Endakali pyao kumasalanya muni datupame, enge nyepae dokonya, lotuu anda andakenya muni singi dokonya, setala naeyapengena” leami.
Dokonya dupame pii lao yaki petala, endakali waka kumatami dupa malu pipengena lao, akali yuumi endaki penge wasingi dokonya, yuu doko muni dutupame sambeami.
Tenge dokonya, yuu sambeamino doko kenge Taiyokosa lengema.
Dopa piamino dokome, wamba propeta Jeremaeyame lao pituu, “Israele tange dupame, akali mendai silipa muni 30 dutupame, sambao nyepengena lao, makande miniamino dutupa nyetami. Nyepala Kamongo dokome namba langiamoli pyoo, akali yuumi endaki penge wasingi dokonya, yuu doko sambatamina” leamo doko, angi jia.
<range>
Jisasa baa Gapena Pondiasa Pailatenya, enombanya laminao pao katasiaminopa, Pailateme baa tipa pyoo, “Emba Judamanya Kiŋi dokope?” lea. Dokopa Jisasame, “Embame leleno dokoaka” lea.
Dokopa pitisa mupapi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, dupame baa-kisa tenge seteaminopa, baa ema napia.
Dopa piamopa, Pailateme baa lamaiyoo, “Emba-kisa tenge longo setao, pii lelyamino dupa embame nasilipi?” lea.
Dokopa Jisasame pii leamino, dupanya mendaipi mende yanu pyala naeyamosa, gapena doko etete paka kaeya.
Ee kana dii lao, Napinya Kaeyamo Pasopa gii doko epelyamoli pyoo, Pailateme akali anjetae dupanya mende, endakali dupame mokekena lelyamili pyoo, mokata pyakamaingi.
Gii dokopa akali Barabasa lenge mende, pundunya kenge singi doko anjetae palea.
Pitisa mupa dupame Jisasa-pipa tilya nyepala, baa anjoo dimini-lamo lao kandatala, Pailateme endakali kambu kateamino dupa tipa pyoo, “Nambame api mokakaowape? Barabasape, pande Jisasa Kraisa lengema dokope?” lea.
<range>
Pailateme disisene pyaanya peteamopa, baanya etanengeme, “Nambame kuakama akali tolatae dokonya, kombea koo mende pyoona, embame baa mende napipi” lanya pea.
Dokopa pitisa mupapi, Judamanya isingi akalipi dupame, “Barabasa mokekena, Jisasa pyao kumasina lapape,” lao endakali kambu dupa, ingi tuu leami.
Dopa piaminopa, Pailateme endakali kambu dupa deaka tipa pyoo, “Nambame akali lapoma dolaponya, anduku nyakamanya mokakapili lao masilyamipi?” lea. Dopa leamopa, dokaitame yanu pyao, “Barabasana” leami.
Dokopa Pailateme dokaita lamaiyoo, “Dopa-tamo doko, nambame Jisasa Kraisa lengema doko, aipa pyuape?” lea. Dopa leamopa dokaitame, “Poko itanya pyao yuku!” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Baame koo aki mende pipyape?” lea. Dopa leamopa, dokaitame eteteaka puu lao, “Baa pyao yuku!” leami.
Pyao yuku leamino dokome, pundu andake mende sakatatamopa, Pailateme mende pyaa naeyalapo-lamo lao kandea. Kandatala baame endakali kambu dokonya enombanya, kingi wasa pyao pituu, “Akali dakenya taiyoko doko, namba-kisa nakatenana, nyakama tange-kisa katena peekelyona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, endakali dupa pitakame, “Baanya taiyoko doko naimapi, naimanya wanepi, dupa-kisa sina kaeya!” leami.
Dokopa Pailateme Barabasa mokatala, Jisasa konjame pyapala, pyao yukuina lao yanda singi dupa maiya.
Dokopa gapenanya yanda singi dupame, Jisasa lanyoo gapomane anda kamapu dokonya pyakamatala, yanda singi waka dupa lanyoo ipao kambu piami.
Dopa petala dupame baanya yonge pee dupa, lyokao nyepala, kiŋinya yonge pee kala pepola jepae mende, baanya pyakamaiyami.
Dee kende nenge-nenge katapae mende nyoo, makipu petala, Jisasanya aiyombanya pisetala, kiŋinya pangali jepae mende, baanya kingi tolae-kaita minasiami. Dopa petala baa lamba lao, luma lakao, mambo pyao, “Judamanya Kiŋi, emba auu pyoo katape!” leami.
Dopa latala dupame baa sopokalimi pyapa, keoo konjame aiyombanya pyapa piami.
Dopa pyoo etapala, yonge pee wamba pyakamaiyamino doko lyokao nyepala, baanya pingi dupa pyakamaiyami. Dopa petala, baa pyao yukulanya laminao peami.
Kamaka pyakalyiaminopa, akali Sairini tange Saimone lenge mende kandanyetala, yanda singi dupame baa pyalanya latala, Jisasanya poko ita doko nyoo sakamaina leami.
Sina latala, yuu manda kenge Gologota lenge dokonya pao pyakalyiami. (Manda Gologota dokonya tenge doko, “Matena Kuli.”)
Gologota pyakalyetala, yanda singi dupame baa tanda kaeyala naena lao, waene matasini-pipa wasepala maiyaminopa, baame nao sepala, nanenya kaeya.
Dokopa yanda singi dupame baa poko itanya pyao yukuiyami. Yukutala baanya yonge pee wamba lyokeamino dupa setapala, yanda singi dupame apimi yonge pee dupanya mende, nyilyape kandamana latala lakii piami.
Dopa petala dupame Jisasa kandatae peteami.
Jisasa-kisa tenge seteamino pii doko, “Dake Jisasa, Judamanya Kiŋi dokona” lao pepa pyatae, doko poko ita ketae dokonya yukuiyami.
Dokopa akali pake nenge lapoma, Jisasa-pipa apata pyao yukuiyami. Mende doko baanya kingi tolae-kaita yukuiyami. Mende doko baanya kingi koeya-kaita yukuiyami.
Jisasa pyao yukutae kateamo dokonya-kaita, endakali paeyamino dupame, baa lamba lao, aiyomba wangatoto pyoo,
“Embame lotuu anda andake doko lakyepala, yuu gii teponya waka mende pituna leeno dokae! Emba Gotenya Ikiningi-tamo doko, emba tange pyoo nyoo, poko ita doko yakinatala, isa ipu” leami.
Mendai dopaka pyoo, pitisa mupapi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, dupame Jisasa lamba lao,
“Baame endakali waka dupa pyoo nyipumuaka doko, baa tange kapa pao pyoo nyala naenge-lamo. Baa Israelemanya Kiŋi daape, epapu poko ita doko yakinatala, isa epena kaeya. Yakinatamo doko, naimame baa lao masoo minamanalena” leami.
Baa Gotenya Ikiningina latala, Gote tungi pingi daape. Goteme baa nea kaeyatamo doko, epapu baa pyoo nyina kaeya” leami.
Akali pake nenge baa-pipa, apata pyao yukutae kateambino dolapome, mendai dopaka pyoo, baa-kisa lamba pii kando piambi.
Jisasa yukutae kateamopaka, 12 kilokonya pituu yuu kuiya. Kuiyamo doko, kuiyataeyaka katao pao, 3 kilokonya tuu lea.
Dokopa Jisasame etete puu lao wii lao, “Ilai, Ilai, lema sabatani?” lea. (Pii dokonya tenge doko, “Nambanya Gote, nambanya Gote, embame namba aipuma yakinelepe?”)
Dopa leamo doko endakali dosa kateamino dupanya, mendapuame sepala, “Ilaija lao wii lelyamona, salapape” leami.
Dopa lateaminopa, akali mendeme alo pyao pao, koma jepae mende itakulimi tuku petala, waene kaa pipae mendenya poeyanyetala, Jisasa nena lao makapusakamaiya.
Endakali yangi dupame lao pituu, “Ilaijame baa pyoo nyala epelyape lao kandamana, kaeyalapa” leami.
Dokopa Jisasame eteteaka puu lao ae latala, baa kumia.
Dokopa lotuu anda andake dokonya, lapalapa andake mendeme, nee nyetae katenge panda dokonya, kame pinyetae katenge doko, ketae pituu titi pyao, isa tuu latala lapo pyoloo pia. Dopa piamopa, yuu doko titiwali minao, kana yale dupa pukutala, saa laloo pia.
Endakali malu dupa pukuloo petala lumbiamopa, Gotenya endakali kumapae malu petae kateamino, longo dupa sakatasia.
Sakataseteamopa, nyakamanya malu dupa yakineami. Maitakao Jisasa sakateamo dokopa, nyakama Jerusalema peaminopa, endakali longo dupame kandeami.
Yanda singi isingi akali dokopi, baa-pipa apata Jisasa isoo kateamino dupapimi, titiwali miniapi, waka tata longo mendapu piamo dupa pitaka, kandao etete paka kaeyapala, “Kiningi etete, akali dake Gote Ikiningi-lamona” leami.
Maria Magadala tange dokopi, Jemesa Jonepanya endangi Mariapi, dee enda longo waka mendapu, Galilea pituu Jisasa nisoo apata epeamino, dupame kuki tependale pituu, piamo dupa kandatae peteami.
<range>
Yuu kuiyalanya piamopa, akali Arimatia tange kamongo Josepe lenge, Jisasa watao paenge dokome,
Pailate peteasa pupala, Jisasanya yonge doko dina lao tee lea. Dopa leamopa, yanda singi dupame kondao nyoo maina lea.
Dokopa Josepeme Jisasanya yonge doko nyoo, lapalapa kyeto epe mendeme, yaki-yaki petala,
Josepeme baa tange malu pitamina lao, kananda enenge tumbinya seteamo dokonya, Jisasanya yonge doko nyoo setea. Setapala, kana andake mendeme kapilya mina-mina pyoo, malu kambu doko piti petala, baa pea.
Dopa piamopa, Maria Magadala tange dokopa, Jemesa Jonepanya endangi Mariapame, malu dokonya yangitena pituu, kandatae peteambi.
Oo yongama Sambata gii epeamopa, pitisa mupapi, Parasaipi, dupame Pailate kanja peami.
Pupala baa lamaiyoo, “Akali andake, akali sambo lenge dokome saka katao pituu, baa yuu gii tepo dokonya, sakatatona leamo doko naimame masilyamano.
Dopa leana, baanya disaipolo dupame pao, baanya yonge doko waa katao nyoo yalo petala, endakali dupa lamaiyoo, baa sakatapyana latamino dokome, endakali dupa eteteaka kyakasetamina, malu doko isokondape pyoo, isoo katao, yuu gii tepo dokonya tuu lena lape.
Dopa leaminopa, Pailateme dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame yanda singi mendatupa lanyoo pupala, malu doko isokondape pyoo isoo katena lapape” lea.
Dokopa dupame pupala, malu doko piamili petae kalyape lao kandatamana latala, kongali pinya kateami. Dopa petala yanda singi dupame isokondape pyoo, isoo katena leami.
Sambata gii doko pateamopa, yuu yongalanya piamopa, Maria Magadala tange dokopa, Jemesa Jonepanya endangi Mariapame malu doko, kanja peambi.
Gii dokopa titiwali andake mende minatala, Kamongonya enjele mende, kaiti-kisa katao isa ipupala, kana doko kapilya mina-mina pyoo nyoo kapya latala, dokonya ketae petea.
Baanya lengelyapi doko yuu-wapaka pingili pia. Dee baanya yonge pee doko, etete kyoo lao pole-pole pia.
Dopa piamo kandatala, yanda singi malu isetae kateamino dupa, walu lao paka kaeyami dokome, kumapae joo lombapae siami.
Dokopa enjele dokome enda dolapo lamaiyoo, “Nyakambame Jisasa pyao yukuiyamino doko, kutilyambino lao nambame masilyona, paka nakaeyalapape.
Wamba baa sakatato leamoli pyoo sakatatalamona, seteamino panda dakenya nasilyamona, kanja ipupa.
Kandatala nyakamba baanya disaipolo dupa katatamisa, yapa pupala, baa malunya sakatatala, Galilea wambao pelyamona, nyakamame dokonya pao kanjaminona, lamaiyapale lao, langya epona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, enda dolapo paka kaeyambinoaka doko, auu kaeyapaeme tumbiamopa, malu doko yapa yakinatala, alo pyao disaipolo dupa lamaiya peambi.
Alo pyao peambinopa, Jisasame kaitinisa kandanyetala, “Wanalapo, yongama etete!” lea. Dokopa dolapome pao, Jisasa mokonya kopetala mambo piambi.
Dopa piambinopa, Jisasame enda dolapo lamaiyoo, “Nyakamba paka nakaenya, nambanya kaiminingi dupa katatamisa pupala, Galilea pena lamaiyepape. Dupame dokonya namba kanjaminona” lea.
Enda dolapo peambinopa, malu isetae kateamino yanda singi dupanya mendapuame, taono dokonya pupala, piamo dupa pitaka pitisa mupa dupa lamaiyami.
Dokopa pitisa mupapi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, dupame pii wasoo nyepala, yanda singi dupa muni longo mendapu maiyami.
Maitala pii dapa lena lamaiyami: “Nyakama luu palipumanopa, Jisasanya disaipolo dupa kuka ipupala, baanya yonge doko nyoo pamini-lamona lapape” leami.
Gapena dokome pii dake setamopa, naimame baa pii auu kaena lao lamaitamanopa, nyakama-kisa pundu mende naipapomona” leami.
Dopa lateaminopa, yanda singi dupame muni dutupa nyepala, lena leaminoliaka pyoo, lao taeyami. Pii doko lao Juda dupa-kisa taeyapae siamo doko, enepapupi dopaka pyoo taeyapae silyamo.
Disaipolo 11-pela dutupa, Galilea pupala, wamba Jisasame manda mendenya pena leamo dokonya peami.
Dokonya pao Jisasa kandatala, baanya kenge minalyoo mambo piami. Dopa piaminoaka doko, mendapuame mona lapo paleami.
Dokopa Jisasa nyakama kateamisa ipupala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Yuupi kaitipi dupa pitaka isepe lao, Goteme pupu lapae doko namba ditiana,
nyakama pupala, akali tata paliu pelyamo dupa pitaka, nambanya disaipolo jina lao pii lamaiyepape. Pii lamaiyoo pituu, Takange dokopi, Ikiningi dokopi, Oli Spirit dokopi, dutupanya kenge doko lao, kaimbu pyakamaiyepape.
Nambame pii manapi langio dupa pitaka, minina lao mana lamaiyepape. Namba nyakama-pipa apataka katao pao, yuu etatamo gii doko nyetamana,” Jisasame lea.
Gote Ikiningi Jisasa Kraisanya wai pii epe doko dapa pyoo tee pia.
Propeta Aisaiyanya buku dokonya Goteme leamoli pyoo, dapa lao pepa pyapae singi: “Salapape! Nambame nambanya wai akali doko wambao pena latopa, baame Mesaeya dokonya kaitini doko depa lakamaita.
Akali dokome endakali napalenge yuu mendenya katapala, wii lao katata. Baame wii lao, 'Kamongonya kaitini doko depa lakamaiyepape. Kaitini koeyapae dupa tolasakamaiyepape' lao katata.”
Goteme leamoli pyoo, Jone kaimbu pingi doko endakali napalenge yuu dokonya ipao katapala, “Nyakama mona kapilyetala, kaimbu nyalapa. Dopa pitaminopa, Goteme nyakamanya koo dupa kunao nepekena” lao katea.
Dopa piamopa, Judia tangepi, Jerusalema tangepi, longo dupa baa kateamo dokonya pii sala peami. Pupala nyakamanya koo dupa lao panata piaminopa, baame endaki Jodane dokonya kaimbu pyata pyakamaiya.
Jone baa yonge pee kamele itimi wasepaepi, matapu bulumakao yanungimi wasepaepi, dupa pyoo katea. Baa paiyombapi, ambulya kakasa lyingipi, dupa nao katea.
Baame endakali dupa lamaiyoo, “Akali maitapyao epelyamo dokonya pupu lapae dokome namba ita minao. Nambame luma lakapala, baanya moko pee kende tata lakamaiyanya, namba epe daa.
Nambame endakimi nyakama kaimbu pyekelyona, baame Oli Spirit dokome kaimbu pyakatana” lea.
Gii dokopa, Jisasa baa yuu Galilea, taono Nasarete katao epeamopa, endaki Jodane dokonya Joneme Jisasanya kaimbu pyakamaiya.
Jisasa kaimbu nyepala, endaki ketae pyakalyiamopa, kaiti saa papa laloo petala, Oli Spirit doko yaka maiyolee joo, lanao ipao baa-kisa petea.
Dokopa kaiti-kisa katao pii mende lea dokome lao pituu, “Emba nambanya Ikiningi mona setenge doko. Namba tange emba etete auu kaengena” lea.
Dokopa endakali napalenge yuu mendasa, Oli Spirit dokome Jisasa lanyoo pea.
Pao mena yanapi kapu katengema yuu dokonya yuu gii 40 kateamopa, Sataneme baa minao makande pia. Dokopa, enjele dupame ipao baa nisiami.
Jone kaimbu pingi doko anjeteaminopa, Jisasa Galilea pupala, Gotenya wai pii epe doko lamaiyoo katea.
Baame lao pituu, “Goteme wamba gii seteamo doko indupa ipao palipilyamo. Gotenya isingi mate doko tengesa ipatelyamona, nyakama mona kapilyetala, wai pii epe doko masoo minalapa” lea.
Jisasa Galilea pete lemba dokonya pao kandeamopa, pisa nyingi akali Saimonepa, kaiminingi Andruapame umbene nuu mende endaki pete dokonya pyandao pisa nyoo kateambi.
Jisasame dolapo lamaiyoo, “Nyakambame pisa nyingimbali pyoo, endakali nyalapale mana langitoo, namba watao ipupa” lea.
Gii dokopaka akali dolapome umbene nuu dupa yakinatala, baa watao peambi.
Umbisale pateaminopa, Jisasame akali Sebedi ikiningi Jemesa, Jonepa sipi andaka umbene nuu tambuo peteambino kandea.
Kandatala baame dolapo epena lea. Dopa leamopa, nyakambanya takange Sebedi, kalai akali dupa-pipa sipi dokonya yakinatala, Jisasa watao peambi.
Jisasame akali kitomende dutupa-pipa pao Kapename pyakameami. Pyakamatala Sambata gii dokonya Judamanya lotuu anda dokonya kolandatala, Jisasame endakali dupa mana lea.
Baame mana leamo doko, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali dupame mana lengemali pyoo laa naeya. Baa-kisa pupu lapae singi joo mana leamosa, endakali dupame sepala, paka kaeyao walu leami.
Gii dokopa, akali imambu koo paleta mende peteamo dokome wii lao,
“Nasarete tange Jisasa, emba Gotenya akali anali latae doko nambame kandengena, embame naima aipa pyaa epepe? Naima minao koeyasalanya epepe?” lea.
Dokopa Jisasame baa pyalanya lao, “Embame embanya nengekaita lyokatala, akali dake yakinatala puu!” lea.
Dopa leamopa, imambu koo dokome akali doko minao walu lasetala, ae andake mende lao akali doko yakinatala pea.
Peamo kandatala, endakali dupa pitaka etete paka kaeyao walu latala, mende lamai-lamai pyoo, “Dake aipa pilyape? Dake mana waka pupu lapae singi mende-lamo! Baame imambu koo dupame mende pina lelyamopa, lelyali pingima-lamona” leami.
Dokopa yuu Galilea dokonya Jisasame piamo dupa pupae lao taeyami.
Jisasa, Jemesa, Jonepi, dutupa Judamanya lotuu anda doko yakinatala, Saimonepa, Andruapanya andaka apata peami.
Pao pyakamalu piaminopa, Saimonenya enda imange doko yonge itaita pimupa, yaina silyamona lao Jisasa lamaiyami.
Lamaitiaminopa, enda doko siamo dokonya pupala, Jisasame baanya kinginya minatala sakatasia. Dokopa yonge itaita piamo doko mee jeteamopa, enda dokome dokaita nee nyoo, nena lao maiya.
Niki landa piamopa, endakali mendapuame yaina pyapaepi, imambu koo paletapi, dupa laminao baa kateasa epeami.
Endakali taono tange dupa pitaka anda kambu dokonya kapatae kateami.
Endakali yaina tata longome pyapae dupa baame mee jakamaiya. Dee baame imambu koo longo dupa watao pyakamaiyaka. Imambu koo dupame baa kandengema dokonyana, dupame pii laa naena daa lea.
Yuu ene yongalanya piamopa, Jisasa sakatao, endakali napalenge yuu mendenya pupala, dokonya loma soo katea.
Kateamopa, Saimonepi, endakali apata kateamino dupame baa kutao peami.
Pao kandatala baa lamaiyoo, “Endakali pitakame emba kutilyaminona” leami.
Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nambame endakali dupa pitaka wai pii epe doko lamaipenge, tenge dokonya epeona, taono yakane tengesa silyamo dokaitanya apata pii lamaitoo mua” lea.
Dopa latala baame Galilea yuu doko pitakanya pao, Judamanya lotuu anda dupanya pii lamaiyoo, imambu koo dupa watao pyakamaiyaka.
Akali kopetali mende Jisasa kateasa ipao luma lakapala, baame kyeto joo lamaiyoo, “Embame nambanya yaina dake mee jakalapo lao maseteno doko, mee jakalapenona” lea.
Dokopa Jisasame akali doko kondo kaeyapala, kingimi watandatala baa lamaiyoo, “Nambame embanya yaina doko mee jipyali lao masilyona, epapu embanya yaina doko mee jekelyona” lea.
Dopa lalu piamopa, akali dokonya kopetali yaina doko mee jia.
Dokopa Jisasame kyeto joo baa lamaiyoo, “Nambame embanya pyakalo doko mende lamaiya naenya, pitisa dokome emba kandena puu. Pupala Mosesame wamba mana seteamoli pyoo, dopale mende Gote kundi maitinopa, endakali dupame embanya yaina doko mee jipya-lamo lao kandenana” lea.
<range>
Jisasame dopa leamoaka doko, akali dokome pupala, piamo dupa lao taeya. Dopa piamo dokonya, Jisasa taono mendenya panao napenya, endakali napalenge yuu dupanya katea. Kateamopa, endakali dupa yuu pitakanya katao baa kateasa epeami.
Gii mendatupa pateamopa, Jisasa baa Kapename pilyia. Pilyeteamopa, baa andaka kalyamo lapae doko siami.
Sepala endakali longo dupa ipao, andaka kamandapi tumbiaminosa, panda nasia. Dokopa Jisasame dokaita wai pii epe doko lamaiyoo kateamopa,
akali kitomendeme akali papa tambutae mende soo epeami.
Ipatala kandeaminopa, endakali tumbia dokome, kolandapenge nanjiamosa, akali doko soo anda ketae pyakalyiami. Pyakalyetala, anda yame pyatae dokonya kaina dosa lopao kapya leami. Dopa petala, lapa toko dokonya kende katatala, lanao pyandeami.
Dokopa akali dokaitame baa tungi pilyamino lao kandatala, Jisasame akali papa tambutae doko lamaiyoo, “Wane, embanya koo dupa kunao nepekelyona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali mendapu peteamino dupame nyakamanya mona andaka masoo pituu,
“Akali dakeme aipuma Gote lamba lao dopa lelyape? Endakali mendeme koo dupa kunao nepala naenge. Goteme iki koo dupa kunao nepengena” lao masiami.
Masiamino dupa Jisasame kandatala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Aipuma nyakamame dopa lao masilyamipi?
Akali dakenya koo dupa kunao nepakamailyona lapu dokopa, nambame koo kunao nepenge pupu lapae doko singi-lamo lao nyakamame nakandelyamino. Dee akali dake lamaiyoo, emba sakatatala, embanya lapa toko doko nyoo soo, puu lato dokopa, nambame koo kunao nepenge pupu lapae doko singi-lamo lao kanjamino.
Dopaka doko, Akalinya Ikiningi dokome isa yuu dakenya katao, endakali dupanya koo dupa kunao nepenge pupu lapae doko baa-kisa singi-lamo lao kanjepalena” lea. Dopa latala baame akali papa tambutae doko lamaiyoo,
“Emba sakata. Sakatatala embanya lapa toko doko nyoo soo, andaka puu lelyona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, akali doko pupae sakatatala, endakali dupanya enombanya lapa toko doko nyoo soo, kamanda pea. Peamopa, endakali dupame kandatala, paka kaeyao walu lapala, Gote mambo pyao, “Wamba naimame dapale mende nakandeamana” leami.
Jisasa baa Galilea pete lemba dokonya deaka pea. Dokopa endakali kambu andake mende baa kateamo dokonya epeaminopa, dokaita mana lamaiya.
Lamaitala baa kaita pao pituu, Alopiasa ikiningi Lipai takisa nyingi anda dokonya peteamo kandatala baa lamaiyoo, “Emba namba watao ipu” lea. Dokopa baa sakatatala, Jisasa watao pea.
Jisasapi, baanya disaipolo dupapi, Lipainya andaka pupala, nee nao peteami. Peteamino dokonya, koo pingipi, takisa nyingipi, longo mendapu Jisasa watao peamino dupa apata nee nao peteami.
Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali Parasai dupame kandeaminopa, Jisasa koo pingipi, takisa nyingipi, dupa-pipa nee nao apata peteamopa, baanya disaipolo dupa tipa pyoo, “Baa aipuma koo pingipi, takisa nyingipi, dupa-pipa nee nao pilyape?” leami.
Jisasame pii leamino doko sepala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Endakali yaina napingi dupa dokosa yangyala naenge. Endakali yaina pyapae dupa dokosa yangingi. Nambame endakali tolatae dupa wii lao lanyalanya naepeo. Endakali koo pingi dupa wii lao lanyalanya epeona” lea.
Jone kaimbu pingi dokonya disaipolopi, Parasaipi, dupame Gote loma soo nee nanao kateami. Dopa piaminopa, endakali dupame Jisasa tipa pyoo, “Jonenya disaipolopi, Parasaipi, dupa Gote loma soo nee nanao kataminopa, aipuma embanya disaipolo dupa dopa napilyamipi?” leami.
Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Akali mendeme enda kelyapala, watapae pyao, baanya tata dupa-pipa apata kalyamo gii dokopa, baanya tata dupame nee nala naenya kaengemape? Daa, enda kelyelyamo akali doko kalyamo dokopa, watapae pyao nee nengema.
Akali enda kelyenge dopale joo, namba nyakama-pipa apata katao, nee nao kalyamano. Gii mendepa, akali waka mendapuame namba nyokonyoo patataminopa, nambanya disaipolo dupa loma soo nee nanao katatamina” lea.
Dopa latala kongali pii mendeaka dee Jisasame lao pituu, “Endakali mendeme lapalapa kaketapae etete enenge mendeme yonge pee atingi mendenya tii telyamo dokonya kii pimbala naenge. Endakali mendeme lapalapa etete enenge mende atingi-kisa kii pimbatala, wasa pyatamopa, enenge doko inungunyetamo dokome, atingi doko kanguo koeyaseta.
Dopaka pyoo, endakali mendeme waene enenge kamuo, penge meme yanungimi wasepae atinginya pyandatamo, dokome waene doko bolo lapala, penge atingi doko kangutamopa, waenepa, pengepa, lapota koeyata. Tenge dokonya, waene enenge kamupae doko penge atinginya kamuo pisala naenge. Waene enenge doko penge enengenyaka kamuo pisingina” lea.
Sambata gii mendenya Jisasapi, baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa wita ee kaina mendenya pao pituu, baanya disaipolo dupame wita dii dupa kii lao nyepa-nyepa pyoo peami.
Dopa piaminopa, Parasai dupame Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Sambata gii dokonya akali dakaitame loome daa latae singi doko yalelyamino kanda” leami.
Dokopa Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Dapitimi piamo doko nyakamame pepanya itaki napiamipi? Wamba akali Abiata doko pitisa mupa dupanya aiyomba joo kateamopa, Dapitipi, akali apata kateamino dupa lopo kaeyami. Lopo kaeyapala, Dapitimi Gotenya lotuu andaka kolandatala, betesa Gote opa maitae, pitisa dupame iki napenge siamo dupa nyepala, akali dupa maiyoo neana” lea.
<range>
Dopa latala baame dokaita dee lamaiyoo, “Goteme Sambata gii doko lao masetala, endakali wasala naeya, etete daa. Endakali lao masetala, Goteme Sambata gii doko setea.
Akalinya Ikiningi dokome Sambata gii doko apata isoo kalyamoakana” Jisasame lea.
Gii mendepa Jisasa baa Judamanya lotuu anda dokonya peamopa, akali kingi yangi talyanga mende peteamo kandea.
Parasai dupame Jisasa kote lamana latala, baame akali doko Sambata gii dokonya kingi doko tolasakamailyape lao, isokondape petae peteami.
Jisasame akali kingi yangi talyanga doko lamaiyoo, “Emba sakatatala, endakali pitakanya enombanya kalya ipu” lea.
Dopa latala baame dokaita tipa pyoo, “Sambata gii dokonya kalai koo pipengepe, pande epe pipengepe? Dee endakali pyao kumasepengepe, pande nisepengepe?” lea. Dopa leamopa, dokaita ema napiami.
Dokaitame akali kingi yangi talyanga doko kondo kaeyala naeyaminosa, Jisasame imbu kaeyao dokaita kandayoko latala, akali doko lamaiyoo, “Embanya kingi tinoka” lea. Leamoli pyoo baanya kingi doko tinokateamopa, tolea.
Tolaseteamopa, Parasai dokaita kamaka pyakalyetala, Kiŋi Erote Antipasa tata dupa-pipa, Jisasa aipa petala pyao kumasemape lao, yapa pao kambuiyami.
Dopa piaminopa, Jisasapi, baanya disaipolo dupapi, anda doko yakinatala, Galilea pete dokonya peami. Peaminopa, Galilea tangepi, Judia tangepi, Jerusalema tangepi, Idumia tangepi, endaki Jodane omotena tangepi, Taeya tangepi, Saidone tangepi, kambu longo dupame Jisasame pilyamo lapae dupa sepala, baa kateamo dokonya epeami.
<range>
Wamba baame endakali yaina pyapae longo mee jakamaiyamo kandeamino dokonya, endakali waka yaina pyapae longome baa watandamana latala, tuu-tuu lao baa katao tambukinalanya piaminosa, sipi yakane mende disaipolo dupame depa lekena lea.
<range>
Imambu koo dupame baa kandeaminoli pyoo, baa kateamo dosa ipao tombauli sepala puu lao, “Emba Gote Ikiningina” lata piami.
Dokopa Jisasame kyeto joo imambu koo dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame namba dokona lao panala naeyalapape, eteteaka daana” lea.
Jisasa baa yuu manda mendenya pupala, akali mendatupa yapao nyotoo lao masiamo dutupa epena leamopa, baa kateamo dokonya epeami.
Epeamino dupanya akali 12 dutupa yapao nyepala, baa-pipa tole katamana latala, kenge aposolo maiya. Dutupame wai pii epe doko lamaiyoo, dee imambu koo dupa watao pingi pupu lapae doko maiyanya yapao nyia.
<range>
Baame 12 disaipolo dutupa yapao nyepala, Saimone kandao kenge enenge Pita lea.
Sebedi ikiningi Jemesa, Jonepa dolapo kandao kenge Bonagesa lea. (Bonagesa tenge doko, “Kaiti toka lelyamo dopale.”)
Dee baame Andruapi, Pilipapi, Batolomyuapi, Matyuapi, Tomasapi, Alopiasa ikiningi Jemesapi, Tadiusapi, Saimone kenge mende Selote lengema dokopi, Jisasa enge nyiamo akali Judasa Iskariota dokopi, dutupa yapao nyia.
<range>
Disaipolo yapao nyepala, Jisasa baa andaka pea. Dokopa endakali deaka ipao kambu piaminosa, baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa nee napenge nanjia.
Endakali yangi dupame baa kyekelyamo leamino doko sepala, baanya tata dupame kii minao lanyala epeami.
Epeaminopa, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali, Jerusalema katao epeamino dupame lao pituu, “Baa-kisa imambu koo dupanya isingi, Belesabulu doko ipao palipya dokome, imambu koo waka dupa watao pilyamona” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baame dokaita epena latala, kongali piimi lamaiyoo, “Sataneme Satane tange aipa petala watao pyatape?
Kiŋi mendenya tata doko pyaloo petala, nyakama wakale pitamino doko, nyakama mendai joo napalitami.
Akali mendenya enda wanepi dupa wakale petala, nyakama yangolapo pyaloo pitamino doko, nyakama mendai joo napalitami.
Dokaitaka joo Sataneme baanya tata doko wakale pyoloo petala, nyakama yangolapo yanda pitamino doko, nyakama mendai joo napalitamiaka. Nyakama etatami.
Akali mendeme akali pupu lapae mendenya andaka kolandatala, baanya pinju dupa pake nyalanya-tamo doko, wambao kendeme baa yaki pinya setapala nyeta.
“Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Endakalinya koo dupapi, Gote kandao lamba lengepi, dupa pitaka Goteme kunao nepakamaita.
Dopaka doko, endakali mendeme Oli Spirit kandao lamba latamo doko, Goteme baanya koo doko kunao nepala naeyata. Tanga tangapi baa-kisa koo doko setana” lea.
Jisasa-kisa imambu koo mende palelyamona leaminosa, baame dopa lea.
Dokopa Jisasanya endangi kaiminingipi, dupa ipao katapala, baa kamanda epena lao, endakali mendeme lanyala pena leami.
Lateaminopa, endakali baa pituu kakopeamino dupame Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Embanya endangi kaiminingipi, kamanda katao, emba ipu lelyamino” leami.
Jisasame yanu pyao, “Nambanya endangi kaiminingipi dupa apitupape?” lea.
Baa pituu kakopeamino dupa kandatala, “Pii soo pilyamino datupa nambanya endangi kaiminingipina kanjepa!
Gotenya masingili pingima endakali dupa nambanya kaiminingipi, pimalengepi, endangipina” lea.
Deaka Jisasame Galilea pete lemba dokonya endakali dupa mana lamaiyoo kateamopa, endakali etete longo ipao kambu piami. Dopa piaminosa, baa sipi mendenya pyakalyetala peteamopa, endakali pitaka lembanya kateami.
Kateaminopa, Jisasame kongali lao endakali dupa mana lamaiya. Lamaiyoo pituu,
“Nyakamame salapape! Akali mendeme ee wai lyandala pea-pyaa.
Lyandeamopa, ee wai yangi kaitininya pea. Peamo dupa pitaka yaka dupame nyoo neami.
Yangi kana-kisa yuu kuki singi dupanya peamo dupa pupae langa lea.
Langa leamoaka doko, pingi auu pyoo napiamosa, niki teamo dokome kumasia.
Yangi yuu ikililyambu tenge palenge dupanya pea. Peamo dupa ikililyambu tambe-tambe andapala, kui pyatala, dii namandea.
Ee wai yangi lyandeamo dupa yuu epenya pupala, andao dii mandea. Yangimi dii 30 mandea. Yangimi dii 60 mandea. Yangimi dii 100 mandeana” lea.
Dopa latala, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakama kalekaita singi dupame pii doko auu pyoo salapapena” lea.
Maitakao Jisasa baa endakali kambu doko yakinateamopa, 12 disaipolo dupapi, dee endakali mendatupa tole kateamino dupapimi kongali pii dupanya baa tipa piami.
Dokonya baame yanu pyao, “Gotenya isingi mate dokonya pii tenge yalo petae palelyamo doko nambame nyakama langitoo. Dopaka doko, endakali netesa katenge dupame kongaliaka salamino.
Sepala, 'dupame lengeme kanjaminoaka doko, tenge angi doko kandao nanyalamino. Pii salaminoaka doko, tenge angi doko nanyalamino. Dopaka pyoo, dupame sepala, mona kapilyala naeyataminopa, Goteme dupanya koo dupa kunao nepakamaiya naeyatana'” lea.
Deaka Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame kongali pii dake sepala, tenge nyala naelyamino doko, aipa petala kongali pii waka dupanya tenge dupa soo nyetamipi?
Akali dokome ee wai joo Gotenya pii doko lyandea.
Ee wai lyandeamo dokonya yangi kaitinisa peamo dupa yakame nyoo neami. Dopaleaka joo, wai pii epe doko endakalimi sepelyaminopa, monanya nasina lao, Sataneme ipupala nyoo nepenge.
Ee wai yangi kana-kisa pao langa leamo dopaleaka joo, endakali dupame wai pii epe doko auu kaeyao yapa nyingima.
Ee wai kana-kisa pingi napiamosa, kumiamo dopaleaka joo, endakali dupame wai pii epe doko auu pyoo nyepelyaminopa, nyakama-kisa pundu kendapi longo epelyamopa, wai pii epe doko pupae yakinengema.
Ee wai yangi yuu ikililyambu tenge palenge dupanya peamo dopaleaka joo, endakali dupame wai pii epe doko singima.
Singimaka doko, yuunya munipi, pinjupi, longo lao nyoo setao katapu laka lao putiti kaenge mana dokome, wai pii epe doko kui pilyamosa, dii namandengema.
Ee wai yangi lyandeamo dupa yuu epenya pupala, andao dii mandea. Dopaleaka joo, wai pii epe doko sepala, endakali yangimi dii 30 mandenge. Yangimi 60 mandenge. Yangimi 100 lao dii mandengena” lea.
Dopa latala baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Endakali mendeme lama kaiyepae nyepala, titopene pengenya koko pyandengepe, pande toko pundi-pundi pyandengepe? Daa, lama kaiyepae doko toko ketae setenge.
Yalo petae silyamo dupa gii mendepa panao seta. Yame pyatae silyamo dupa gii mendepa lopapae seta.
Nyakama kalekaita singi dupame pii doko auu pyoo salapapena” lea.
Dopa latala dee baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame endakali mende-kisa mana minatamino dopaka pyoo, Goteme nyakama-kisa mana minata. Dopana, nyakamame pii silyamino dokonya tenge doko masetala pyepape. Dopa pitaminoliaka pyoo, Goteme mana mendatupa apata konda pyakata.
Endakali mende-kisa Gotenya pii longo setamo doko, baa konda pyoo maita. Dopaka doko, Gotenya pii nasingi mende-kisa kuki setamopa, sekelyamo lao masetamo doko, dutupa tange nyokonyetana” lea.
Jisasame kongali pii mende lao pituu, “Gotenya isingi mate doko akali mendeme ee wai lyandenge dopale.
Baame lyandatala, kuka luu palipa, yongama sakatata pilyamopa, ee wai doko tange langa latala, andenge. Dopa pilyamopa, aipa petala langa lao andelyape lao nakandenge.
Yuu dokome pilyamopa, ee wai doko langa lenge. Dokopa, yoko pingi. Dopa petala, mange dokonya dii lyoo, wambu pingi.
Dii doko wambu petelyamopa, ee pokenge akali dokome konja-wuame lyao mandengena” lea.
Jisasame deaka dokaita lamaiyoo, “Naimame Gotenya isingi mate doko aipalena lamape? Dee aki mendepa makande pimape?
Doko ee wai mastet lenge dopale. Ee wai waka dupa ita minao, mastet wai doko etete yakane mende.
Yakaneaka doko, endakali mendeme mastet wai doko yuunya lyandelyamopa, andao yale jetala, ee wai waka pokatae dupa ita miningi. Dokopa, wangya dupame lumba nelyamo dupanya yakame ipao anda pingimana” lea.
Baame kongali dopale dupame wai pii epe doko endakali dupame sepengeli pyoo lamaiyoo katea.
Baame pii mende mee lamaiya naeyao, kongali laowaka lamaiya. Baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa iki katao, kongali dupa pitakanya tenge dupa lamaita pia.
Yuu kuiyamopa, Jisasame baanya disaipolo dupa lamaiyoo, “Naima endaki pete dakenya omotena mua” lea.
Dokopa endakali kambu dupa yakinatala, Jisasa sipi peteamo dokonya pituu peami. Dee sipi waka mendatupa apataka peami.
Peaminopa, poo yale mende leamopa, endaki buli piamo dokome, tandyoo sipi dokonya kolandea. Dopa piamopa, sipi doko endakimi tumbalanya pia.
Jisasa baa sipi dokonya maitakaita sanda setapae mendenya paleamopa, disaipolo dupame baa pyale tatala, “Mana Lenge Akali, naima kumalamane-lamo doko, embame nakandelepe?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasa sakatatala, poo doko kaena latala, endaki buli piamo doko lamaiyoo, “Emba yatu laa! Ema napinya mee saa!” leamopa, poo doko yatu lao, endaki doko ema napyoaka pia.
Dokopa baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Aipuma nyakama paka kaelyamipi? Nyakamame namba tungi napilyamipi?” lea.
Dopa piamopa, disaipolo dupa etete paka kaeyapala, nyakamalapo laloo pyoo, “Endakipa poopa dolapome baanya pii lapyali pilyambino doko, akali dake api laa kanjemape?” leami.
Dokopa Jisasa baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa Galilea pete omotena, Gerasamanya yuu dokonya peami.
Pao pyakamatala, Jisasa baa sipi doko yakinatala peamopa, akali imambu koo paleta mendeme endakali malu katenge dupanya katao ipao baa kandanyia.
Akali doko endakali malu katenge dupanya palenge. Endakali mendeme sene kendemepi baa anjala naengema.
Paa longosa baa sene kendepi, anengapupi, dupame anjeta pilyaminopa, baame dupa minao pindanya nepenge. Dopa pilyamopa, endakali mendeme kapa pao baa minao lambapenge nanjingi.
Kuka kotakapi, koteaka lao baa endakali malupi, yuu mandapi, dupanyaka paliu katenge. Dupanya katapala ae latae katao, baanya yonge doko tange kaname konjeta pingi.
Jisasa londati joo kateamopa, akali dokome kandatala, alo pyao ipupala baa kateamo dosa luma lakea.
Luma lakapeamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Imambu koo, embame akali dake yakinatala puu!” lea. Dopa lateamopa, baame puu lao, “Jisasa, emba Gote Etete Ketae Katenge dokonya Ikiningi. Embame namba aipa pitipi? Embame Gotenya kenge dokonya kyeto joo, namba tanda andake nanditoo lao laa” lea.
<range>
Dokopa Jisasame baa tipa pyoo, “Emba kenge apipi?” lea. Dopa leamopa, akali dokome yanu pyao, “Naima imambu koo longo kalyamano. Tenge dokonya, namba kenge Longo lengena” lea.
Dopa latala, imambu koo dupame kongo latae katao, nyakama yuu dokonya pyao watala naena lao wii lao tee leami.
Mena tausene lapomapi mende manda kili-kili dokonya nao kateami. Dokopa, imambu koo dupame Jisasa tee lao, “Naima mena dokaita-kisa landa pyalapa lapoko!” leami. Dopa leaminopa, mena dokaita-kisa kolandena leamopa, imambu koo dupame akali doko soo yakinatala, mena dupa-kisa pao landa piami. Landa pyateaminopa, mena elyambu doko pitaka alo pyao pao, endaki pete dokonya mangatala kumiami.
<range>
<range>
Kumateaminopa, mena setao katenge dupa taononyapi, mee akali palenge yuu dupanya paka pupala, dopa pyomona lao lamaiyami. Lamaitiaminopa, endakali dupame piamo dupa kanja epeami.
Dupa Jisasa kateamo dokonya ipupala kandeaminopa, wamba akali imambu koo longo paleta kateamo doko indupa yonge pee dupa petala, mona paliu peteamo kandatala, paka kaeyami.
Dokopa wamba kandeamino endakali dupame ene kanja epeamino dupa dopa pyomona lao lamaiyami.
Lamaitiaminopa, dupame kongo lao Jisasa baa nyakamanya yuu doko yakinatala, pena leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baa sipi dokonya pyakalyiamopa, wamba imambu koo paleta kateamo dokome baa apata buape lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame daa latala, “Kamongome emba kondo kaeyapala, embanya pyakalamo dupa andaka pupala, emba tata dupa lamaipi” lea.
Dopa lamaitiamopa, akali dokome pupala, baa-kisa Jisasame piamo dupa pitaka yuu Dekapolisa dokonya panao lamaiyamopa, endakali siamino dupa pitaka walu leami.
Jisasa baa sipi dokonya pituu, Galilea pete dokonya yangitena pilyetala kateamopa, endakali longo mendapu ipao kambu piami.
Dokopa Judamanya lotuu anda mendenya isingi akali Jairusa lenge doko epea. Ipao Jisasa kandatala, baanya moko siamo dosa tombauli sepala
kongo lao, “Nambanya wanenge doko kumalanya pilyamona, embame baa-kisa kingi setapala, saka nyakala ipu” lao tee lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasa baa-pipa apata peambinopa, endakali longome baa watao pupala, katao tambukiniami.
Kateamino dupanya enda mende ee kana 12 dutupanya yuu gii dii lao angupae kandenge doko etala naeya.
Dopa piamosa, enda dokome dokosa longo dupa-kisa muni longo nepeamoaka doko, dupame angi nisala naeyamopa, etete koeyala pea.
Jisasame pilyamo lapae dupa sepala, enda dokome maitakaita pupala, Jisasanya yonge peenya watandato doko, baanya yaina doko mee jakalapomona lao masetala, baanya yonge pee dokonya kingimi watandea.
<range>
Watandalu piamopa, enda dokome baanya yaina doko etalumu lao sia.
Dokopa Jisasa baanya pupu lapae mendatupa puumu lao sepala, endakali kambu kateamino dupa kandapilyetala, “Apimi nambanya yonge peenya watandelyape?” lea.
Baanya disaipolo dupame yanu pyao, “Endakali kambu dakeme emba katao tambukinilyamino kandeleno doko, aipuma embame 'Apimi namba watandelyape?' leepe?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, apimi pyape lao kanjanya, Jisasame kandayoko lea.
Dopa piamopa, enda dokome baa-kisa piamo dutupa pitaka masetala, paka kaeyao, walu lao ipao Jisasanya moko seteamo, dosa tombauli sepala, baame piamo dupa pitaka panao Jisasa lamaiya.
Dokopa Jisasame enda doko lamaiyoo, “Wanaku, embame namba tungi pyapino dokome, embanya yaina doko etelyamona, emba mona yaepatala puu” lea.
Dopa lao kateamopa, Judamanya lotuu anda isingi akali Jairusanya andaka katao, akali mendapuame ipupala Jairusa lamaiyoo, “Embanya wanenge doko kumatalamona, mana lenge akali doko epena laa naenya, kaeya” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame soo nasili petala Jairusa lamaiyoo, “Embame paka nakaenya, Gote tungi pyatala katape” lea.
Dopa latala baame endakali pitaka baa watao naepena latala, Pita, Jemesa, Jemesa kaiminingi Jonepi, dutupa-pipa iki peami.
Pao Jairusanya andaka pyakamatala kandeaminopa, endakali dupame yako lao ee leami.
Dokopa Jisasame andaka kolandatala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Aipuma nyakama yako lao ee lelyamipi? Wanaku doko kumala naeyalamo. Mee luu palelyamona” lea.
Jisasame leamo doko sepala, endakali dupame baa kilya kandao gii kaeyami. Dopa piaminosa, baame dokaita watao kamanda pyalyetala, wanaku dokonya endangi takangepi, disaipolo tepoma apata peamino dutupa-pipa iki wanaku kumapae siamo dokonya peami.
Pupala wanaku dokonya kinginya minatala baa lamaiyoo, “Talita kum” lea. (Pii dokonya tenge doko, “Wanaku emba sakata.”)
Dopa leamopa, wanaku ee kana 12 patae doko sakatatala paeya. Paeyamo kandatala, dupame etete paka kaeyao, walu leami.
Dokopa Jisasame dokaita etete kyeto joo lamaiyoo, “Endakali dupame pyomo dake setamina, mende lamaiya naeyalapape” lea. Dopa latala, “Baa nee nena maiyepa” lea.
Jisasame yuu doko yakinatala, baa katao andeamo yuu dokonya peamopa, baanya disaipolo dupame watao peami.
Pupala Sambata gii doko epeamopa, baame Judamanya lotuu anda dokonya mana lamaiya. Lamaiyamopa, pii siamino endakali longo dupame walu latala lao pituu, “Baanya masepae epe tolatae dokopi, mirakolo kalai pupu lapae pilyamo dokopi, dolapo anja-tae nyiape?
Akali dake kapenda kalai pingi doko daa kandamuape? Baa Maria ikiningi, Jemesa, Josepe, Judasa, Saimonepi dutupanya kaiminingi daape? Baanya pimalenge dupa ae naima-pipa apata napilyamape?” leami. Dopa latala dupame Jisasa kandao mona koo palyetala, baa yakineami.
Dokopa Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Propeta mende yuu waka dupanya kalyamo doko, endakali dupame baa andanda semaingima. Dopaka doko, propeta mende baanya yuu dokonya kalyamo doko, baa tata dupame baanya pii nasepala, andanda semaiya naengemana” lea.
Dokopa yuu dokonya baame mirakolo kalai mendapu kapa pao pipenge nanjiamosa, endakali kuki mendatupa-kisa kingi setao yaina mee jakamaiya.
Endakali dupame baa tungi pyala naeyaminosa, baa mona kenda kaeya. Maitakao Jisasa baa yuu yakane dupanya pao, endakali dupa mana lamaiya.
Mana lamaitala Jisasame 12 disaipolo dutupa epena latala, imambu koo dupa watao pina lao pupu lapae maitala, dupa lapo-lapo lao pena lea.
Pena lao pituu, “Nyakama kaita patamino dokonya nee napengepi, nokainapi, munipi, yonge pee wakaowapi, mende nyoo napupape. Pangali minao, moko pee pyoo pupape” lao kyeto joo lamaiya.
<range>
Dopa latala baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakama pao katatamino gii dutupanya anda tee pyao palitamino dokonyaka paliu kalyepape.
Yuu tange dupame nyakama mambo pyao lanyala naeyao, nyakamanya pii doko nasoaka piami kandeno doko, nyakamame yuu doko yakinatala pupape. Yuu tange dupa ketae kenda pipae silyame-lamo lao kandena, nyakamanya mokonya yuu katatamo dupa lyanda lanya setapala pupape” Jisasame lea.
Dopa leamopa, dupame pupala, endakali dupa mona kapilyina lao, wai pii epe doko lamaiyami.
Pii lamaiyoo pituu, imambu koo longo mendapu watao piami. Dee endakali yaina pyapae longo dupa olipi ipangeme kai pyakamaiyaminopa, yaina dupa mee jia.
Jisasame kalai andake pilyamo lapae doko yuu dupa pitakanya taeyamopa, Kiŋi Erote Antipasame sia. Endakali mendapuame lao pituu, “Jone kaimbu pingi doko malunya sakatatala, kalai pupu lapae dupa pyoo kalyamona” leami.
Yangi dupame baa Ilaijana leaminopa, yangimi baa propeta wamba kateamino dopale mende-lamona leami.
Eroteme pii doko sepala, “Jone kaimbu pingi, nambame mange kepeo doko, sakatapya-lumuna” lea.
Wamba Eroteme baanya kaiminingi Pilipa etanenge Erodiasa lenge doko tondao nyia. Dopa piamopa, Joneme Erote lamaiyoo, “Embanya kaimininginya etanenge tondao nyilino doko, loome daa latae singi doko yalelenona” lao kateamosa, enda Erodiasa dokome Jone imbu kaeyapala, pyao kumasalanya piamopa, kapa napea. Eroteme Jone doko akali tolatae epe etete mende-lamo lao kandatala, baa paka kaeyapala, auu pyoo isoo katea. Baame Jonenya pii dupanya tenge nanyiamoaka doko, mee baanya pii doko auu kaeyao sia. Dopa petala Eroteme Erodiasa auu kaeyapae nyina lao masetala, Jone anjinya pyandea.
<range>
<range>
<range>
Erotenya mandenge gii doko epeamopa, baanya kalai akali andake dupapi, yanda singi mupa dupapi, Galilea tange akali andake dokaitanya nee yangakamaiya. Gii dokopa, Erodiasame kandeamopa, Jone pyapenge kaitini mende sia.
Dokopa nee nao peteamino dokonya Erodiasa wanenge doko ipao kolandatala, danisa lea. Dopa piamopa, Erotepi, baa-pipa apata nee nao peteamino dupame etete auu kaeyao kandeami. Kandatala Kiŋi Eroteme wanaku doko lamaiyoo, “Embame dopale mende namba-kisa tee latenopa, nambame latenoli pyoo, emba dyaapo.
Embame nambanya isingi mate doko aopa lao konjepala, yangi dii lateno doko, dyaapoakana lao nambame kiningi etete lelyona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, wanaku doko endangi peteasa pupala, baa tipa pyoo, “Aki mende dina lao tee laowape?” lea. Dopa leamopa, endangimi baa lamaiyoo, “Jone kaimbu pingi dokonya aiyomba doko dina lape” lea.
Dokopa kiŋi doko peteasa wanaku doko alo pyao pupala, “Embame Jone kaimbu pingi dokonya aiyomba doko pelesa mendenya setapala, epapuaka dii” lea.
Dopa leamopa, kiŋi doko etete mona kenda kaeyamoaka doko, wamba endakali dupanya enombanya kiningi etete maitoana leamo doko masetala, wanaku dokonya pii nepala naeyatoo lao masia.
Dopa lao masetala dokopaka, yanda singi mendeme Jonenya aiyomba doko kepao nyala pena leamopa, baa anjetae andaka pupala, Jonenya aiyomba doko kepao nyia.
Kepao nyepala pelesa mendenya setapala, nyoo ipao wanaku doko maitiamopa, wanaku dokome nyepala, endangi pao maiya.
Dopa piamo doko sepala, Jonenya disaipolo dupame baanya yonge doko nyoo pao malu piami.
Aposolo dupa Jisasa kateamo dokonya pilyetala, nyakamame kalai piamipi, mana lamaiyamipi, dupa dopa pipumana lao baa lamaiyami.
Dokopa endakali longo mendapu pao ipao piami dokome, Jisasapi, baanya disaipolo dupapi, nee napenge gii nasia. Dopa piamosa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Naima iki endakali napalenge yuu mendasa, kuki koto nyemana mona ipupa” lea.
Dopa lateamopa, nyakama sipi mendenya pao pyakalyetala, endakali napalenge yuu mendakaita peami.
Peaminopa, endakali longo dupame nyakama dutupa dosa paanya pelyamino lao kandatala, taono dupa pitakanya tange dupame mee kaitini alo pyatala, wambao pao kateami.
Jisasa sipinya pituu isa pyakanatala, endakali kambu andake mende kateamino kandea. Dokaita sipisipi setao katenge akali mende nakatenge joo kateaminosa, kondo kaeyapala, baame pii longo mendapuame mana lamaiya.
Lamaiyoo kateamopa, niki lenge landa pyalanya pia. Dokopa baanya disaipolo dupame baa kateasa ipupala lao pituu, “Endakali napalenge panda dakenya yuu kuiyalanya pilyamona,
embame dokaita maketa seta dupanya tange nee sambao nala pena laa” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baame pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Nyakamameaka nee maiyepa” lea. Dokopa dokaitame baa lamaiyoo, “Naimame muni andake anjataeme betesa sambapala, endakali longo dake nena lao maimape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Betesa akipate silyape lao kanja pupa” lea. Pao kandatala dokaitame baa lamaiyoo, “Naimanya 5-pela betesa-pipa, pisa lapoma-pipa iki silyamona” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame disaipolo dupa lamaiyoo, “Tanu sakapae dupanya endakali dupa pitaka kambu pyao wakale-wakale petena lapa” lea.
Leamoli pyoo, kambu mende 50 lao pitipa, 100 lao pitipa piami.
Dokopa Jisasame 5-pela betesa, pisa lapoma-pipa siamo dutupa nyepala, kaiti-kisa kandalyetae katao yaka pilino lea. Yaka pilino latala baame betesa dutupa konjepala, baanya disaipolo dupame mokosina lao maiya. Dopa petala baame pisa dolapo endakali dupa pitakanya konjakamaiyaka.
Mokosoo maiyaminopa, dokaita pitakame nao tiaka kaeyami.
Napeaminopa, disaipolo dupame betesa pisapi konjepae kakana siamo dupa nyoo, 12-pela baseketa tumbasiami.
Nee neamino akali dupa 5 tauseneme neami.
Dopa petala, Jisasame baanya disaipolo dupa sipinya pyakalyetala, Galilea pete omotena, yuu Betsaida wambao pena lea. Baame endakali kambu dupa andaka pena latala, kandao katea.
Dokaita pateaminopa, baa loma sala yuu manda mendenya pea.
Yuu kuiyala peamopa, sipi doko endaki pete kaina dokonya peamopa, Jisasa baa iki yuu manda dokonya katea.
Dokopa paanya peamino dokaita-kaita poo andake mende lao epeamosa, dokaitame leke-leke tao endaki tandyoo peamino Jisasame kandea. Kandatala yuu yongao pukiamopa, baa endaki pete ketae dokonya moko katao pupala, dokaita nyoo maita pyalanya pia.
Baa endaki pete ketae dokonya moko katao epeamo kandatala, baanya disaipolo dupame timango mende-lamo lao masetala, paka kaeyapala ae leami. Ae leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Namba kalyona, nyakama paka nakaeyalapa” lea.
<range>
Dopa latala, Jisasa sipinya pyakalyiamopa, poo doko yatu lea. Leamo kandatala, disaipolo dupa walu lao pakame kumiami.
Jisasame betesa kukimi akali 5 tauseneme nao kapa pena leamo tenge doko, disaipolo dupame nyala naeyami. Dopaka pyoo, Jisasame endaki ketae paeyamo tenge doko nyala naeyao nongo piami.
Dokopa Jisasa disaipolo dupa-pipa endaki pete dokonya omotena, yuu Genesarete pyakamatala, sipi doko minanya seteami.
Sipi doko yakinatala peaminopa, endakali dupame Jisasa baa epelyamo lao yapa kandeami.
Yuu kungu dupa pitakanya baa mendasa kalyamo lapae siamino dokonya pupala, endakali yaina pyapae dupa lapa tokonya soo pata piami.
Baa taono andakepi, yakanepi, mee yuupi, dupanya peamoli pyoo, yaina pyapae dupa lapa tokonya soo ipupala, maketa kamapu dupanya setapa piami. Dopa petala endakali soo epeamino dupame baanya yonge pee punanya yaina pyapae dupame watandena lao, Jisasa tee leami. Watandeamino endakali dupa pitakanya yaina dupa mee jeta pia.
Parasaipi, Juda tange pitakapi, dupanya yumbangenya mana dupa watao, nee nalanya kingi wasa pingili pyoo pyatala, nee nengema. Dupame maketanya katao ipupala, kingi wasa napinya, mee nee nanengema. Mana singili pyoaka, endaki pengepi, kapopi, titopenepi, dupa wasa pingima. Gii mendepa Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali Jerusalema katao epeamino dupapi, Parasaipi, dupa Jisasa kateamo dokonya ipao kambu piami. Dokopa baanya disaipolo yangimi kingi wasa napyao, mee nee neaminosa, akali dupame kandokondape pyoo kandeami.
<range>
<range>
<range>
Kandatala Parasaipi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, dupame Jisasa tipa pyoo, “Embanya disaipolo dupa kingi wasa napinya mee nee nelyamino doko, naimanya yumbangeme mana wambatae seteamino dupa aipuma watao minala naelyamipi?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakama, Gote watao miningi mane-mane pingima dupa kandao, wamba Goteme propeta Aisaiya-kisa nyakama-pipa makande pyokondape pyoo, dapa lea-pyaa: 'Endakali tata dakeme kambumi namba mambo pingimaka doko, nyakamanya moname namba angi mambo napingima.
Dupame endakalinya mana setapae dupa mana lao pituu, “Dake Gotenya mana setapaena” lengema. Nyakamame namba mambo pingimaka doko, nambame nyakamanya pii nasingina' Goteme Aisaiya-kisa lea-pyaa.
Nyakama Parasaipi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, dupame Gotenya mana setapae dupa nepatala, endakalinya mana dupa watao minao kalyaminona” Jisasame lea.
Dee baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame nyakama tangenya mana dupa watao minamana latala, Gotenya mana setapae dupa waa katao, anguo nepelyamino.
Wamba Mosesame lao pituu, 'Embanya endangi takangepi dolapo andanda semaiyoo katape' lea. Deaka lao pituu, 'Endakali mendeme baanya endangi takangepi dolapo kandao, Goteme minao koeyasina latamo doko, baa pyao kumasepengena' lea.
Mosesame dopa leamoaka doko, nyakamame mana waka mende miningima-lamo. Akali mendeme endangi takangepi lamaiyoo, 'Nambame nyakamba oapi dipenge dupa pitaka, Gote maitalona' latamo kandao doko, nyakamame kapana lao mana lengema-lamo. Dopa lao nyakamanya yumbange dupanya mana minilyamino, dokome endangi takangepi nisepengena lao, Gotenya loo seteamo doko mee joo nepengema-lamo. Dee nyakamame mana dopaleaka longo miningima-lamona” Jisasame lea.
<range>
<range>
Dokopa Jisasame endakali kambu piamino dupa dee baa kateamo dokonya epena latala lamaiyoo, “Nyakama pitakame pii nambame lelyo dake sepala, masokondape pyepape.
Endakali mendeme nee nelyamo dokome, baa Kamongo doko mambo napina lao kaita lyokala naenge. Endakali mendenya nengekaita pii koo epelyamo dokome, baa Kamongo doko mambo napina lao kaita lyokengena” lea.
<range>
Jisasa endakali kambu doko yakinatala, andaka pao peteamopa, baanya disaipolo dupame kongali pii leamo dokonya tenge aipale mende palelyape lao baa tipa piami.
Tipa piaminopa, baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame masala naelyamipi? Kamanda singi mende nengekaita pelyamo doko mona andaka napenya, mee inginya soo kamanda ipao penge. Dopa pilyamo dokome, baa minao koeyasala naengena” lea. (Dopa leamo dokome, Jisasame nee dupa pitaka napengena lea.)
<range>
Dopa latala dee Jisasame lao pituu, “Endakali mende-kisa mona andaka pituu, kamanda koo pyakalyingi dokome, baa minao koeyasingi. Masingi koopi, enda akalipi nyele-nyele paengepi, pake nengepi, endakali pyao kumasingipi,
<range>
kepo kolengepi, longo setapu laka lao masingipi, tuu pyoo mende minao koeyasotoo lao masingipi, minakasingipi, elya nakaengepi, waka mendenya oapi setamo dupa kandatala nyipu laka lao masingipi, lamba lengepi, alyasale joo kalyo lao masingipi, kyakaenge mana miningipi,
koo dutupa pitaka monanya paliu kamanda ipupala, endakali dupa minao koeyasingina” Jisasame lea.
Jisasame yuu doko yakinatala, yuu andake Taeya dokonya pea. Pupala baa anda mendenya kolandatala, elyakalao pititoo lao masiamoaka doko, baa yalo pipenge nanjia.
Dokopa wanaku imambu koo paleta mendenya endangimi anda dokonya Jisasa pilyamo lapae sepala, baa kolandatala, Jisasanya moko seteamo dosa luma lakapala, aiyomba yuunya sia.
Endangi kamalya petenge, yuu dokonya tange dokome, baanya wanenge-kisa imambu koo palenge doko Jisasame watao pyakamaina lao tee lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame enda doko lamaiyoo, “Wanenya nee dupa yana namaipenge. Wambao wanenya nee dupa tange nao tiaka kaena maipengena” lea.
Dopa leamopa, enda dokome yanu pyao, “Akali andake, wane dupame nee nelyaminopa, kuku-kakanapi isa pelyamo dupa yana toko pundi-pundi kalyami dupame nyoo nengemakana” lea.
Dokopa Jisasame enda doko lamaiyoo, “Embame kiningi namba tungi pyao leleno dokonya, imambu koo dokome embanya wanenge doko yakinatala patelyamona, emba andaka puu” lea.
Enda dokome andaka pupala kandeamopa, imambu koo dokome wanaku doko yakinatala pateamopa, baa auu pyoo tokonya paliu sia.
Jisasa yuu andake Taeya doko yakinatala, yuu Saidone-kaita pao, yuu Dekapolisa pyakanatala, dokonya-kaita lanao pao Galilea petesa pyakanea.
Dokopa endakali mendapuame akali kaleketa muumaa mende baa kateamo dokonya laminao ipupala, kingimi watandena lao tee leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame akali doko iki laminao, endakali kambu doko yakinatala, umbisale pupala, baanya kingi konde dolapo akali dokonya kalekaita pyandakamaiya. Dopa petala baanya kingi kondenya sopokali talyinya pisetala, muumaa dokonya kekenya watandea.
Dopa petala kaiti-kisa kandalyetae katao, mona ŋee latala, “Epata” lea. (Pii dokonya tenge doko, “Lumba.”)
Dopa leamopa, akali dokonya kalekaita dolapo lumbapa, keke doko tolata piamopa, pii tolao lea.
Dopa piamopa, Jisasame endakali kambu doko kyeto joo lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame kanjamino dupa mende lamaiya naeyalapape” lea. Dopa leamoaka doko, dupame pii nepatala, lamaiyoo taeyami.
Endakali siamipi, kandeamipi, dupame paka kaeyao walu latala, “Baame kalai pitaka auu pyoo pilyamo. Kaleketa dupanya kalekaita lumbakamaiyoo, dee muumaa dupame pii lena lelyamoakana” leami.
Gii mendepa endakali kambu andake mende deaka ipao kateami dokaitanya nee nasia. Dopa piamosa, Jisasame baanya disaipolo dupa epena latala lamaiyoo,
“Endakali dakaita namba-pipa yuu gii tepoma katapuma. Indupa nee etalame-lamo dokonya, nambame dakaita kondo kaelyo.
Yangi dupa tependa tangena, nee nanao andaka pena latopa, kaitinisa laowambe lapae setamina” lea.
Dopa leamopa, disaipolo dupame baa lamaiyoo, “Endakali napalenge yuu dakenya, naimame nee anja-tae nyepala nena maimape?” leami.
Jisasame, “Nyakamanya betesa akipate silyape?” leamopa, nyakamame, “7-pela silyamo” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baame endakali kambu doko isa petena lea. Dopa latala betesa 7-pela dutupa nyepala, Gote lao yaka pilino latala konjia. Konjepala baanya disaipolo dupame mokosoo maina lao maiya. Maiyamopa, baanya disaipolo dupame endakali kambu peteamino dupa dii lao mokosoo maiyami.
Pisa kuki mendatupa apata siaka, dutupa Jisasame Gote lao yaka pilino latala, apata mokosoo maina lea.
Endakali dokaitame nao tiaka kaeyateaminopa, konjepae kakana siamo dupa 7-pela baseketanya tumbasiami.
Akali nee neamino dupa 4 tausenepi mende. Dokaita napeaminopa, Jisasame andaka pena lea.
Pena latala baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa sipi mendenya pyakalyetala, yuu Damanuta peami.
Dokopa Parasai dupame ipupala, Jisasa pii yanda pimaiyami. Dupame baa minao makande pyoo, “Embame kalai pilino doko, Gote-kisa katao pilini-lamo lao kandamanana, mirakolo mende pii” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame mona ŋee yale pyoo latala, “Aipuma endakali indupa palelyamino dupame mirakolo mende pii lelyamipi? Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Mirakolo mende nyakama kanjepale lao napitoana” lea.
Dopa latala baame dokaita yakinatala, disaipolo dupa-pipa sipinya pyakalyetala, endaki pete dokonya omotena peami.
Disaipolo dupame betesa kame sepala ipateaminopa, sipi dokonya mendai iki sia.
Dokopa Jisasame disaipolo dokaita kongali lao lamaiyoo, “Parasaipi, Erote Antipasapinya yisa dupame nyakama koeyasetamina, wandyuu kalyepape” lea.
Dopa leamopa, nyakamalapo laloo pyoo, “Naimanya betesa nasipumu dokonya, baame dopa lelyamona” leami.
Dopa leamino doko Jisasame kandatala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame aipuma betesa nasilyamo lao mende lamai-lamai pilyamipi? Nyakama nongo pyapala, namba kandao apipi lao masala naelyamipi?
Nyakama lenge tenge-lamo doko, angi kanja naelyamipi? Nyakama kale katenge-lamo doko, angi nasilyamipi? Nambame kalai pilyo dupa nyakamame kame silyamipi?
Nambame 5-pela betesa nyepala, akali 5 tauseneme nena lao konjakamaiyo dokonya nao, kakana baseketa akipatenya tumbasiamipi?” lao Jisasame tipa pia. Dupame yanu pyao, “12-pela baseketana” leami.
Jisasame dee tipa pyoo, “Nambame 7-pela betesa nyepala, akali 4 tauseneme nena lao konjakamaiyo dokonya nao, kakana baseketa akipatenya tumbasiamipi?” lea. Dopa leamopa, dokaitame, “7-pela baseketana” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame namba kandao apipi lao masala naelyamipi?” lea.
Dokopa Jisasa baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa Betsaida yuu dokonya peami. Pupala kateaminopa, endakali dupame akali lenge monda mende baa kateamo dokonya laminao ipupala, Jisasame watandena lao tee leami.
Jisasame akali lenge monda doko kinginya minatae katao, taono yakane doko yakinatala peambi. Pupala baame sopokali talyinya lenge dolaponya pisetala, baanya kinginya minia. Dopa petala, “Embame dopale mende kandelepe?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, baame kandalyetala, “Nambame endakali dupa kandapupa, ita jepae mendapu kaita paele pilyaminona” lea.
Dokopa Jisasame akali dokonya lenge dolapo deaka kingimi minia. Minateamopa, baame dupa pitaka auu pyoo kandea.
Kandeamopa, Jisasame akali doko lamaiyoo, “Emba taononya napenya, andaka puu” lea.
Jisasapi, baanya disaipolo dupapi yuu Sisaria Pilipae dokonya taono dupanya peami. Pao pituu Jisasame disaipolo dupa tipa pyoo, “Endakali dupame namba kandao apina lelyamipi?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, dupame yanu pyao, “Yangimi emba kandao Jone kaimbu pingi dokona lelyamino. Yangimi emba Ilaijana lelyamino. Yangimi emba propeta wamba kateamino dupanya mendena lelyaminona” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita tipa pyoo, “Endakali dupame dopa lalumino doko, nyakamame namba kandao apina lelyamipi?” lea. Dopa leamopa, Pitame yanu pyao, “Emba Kraisa dokona” lea.
Dopa lateamopa, Jisasame dokaita kyeto joo lamaiyoo, “Endakali waka mende, namba dokona lao lamaiya naeyalapape” daa lea.
Dokopa Jisasame disaipolo dupa tee pyao lamaiyoo, “Akalinya Ikiningi doko tanda longo napenge. Judamanya isingi akalipi, pitisa mupapi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, dupame baa maka kaeyapala, pyao kumasetami. Kumasetaminopa, yuu gii tepo dokonya baa dee sakatatana” lea.
Jisasame pii dutupa panao lateamopa, Pitame baa laminao umbisale pupala, pyalanya lea.
Dopa lateamopa, baame kapilyetala, baanya disaipolo dupa kandatala, Pita pyalanya lao, “Satane, emba puu! Embame Gotenya masingi doko masala naenya, endakalinya masingi doko masilinona” lea.
Dopa latala baame endakali kambu dokopi, disaipolo dupapi lamaiyoo, “Endakali mendeme namba watao ipatoo lao masetamo doko, baa tange kame sepala, baanya poko ita doko nyoo soo, namba watao ipupenge.
Endakali mendeme namba watatosa tanda natona lao masetala, wanditamo doko, baa alu pita. Dopaka doko, endakali mendeme nambapi, wai pii epe dokopi lao masetala, baa tange kame setamo doko, baa auu pyoo katata.
Endakali mendeme namba yakinatala, yuunya oapi dupa pitaka nyoo setao katapala, baa alu pitamo doko, oapi dupame tanga baa aipa petala nisetape?
Dee aki mende Gote maitala, baa tange kapa pao pyoo nyetape?
Gote yakinatala, koo pyoo kalyamino dupanya kainanya katapala, endakali mendeme nambapi, nambanya pii dokopi lao panalanya elya kaeyatamo doko, Akalinya Ikiningi doko enjele epe dupa-pipa Takangenya tii pipae dokonya ipatamo dokopa, baame dopaka pyoo endakali doko kandao elya kaeyatakana” Jisasame lea.
Dopa latala Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Endakali ae kalyamino datupanya mendapu kumala naeyataminopa, Gotenya isingi mate doko panao ipatamopa, dokonya pupu lapae doko kandatamina” lea.
Yuu gii 6-pela pateamopa, Pita, Jemesa, Jonepi, dutupa iki Jisasame laminao, yuu manda ketae mendenya pea. Dokonya katao kandeaminopa, Jisasa baa waka jia.
Baanya yonge pee dupa etete kyoo lao pole-pole pia. Jisasanya yonge pee kyoo leamo dopale joo, endakali mendeme kyoo lena lao wasa napingima.
Dokopa Ilaija Mosesapa, Jisasa-pipa pii lao kalyu piaminopa, kandeami.
Kandatala Pitame Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Mana Lenge Akali, naima dakenya katamanopa, auu pilyamona, sele anda tepoma pimana. Mende embanya, mende Mosesanya, mende Ilaijanyana” lea.
Pitame paka kaeyapala, aipa laowape lao masala naeyao, mee lea.
Dopa leamopa, kopa mendeme ipupala, dokaita sanga pia. Kopa dokonya-kaita pii mende epea dokome, “Doo kalyamo doko nambanya Ikiningi mona setenge dokona, nyakamame baanya pii doko sakamaiyepape” lea.
Dokopa disaipolo tepoma dutupame kandayoko leaminopa, Jisasa iki katea.
Yuu manda doko yakinatala, lanao epeaminopa, Jisasame kyeto joo dutupa lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame kanjimino doko mende lamaiya naeyalapape. Tanga Akalinya Ikiningi doko kumapala, dee sakatatamopa, endakali dupa lamaitamina” lea.
Baame pii leamo doko mende lamaiya naenya, nyakamalapo laloo pyoo, “Kumapala dee baa sakatata lalamo dokonya tenge doko aipa pyoo laape?” leami.
Dopa petala disaipolo tepoma dutupame Jisasa tipa pyoo, “Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali dupame aipuma Ilaija wambao ipatatamopa, Kraisa ipupengena lengemape?” leami.
Baame yanu pyao, “Dupa pitaka depa lasalanya, Ilaija wambao ipupenge. Dopa latae singi-tamo doko, tenge aipuma Akalinya Ikiningi doko maka kaeyapala, tanda longo maitamina lao pepa pyapae silyape?
Jone kaimbu pingi doko Ilaija joo ipatea. Pii pepa pyapae singiliaka pyoo, baa epeamopa, endakali dupame masiamili pyoo, baa minao koeyasiamina” Jisasame lea.
Jisasa, Pita, Jone, Jemesapi pilyetala kandeaminopa, endakali kambu andake mendeme disaipolo yangi dokaita katao, kakopeami dokonya, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali mendapu katapala, disaipolo dupa-pipa pii yanda pyoo kateami.
Jisasa epeamopa, endakali kambu dupa pitakame walu lao kandatala, yapa pao kingi nyiami.
Dokopa Jisasame dokaita tipa pyoo, “Nyakama aki mendenya pii longo lelyamipi?” lea.
Akali kambu dupanya katea mendeme yanu pyao, “Mana Lenge Akali, nambanya wane doko imambu koo mendeme muumaa jiamosa, embame nisatale lao laminao epo.
Imambu koo dokome baa minao, lungu pilyamoli pyoo, lombapae singi. Dopa pilyamopa, wane doko nengekaita kambapupaka mandyuu, nenge kitakato lao, kingi mokopi tinokao tui lenge. Nambame embanya disaipolo dupame imambu koo watao pyakamaina lamaipupa, dupame kapa pao watao pyala naeyalaminona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame lao pituu, “Nyakama Gote tungi napingi tata, oo koto-koto doko namba nyakama-pipaka tole katatope? Nyakama nongo pilyamino doko andukupa tolataminopa lao, nambame malisoo kataowape? Wane doko laminao asa ipupa” lea.
Dokopa wane doko laminao, Jisasa kateasa epeaminopa, imambu koo dokome Jisasa kanju katao, wane doko walumane minao, lombanya seteamopa, nengekaita kambapupaka mandea.
Dokopa Jisasame takange doko tipa pyoo, “Wane dake gii andukupa tee pyao dopa piape?” lea. Baame yanu pyao, “Koosa tee pyao pia.
Paa longosa imambu koo dokome baa soo itatenya yangata, endakinya soo pyandata pyoo, kumasalanya pingina, embame dopale mende kapa pao piti-tamo doko, naima kondo kaeyao pipoko!” lea.
Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Embame aipuma, 'Dopale mende kapa pao piti-tamo doko' pii leepe? Endakali mendeme Gote tungi pilyamo dokome kalai dupa pitaka kapa pao pingina” lea.
Dopa leamopa, wane dokonya takange dokome puu lao, “Nambame Gote kuki tungi pilyona, kyeto joo tungi pyatoo, embame nisepe!” lea.
Dokopa endakali kambu dupame yapa ipao Jisasa katao kakopeamino kandatala, baame imambu koo doko pyalanya lao, “Emba muumaa kaleketa imambu koo dokome, wane dake yakinatala puu. Emba baa-kisa dee naipupi” lea.
Dopa leamopa, imambu koo dokome puu lao ae latala, wane doko minao etete walu lasetala, baa yakinatala pea. Dokopa wane doko kumapae joo siamopa, endakali longome, “Baa kumatelyamona” leami.
Dokopa Jisasame wane dokonya kinginya minatala, toeya katasia.
Toeya kataseteamopa, Jisasapi, disaipolo dupapi andaka peami. Dokopa disaipolo dupame Jisasa tipa pyoo, “Aipuma naimame imambu koo doko kapa pao watao pyala naeyalamape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Imambu koo dopale dupa lomame iki watao pingina” lea.
Jisasame disaipolo dupa-pipa yuu doko yakinatala, Galilea-kaita peami. Pao pituu Jisasame baanya disaipolo dutupa iki mana lamaiyanya, endakali mendeme nakandena lao masia.
Dokopa baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Akalinya Ikiningi doko enge nyepala, endakali dupame baa pyao kumasetami. Kumapala baa yuu gii tepo dokonya malunya dee sakatatana” lea.
Pii leamo dokonya tenge nyala naeyapala, disaipolo dupame baa tipa pyaanya paka kaeyami.
Dokaita Kapename pupala, andaka pituu Jisasame disaipolo dupa tipa pyoo, “Nyakamame kaitinisa aki mendenya lao ipamipi?” lea.
Nyakama dutupanya mende api alyasale joo kalyape lao, pii yanda pyoo kaitinisa lao epeamino, dokonya ema napiami.
Dokopa Jisasame 12 disaipolo dutupa tengesale epena latala lamaiyoo, “Endakali mende alyasale joo katapuli lao masetamo doko, baa anasale jepala, endakali pitakanya kalai akali joo katapengena” lea.
Dopa latala baame wane koo mende lanyepala, dokaitanya kainanya katasia. Dopa petala, baame wane doko kopinyetala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Endakali mendeme namba lao masetala, wane koo dapale mende lanyilyamo dokome, namba lanyingiaka. Namba lanyilyamo dokome namba iki lanyala naenge. Namba puu leamo akali doko lanyingiakana” lea.
<range>
Joneme Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Mana Lenge Akali, akali mendeme embanya kengenya imambu koo dupa watao pyapya doko kandatala, naima-pipa apata napaenge dokonyana, baame kalai pipya doko kaena daa lapumana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Baame kalai pilyamo doko nyakamame daa nalalapape. Endakali mendeme nambanya kengenya kalai pupu lapae mende pilyamo dokome, namba kandao yapa pii koo nalenge.
Naima nisilyamo endakali dokome naima koeyasala naenge.
Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Nyakama namba tata-lamona latala, endakali mendeme endaki kapo mendai kamuo ditamo dokonya, yole doko alu napyoo, sulu setana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Namba tungi pingi wane koo mende, endakali mendeme koo pina lao mapisetamo doko, kana andake mende baanya mangenya kende katatala, soo solowatanya pyandamili doko, auu pipyali.
Embanya kingi mendeme emba koo pyaale lao mapisetamo doko, kepanya nepape. Emba kingi mendai iki kateta, lete etete katenge dokonya pupili doko, auu pipyali. Emba kingi lapota kateta, itate konjala naenge ele panda koo dokonya pupili doko, auu napipyali.
<range>
Embanya moko mendeme emba koo pyaale lao mapisetamo doko, kepanya nepape. Emba moko mendai iki kateta, lete etete katenge dokonya pupili doko, auu pipyali. Emba moko lapota kateta, itate konjala naenge ele panda koo dokonya soo pyandamili doko, auu napipyali.
<range>
Embanya lenge mendeme emba koo pyaale lao mapisetamo doko, lukunya nepape. Emba lenge mendai iki tao, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya pupili doko, auu pipyali. Emba lenge lapota tapeta, ele panda koo dokonya soo pyandamili doko, auu napipyali.
Ele panda koo dokonya, nene ambo dupame nelyamo doko nao etala naenge. Itateme telyamo doko tao etala naengeaka.
“Nee opa mailyami dupa soleme pyoo wasingi. Dopaka pyoo, kenda pipaepi, makande pipaepi, dupanya-kaita endakali dupa Goteme pyoo wasingi.
Sole epeaka doko, tende patamo doko, nyakamame aipa petala dee tende pisetamipi? Nyakama sole katatae joo, auu pyoo kalyepape” Jisasame lea.
Jisasa baa Kapename yakinatala, Judia pao pyakamatala, endaki Jodane omotena pea. Dokopa endakali kambu dupa ipatae katao, baa kateamo dokonya ipao kambu piami. Dopa piaminopa, baame pingiliaka pyoo, endakali dupa deaka mana lamaiya.
Dokopa Parasai mendapuame ipupala, baa minao makande pyoo, “Akali mendeme baanya enda yakinatamo doko, loome daa latae singi doko yalatape?” leami.
Jisasame yanu pyao, “Wamba Mosesanya mana seteamo dokonya aipa latae silyape?” lea.
Dupame yanu pyao, “Akali dokome enda yakinenge pepa doko maitala, yakinapengena latae silyamona” leami.
Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamanya yumbange dupame tuu-tuu piaminosa, Mosesame mana doko pepa pyanya setea-pyaa.
Seteamoaka doko, Goteme tee pyao yuu kaitipi wasiamo dokopa, enda akalipa lao wasia.
Tenge dokonya, akali dokome baanya endangi takangepi yakinatala, enda dokopa tole pingi.
Dopa pilyambinopa, nyakamba lapo joo napetenya, yonge mendai joo petengemba.
Goteme nyoo pyasetae doko, endakalimi wakale pyoloo napipengena” Jisasame lea.
Dopa lateamopa, baanya disaipolo dupame dee andaka patala, pii leamo dokonya Jisasa tipa piami.
Dokopa baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Akali mendeme baanya enda doko yakinatala, waka mende nyetamo dokome, enda wambatae dokonya enombanya baa kepo kolata.
Dopaka pyoo, enda mendeme akalingi yakinatala, waka mendenya patamo doko, baa kepoaka kolatana” lea.
Endakali mendapuame Jisasa kateamo dokonya wane wanakupi dupa Jisasame kingi aiyombanya setapala, pii epe lamaina lao laminao epeaminopa, disaipolo dupame dokaita pyalanya leami.
Dokopa Jisasame imbu kaeyapala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Gotenya isingi mate doko wane wanakupi koo dapale joo kalyamino dupanyana, epekena kaita lyokala naeyalapa.
Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Wane wanakupi koo dupame Gotenya isingi mate doko nyingimali pyoo, endakali mendeme nanyetamo doko, Gotenya isingi mate dokonya napatana” lea.
Dopa latala baame wane wanakupi koo dupa kopinyetala, kingi aiyombanya setao auu pisia.
Dopa petala Jisasa paanya kaita nyiamopa, akali mendeme yapa ipao luma lakapala, baa tipa pyoo, “Mana Lenge Akali Epe, namba lete etete katenge doko aipa petala nyotope?” lea.
Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Aipuma embame namba kandao epena leepe? Endakali mende epe daa, Gote iki baa epe kalyamo.
Mosesanya loo dutupa embame masilino: 'Endakali pyao kumasala naeyape. Kepo kolala naeyape. Pake nala naeyape. Endakali mende sambo lao minakasala naeyape. Endakali mendenya dopale mende sambo lao tolao nyakamaiya naeyape. Embame embanya endangi takangepa, dolapo andanda semaiyoo katapena'” lea.
Akali dokome Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Mana Lenge Akali, namba wane kolesa pituu, Mosesanya loo dutupa pitaka watao minio, dopaka pyoo minao kalyona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame akali doko kondo kaeyao kandatala, “Emba mendai mende daa jilyamona, pupala embanya oapi dupa pitaka muni nyepala, endakali daa jingi dupa maitala, namba watao ipupi. Dokopa embanya epe dupa kaitinya sakatana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, baanya oapi etete longo singi dokonyana, mona etete kenda kaeyao, enomba kumatala, Jisasa yakinatala pea.
Pateamopa, Jisasame kandayoko latala, disaipolo dutupa lamaiyoo, “Yuunya kamongo dupa Gotenya isingi mate dokonya paanya, etete leke-leke tatamina” lea.
Dopa leamopa, disaipolo dupame sepala, mona kenda kaeyaminosa, Jisasame deaka lamaiyoo, “Wane paluma, endakali dupa Gotenya isingi mate dokonya paanya, eteteaka leke-leke tatami.
Kamele mendeme kepo tii mendenya leke-leke tao kolandapyaliaka doko, yuunya kamongo mendeme Gotenya isingi mate dokonya paanya, etete leke-leke tapyalina” lea.
Dokopa pii dutupa sepala, disaipolo dupa etete walu leami. Walu latala nyakamalapo laloo pyoo, “Dopa-tamo doko, endakali apimi Gotenya isingi mate dokonya patape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita kandatala lamaiyoo, “Endakalimi nyakamanya pupu lapae dokome Gotenya isingi mate dokonya napatami. Endakalimi kapa pao napipenge dupa pitaka Goteme kapa pao pingina” lea.
Dokopa Pitame baa lamaiyoo, “Naimanya tatapi, pinjupi, dupa pitaka yakinatala, emba watao epelyamano” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame lao pituu, “Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Nambapa, wai pii epe dokopa, dolapo lao masetala, endakali mendeme baanya ee andapi, takange endangipi, kaiminingi pimalengepi, wane wanakupi, dupanya mende yakinatamo dokome, ee andapi, endangipi, kaiminingi pimalengepi, wane wanakupi, dupa wakao 100 lao baa nyeta. Dee endakali dokome kenda pipae longo dupa apata nyoaka katata. Dopa petala yuu enenge ipatamo dokonya, baa lete etete katenge doko nyeta.
<range>
Salapape! Epapu endakali longo mendapu wambao kalyamino dupa, tanga maita pyatami. Maitapyao kalyamino dupa, wambatamina” Jisasame lea.
Jisasa disaipolo dupa-pipa Jerusalema paanya, kaita peaminopa, Jisasa wambea. Dokopa disaipolo dupa walu leami kandatala, watao peamino dupa paka kaeyami. Dopa piaminopa, baame 12 disaipolo dutupa lanyepala, tenda baa-kisa pitamo dupa dokaita lamaiyoo pituu,
“Naima Jerusalema pelyamano. Patatamanopa, akali mendeme Akalinya Ikiningi doko enge nyepala, pitisa mupapi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, dupa laitaka pyaapomo. Laitaka petatamopa, baa nyoo kote latala, pyao kumasalanya, akali kamalya katenge dupanya kingilyaka maitami.
Dopa petataminopa, baa lamba lao, sopokalimi pyao, konjame pyao petala, angi pyao kumasetaminopa, baa yuu gii tepo dokonya dee sakatatana” Jisasame lea.
Sebedi ikiningi Jemesa, Jonepi ipupala Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Mana Lenge Akali, nalimbame emba-kisa dopale mende tee latambanopa, embame latamba dopaka pipi laka lao masilyambanona” leambi.
Jisasame dolapo lamaiyoo, “Nambame nyakambanya aki mende pyakapili lao masilyambipi?” lea.
Dokopa dolapome yanu pyao, “Embanya tii pipae dokonya ipatenopa, nalimbanya mende embanya kingi tolae-kaita pilyepa lape, mende kingi koeya-kaita pilyepa lapena” leambi.
Dopa leambinopa, Jisasame dolapo lamaiyoo, “Nyakambame masala naeyao lelyambino. Nambame kenda pipae salapo-lamo doko, nyakambame kapa pao setambipi? Namba kumala pelyo dopa pyoo, nyakambame kapa pao kumala patambipi?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, dolapome yanu pyao, “Nalimbame kenda pipae dupa kapa pao setambaka. Dee nalimba emba kumateno dokonya kapa pao kumatambakana” leambi. Dopa leambinopa, Jisasame dolapo lamaiyoo, “Kini, nambame kenda pipae salapo-lamo doko, nyakambame setambiaka. Namba kumalapo dopaka pyoo, nyakamba kumatambiaka.
Dopaka doko, nambanya kingi tolae-kaita petena lapengepi, koeya-kaita petena lapengepi, doko nambanya kalai daa. Goteme pititamina lao yapao nyiamo endakali dupa pititamina” lea.
Dopa lelyambino lapae doko sepala, 10 disaipolo dutupame Jemesa, Jonepa imbu kaemaiyami.
Dopa piaminopa, Jisasame disaipolo dupa epena latala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Akali kantri waka isingi, Gote tungi napingi dupame, nyakamanya endakali isingi dupa kandanya palyetala, nyakama alyasale joo katengema, doko nyakamame kandengema. Kantri dupanya akali andake dupame, nyakamanya pii watao minekena lao kandatae paengema, mana doko nyakamame kandengemaka.
Nyakamame dopa napyepape. Nyakamanya mende akali andake joo katapuli lao masetamo dokome, dokaitanya kalai akali joo katapenge.
Nyakamanya mende alyasale joo katapuli lao masetamo dokome, dokaitanya kendemane joo katapenge.
Dopaka pyoo, Akalinya Ikiningi dokome baanya kalai pyekena lao naepea. Baame endakali longo dupa nisoo, kii tamao nyalanya baa tangeme kumala epeana” lea.
Dokopa dokaita Jereko peami. Dokonya katao, Jisasapi, disaipolopi, endakali kambu andake mendepimi Jereko yakinatala peami. Pao kandeaminopa, Timiasa ikiningi Batimiasa, lenge monda doko kaitinisa muni tee lao petea.
Baa Nasarete tange Jisasa ipao pelyamo lapae sepala, wii lao, “Dapiti Yumbange Jisasa, namba kondo kaeyapoko!” lea.
Dopa leamopa, endakali longo dupame baa pii kaena lao, pyalanya leami. Dopa leaminopapi, baame etete puu lao wii lao, “Dapiti Yumbange, namba kondo kaeyapoko!” lea.
Dokopa Jisasa katapala, “Baa epena lapa” lea. Dopa leamopa, endakali dupame akali lenge monda doko lamaiyoo, “Emba ipu lelyamona, paka nakaenya sakatao puu” leami.
Dokopa baanya yonge pee ketae pingi doko lyokanya pyale latala, pupae sakatao Jisasa kateamo dokonya pea.
Dokopa Jisasame baa tipa pyoo, “Nambame embanya aipa pyakapili lao masilipi?” lea. Akali lenge monda dokome yanu pyao, “Mana Lenge Akali, namba dee lenge tao kandatoo, embame namba nisepoko!” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Embame namba tungi pyapino dokome, embanya lenge dolapo auu pilyamona puu” lea. Dopa lalu piamopa, baanya lenge dolapo auu peteamopa, Jisasa watao pea.
Jisasa disaipolo dupa-pipa Jerusalema tengesa, Olipimanda, taono Betepasa, Betaniapa makisa singi dokonya peami. Pao pituu, Jisasame disaipolo lapoma wambao pena lea.
