Pena latala dolapo lamaiyoo, “Taono yakane silyamo omonya pupala, dongi yakane wamba endakali napetenge mende anjetae kalyamona, tata lao minao ipupape.
Endakali mendeme, 'Aipuma dopa pilyambipi?' lea kandeno dokopa, 'Kamongome pipenge mende pitoo latala, nyala pupa laamo. Kalai petala, dee yapa peakatoo laamona' lapape” lea.
Dokopa dolapome pupala, dongi yakane doko kaitini lembasa anda kambu mendenya anjetae kateamo kandatala, tata leambi.
Tata leambinopa, endakali kateamino dupame, “Dongi yakane doko aipuma tata lelyambipi?” leami.
Jisasame leamoli pyoo, dokaita lamaiyambinopa, yakana latala nyoo pena kaeyami.
Akali dolapome dongi doko Jisasa kateamo dokonya minao ipupala, nyakambanya yonge pee ketae pingi dolapo lyokanya dongi maitanya setapeambinopa, Jisasa dokonya ketae petea.
Endakali longo dupame nyakamanya yonge pee ketae pingi dupa kaitini dokonya kuiyami. Yangimi ita yoko dupa lakao kaitini dokonya kuiyamiaka.
Dokopa endakali dupa wambata, maita pyata pyoo pao pituu, wee dapa leami: “Gote lao mambo pilyamano! Kamongonya kengenya epelyamo akali dake Goteme auu pisetae!
Wamba Dapitimi naimanya yumbange dupa isoo kateamoli pyoo, indupa Kraisame naima isoo kalyanya epelyamo dake Goteme auu pisetae! Gote Ketae Kaitinya Katenge doko lao mambo pilyamanona” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasa pao Jerusalema pyakamatala, lotuu anda andake kame dokonya kolandatala, siamo dupa pitaka kandea. Niki lenge landa pyalanya piamopa, 12 disaipolo dutupa-pipa taono Betani dokonya peami.
Oo yongama Betani yakinatala epeaminopa, Jisasa baa lopo kaeya.
Lopo kaeyapala, piki ita mende yoko pyoo omosale kateamo kandatala, dii lyilyape lao kanja pea. Pao kandeamopa, piki dii nalyingi gii dokonyana, dii nalyoo yoko iki pyoo katea.
Jisasame piki ita doko lamaiyoo, “Tanga tangapi endakali mendeme embanya dii mende lyao nanatamina” lea. Pii leamo doko disaipolo dupame siami.
Jisasa disaipolo dupa-pipa Jerusalema pyakamatala, baa lotuu anda andake kame dokonya kolandatala, endakali maketa setao kateamipi, sambao kateamipi, dupa kandatala, imbu kaeya. Dopa petala toko ketae muni aloo piamino dupapi, yaka maiyolee maketa seteamino dupa sepeta minalyetala kaii lao nepatala, watao pia.
Watao pyapala, endakali mendeme oapi mende soo, lotuu anda andake kame andakote-kaita, poko napina lao daa lea.
Dopa latala baame dokaita mana lamaiyoo, “Pii pepa pyapae singi dokonya, 'Nambanya anda doko akali tata dupa pitakanya loma singi anda latamina' lapae nasilyape? Dopaka doko, nyakamame anda dake pake nenge dupanya yalo pingi kananda jetelyaminona” lea.
Endakali kambu kateamino dupa pitakame mana leamo doko sepala, walu leami. Tenge dokonya, Pitisa mupapi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali dupapimi Jisasa paka kaeyapala, baa pyao kumasemana lao kaitini kutiami.
Yuu kuiyala peamopa, Jisasa disaipolo dupa-pipa Jerusalema yakinatala peami.
Oo yongama wamba kaita dokonya pao pituu kandeaminopa, piki ita wamba dii namandena leamo doko tengenya pituu, sapuo pao mangenya tuu latae katea.
Jisasame piki ita doko kandao pii leamo doko Pitame masetala Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Mana Lenge Akali, kuaka embame piki ita dake sapuina lapino dokonya, sapupya-lamo kanda!” lea.
Dopa leamopa, baame disaipolo dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame Gote tungi pyalapape.
Endakali mendeme mona lapo palya naenya, Gote tungi pyatala, yuu manda dake sakatatala, solowatanya pyakala pena latamo doko, kini dopaka pita.
Nyakamame Gote tungi pyatala, dopale mende nyemana lao loma soo tee latamino dupa pitaka Goteme ditana lao nambame nyakama langilyo.
Nyakamame loma salanya pituu, endakali mendeme nyakama-kisa koo pitamo dupa kame sakamaiyepape. Dopa pitamino dokome, nyakamanya Takange kaitinya katenge dokome nyakamanya koo dupa kunao nepakatana” Jisasame lea.
<range>
Jisasa disaipolo dupa-pipa Jerusalema pilyetala, lotuu anda andake kame dokonya paeya. Dokonya paeyamopa, pitisa mupapi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, dupame ipupala tipa pyoo, “Emba apimi kalai andake dupa pii lapumupa pilipi?” leami.
<range>
Dokopa Jisasame yanu pyao, “Nambame nyakama tipa mende pitoaka, nyakamame yanu pyakatamino doko, nambame kalai datupa akali dokome pupu lapae ditala, pii lapyana lao nyakama langitoo.
Joneme kaimbu piamo mana doko apimi pupu lapae maitala, pina leape? Goteme pina leape, pande akalimi pina leamipi? Nyakamame namba langyepa” lea.
Dopa leamopa, dokaitame pii doko sepala, nyakamalapo laloo pyoo, “Naimame, 'Goteme pina leana' latamano doko, 'Aipuma nyakamame Jonenya pii doko kiningina lao masala naelyamipi?' laapomo.
Dopaka doko, endakali kambu dakeme Jone baa propeta kiningina lao masingima dokonya, naimame akalimi pina leamina laanya paka pyuumuna” leami.
Dopa latala, dupame Jisasanya pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Apimi Jone kaimbu pina leape lao, naimame masala naelyamanona” leami. Dokopa Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Dopa-tamo doko, nambame kalai datupa akali dokome pupu lapae ditala, pii lapyana lao, nyakama langya naeyatoakana” lea.
Jisasame Judamanya isingi akali dupa kongali pii mende lamaiyoo, “Akali mendeme waene ee mende kakopatala pokea-pyaa. Pokatala dii lyao waene ipange nyalanya, takyoo indyapenge yuli mende tombao wasia. Wasetala ee doko kandao isoo pitipenge anda ketae mende pia. Dopa petala akali mendapu-pipa propeta mokosetamanopa latala, ee doko isoo bisnis pyoo katekena latala, baa yuu londati mendakaita pao katea.
Waene wambu pingi gii epeamopa, baanya kalai akali mendeme ee isakamaingi akali dupa kateamino dokonya pupala, waene dii mendapu lyao peekena pena lea.
Leamo dokonya pateamopa, ee isoo katenge dupame baa pyao indyepala, mee pilyina leami.
Deaka akali ee tange dokome kalai akali mende pena lea. Pateamopa, akali dupame kalai akali doko pyao aiyomba lombapala, baa-kisa mana koo elya pipae mendapu miniami.
Deaka baame kalai akali mende pena lateamopa, doko pyao kumasiami. Dopaka pyoo, baame kalai akali longo pena lea. Pateaminopa, yangi dupa mee pyao indyepala, yangi dupa pyao kumasiami.
Dopa peteaminopa, akali dokonya ikiningi mona setenge mendai iki katenge doko, andanda samaiyaminona lao masetala, baa etao pena lea.
Wane doko epeamo kandatala, ee isakamaingi akali dupame nyakamalapo laloo pyoo, 'Wane dakeme takangenya moeya dupa nyepengena, baa pyao kumasetamano, doko baanya moeya nyepenge dupa naima nyetamana' leami.
Dopa latala wane doko pyao kumasetala, kamalya pyale leamina” lea.
Dopa latala Jisasame dokaita tipa pyoo, “Dopa piami-lumu dokonya waene ee tange dokome ipupala aipa pitape? Tange doko ipupala, ee isakamaingi dokaita pyao kumasetala, akali waka mendapuame isoo katekena lao laitaka pita.
Laitaka pita dokonya, nyakamame pii pepa pyapae silyamo dake itaki pyala naeyamipi? 'Kapenda dupame anda pipenge kana mende kandao, koeyapae-lamo latala yakineamino doko, kana mupa jetelyamo.
Kana mupa jetelyamo doko, Kamongome pipya-lamo dokonya, naimame eteteaka auu kaeyao sani kandelyamano'” lapae silyamo.
Jisasame dopa lamaiyamopa, Judamanya isingi akali dupame pii kongali doko nyakama kandao lalumuna lao sepala, baa anjemana lao kaita kutiami. Kutiaminoaka doko, endakali kambu kateamino dupa paka kaeyapala, baa yakinatala peami.
Jisasame pii mende kopeta latamo dokonya, baa mangenya minamana latala, Judamanya isingi akali dupame Parasai mendapuapi, Kiŋi Erote Antipasa tata mendapuapi, baa kateamo dokonya pena leami.
Akali dupame pupala baa lamaiyoo, “Mana Lenge Akali, embame akali andake dupa paka nakaeyao, kiningi pii doko tolao lenge. Endakali dupame pipimili lao Goteme masilyamo dokonya-kaita embame tolao mana lenge. Dopana, gapomane isingi mupa Sisa naimame takisa maipengepe, daape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame baa minao makande pilyamino lao kandatala, dokaita lamaiyoo, “Aipuma namba minao makande pilyami? Muni konde mende kandatoo, nyoo pealapa” lea.
Dokopa muni konde mende maitiaminopa, baame dokaita tipa pyoo, “Muni dakenya apinya lengelyapi, kengepi kalyape?” lea. “Doko Sisanya kalyamona” leami.
Dokopa Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Sisanya dupa Sisa tange maiyakamaiyepape. Gotenya dupa Gote tange maiyakamaiyepape” lea. Jisasame dopa leamopa, dokaitame baa kandatala, paka kaeyao walu leami.
Sadyusi dupame endakali kumapae dupa sakatala naeyatamina lengema. Dopa lengema dokaita Jisasa kateamo dokonya ipupala baa lamaiyoo,
“Mana Lenge Akali, wamba Mosesame mana pepa pyao seteamo dokonya, 'Akali mende enda nyepala, wane manja naeyao kumatamopa, baanya kaiminingi dokome enda walyakae doko piseta. Baapa, enda walyakae dokopa wane mupa manditambino doko kaiminingi kumia dokonya lao manjakamaitana' lao pyapae singi.
Gii mendepa akali mendenya ikiningi 7-pela kateami-pyaa. Dutupanya mupa dokome enda nyepala, wane manja naeyao kumia.
Dopa piamopa, kaiminingi laponge dokome enda doko pisiamoaka doko, wane namandeamopa, akali doko kumia. Kaiminingi teponge doko dopaka pia.
Dopaka pyoo, kaiminingi 7-pela dutupa pitakame enda dokoaka nyepala, wane manja naeyaowaka kumiami. Dokaita kumao ete dokonya enda doko kumia.
Akali kaiminingi 7-pela dutupa pitakame enda mendai dokoaka nyiamino dokonya, tanga endakali sakatatamino gii dokopa, enda doko apinya joo pitatape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame pii pepa pyapae singi doko masala naeyao, Gotenya pupu lapae doko masala naeyaowaka pingima. Tenge dokonya, nyakamame kopeta lelyamino.
Endakali kumapae dupa dee sakatatamino gii dokopa, akali enda nyala naeyao, enda akali napao, kaitinya enjele dupa katengemali pyoo katatami.
Ita saka mendenya ita yuli teana lao Mosesame pepa piamo doko itaki napiamipi? Atome dokonya Goteme Mosesa lamaiyoo, 'Namba Abrakame, Aisake, Jekopepinya Gotena' lea. Baa kumapae dupanya Gote daa. Baa saka katenge dupanya Gote. Abrakame, Aisake, Jekopepi dee tanga sakatao katatamina lao, Goteme masala naeyali doko, baa nyakamanya Gote laa naeyali. Dopana, nyakamame endakali kumapae dupa sakatala naeyatamina lelyamino, doko kopeta lelyaminona” Jisasame lea.
<range>
Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali dupanya mende ipao kateamo dokome, Sadyusi dupame Jisasa pii yanda pimaiyamino doko sepa, dee Jisasame dokaitanya pii auu pyoo yanu piamo doko sepaka pia. Dopa petala baame Jisasa tipa pyoo, “Mosesanya loo dupanya anduku mupa joo silyape?” lea.
Jisasame yanu pyao, “'Nyakama Israele tange dupame salapape! Naimanya Kamongo doko, Gote, baa mendai iki doko kalyamo.
Embame embanya Kamongo Gote doko, embanya monapi, imambupi, masingipi, pupu lapaepi, dutupa pitakame auu kaeyape.' Doko loo mupa doko.
Loo lapo dokome, 'Embame emba tange auu kaengeli pyoo, embanya endakali yango dupa auu kaeyape.' Loo dolapo ita minao, loo dupanya waka mende alyasale joo nasilyamona” Jisasame lea.
Dopa leamopa, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali dokome baa lamaiyoo, “Mana Lenge Akali, embame kiningi leeno. Gote doko baa mendai iki kalyamo. Waka mende nakalyamo.
Gote doko monapi, imambupi, masingipi, pupu lapaepi, dutupa pitakame auu kaenge dokopi, dee tange auu kaengeli pyoo, endakali yango dupa auu kaenge dokopi, loo lapoma dolapome kundi maingipi, opa yangengepi, dolapo ita miningina” lea.
Akali dokome auu pyoo yanu piamo kandatala, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Emba Gotenya isingi mate dokonya omosale joo nakalyenona” lea. Dopa lateamopa, endakali dupa pitakame Jisasa pii mende dee tipa pyaanya, paka kaeyami.
Jisasame lotuu anda andake kame andakote dokonya mana lamaiyoo katao, endakali dupa tipa pyoo, “Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali dupame aipa pyoo kandatala, Mesaeya doko Dapiti Yumbangena lengemape?
Oli Spiritame lungu piamopa, Dapitimi dapa lea: 'Kamongo Gote dokome nambanya Kamongo Mesaeya doko lamaiyoo, “Emba nambanya kingi tolae-kaita piti. Dokonya pititinopa, nambame embanya yandapipi dupa ita minatakala, embanya moko pundi-pundi katena latona' lapae silyamo.”
Dopa latala, Jisasame dokaita tipa pyoo, “Dapitimi Mesaeya doko kandao, baanya Kamongona lea-lumu doko, kaitini andukunya-kaita Mesaeya doko baanya yumbangena leape?” lea. Jisasame pii leamo doko endakali kambu andake kateamo dokome auu kaeyao siami.
Jisasame dokaita mana lamaiyoo, “Nyakama Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali dopale jetamina, wandyuu kalyepape. Dupame nyakama alyasale joo kalyamano lao masetala, yonge pee auu petae dupa petala, endakali dupame mambo pyao, nyakama kandamili lao maketa kamapu dupanya paengema.
Dopaka pyoo, Judamanya lotuu lelyamipi, nee andake nelyamipi, dupanya nyakama enomba nyoaka, pitipumali lao masingima.
Dupame enda walyakae dupanya yuu andapi dupa minakasoo nyingima. Dee endakali waka dupame nyakama epena lao masina latala, loma londe pyoo singimaka. Goteme endakali dopale pingi dupa kenda pipae etete andake maitana” lea.
Dopa latala Jisasa Judamanya lotuu anda andake muni pyasingi dokonya tengesa pao pitipala, endakali dupame aipa pyoo muni pyasilyamipi lao kandea. Kandao peteamopa, yuunya kamongo longo dupame muni longo lao pyasiami.
Dopa piaminopa, enda walyakae daa jepae mendeme ipupala, konde lapoma iki pyasiamo dolapo 2 toea joo pyasia.
Dokopa Jisasame baanya disaipolo dupa epena latala, “Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Enda walyakae daa jepae dakeme muni pyasalamo dokome, endakali waka pyasalamino dupa pitaka ita minalamo.
Endakali dokaitame nyakamanya muni longo sipya dupanya kakana nyoo pyasalamino. Dopa piminopa, enda daa jepae dakeme baanya kuki sipya dupa pitaka pyasalamona” lea.
Jisasame lotuu anda andake kame doko yakinatala peamopa, baanya disaipolo dupanya mendeme baa lamaiyoo, “Mana Lenge Akali, anda yale epe dupa kana yale auu petae dupame petae kalyamo kanda” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Anda yale epe kana soo namba-namba pyoo petae kalyamo kandeleno datupa, tanga dopa petae nakatata. Pitaka pyao kaluo nepatamina” lea.
Jisasa Olipimanda pituu, lotuu anda andake katenge dokaita-kaita, kandamatae petea. Peteamopa, Pita, Jemesa, Jone, Andruapi, dutupame elyakao baa tipa pyoo,
“Embame laleno dutupa gii andukupa pitape? Kongali aipale mende pitamopa, naimame kandatala, dutupa pitaka angi jalanya, tengesa petelyamona lao masetamape? Naima langi” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, Jisasame yanu pyao, “Endakali mendeme nyakama minao kyakasetana, kandao kalyepape.
Endakali longome nambanya kengenya ipupala, 'Namba Kraisa dokona' lao, endakali longo minao kyakasetami.
Yanda pilyamino lapaepi, yanda ingingi lapaepi, dupa sepala, nyakama walu nalalapape. Pipae, lapaepi, dupa pitaka ipatamoaka doko, yuu etapenge gii doko maitapyao ipata.
Kantri mendeme kantri mende yanda pimaita, kiŋi mendeme kiŋi mende yanda pimaita pitami. Dee yuu wakale-wakale dupanya titiwali dupa minata, lopo andake dupa sepa pita. Dopa pitamo doko, enda wane manjanya, maita pingi dopale joo pita.
Endakali dupame nyakama anjoo soo, kanjole dupa-kisa kote laa patami. Dee Judamanya lotuu anda dupanya nyakama pyatamiakana, kandao kalyepape. Nyakamame namba watao paeyataminosa, endakali dupame gapenapi, kiŋipi, dupanya enombanya nyakama laminao pao, katasetami. Katasetataminopa, nyakamame nambanya pii doko akali dokaita panao lamaitami.
Yuu etapenge gii doko ipatala naeyatamopa, wambao endakali dupa pitaka-kisa wai pii epe doko lamaiyoo taeyapenge.
Endakali dupame nyakama anjetala, laminao kote anda dokonya pataminopa, nyakamame aipa lamape lao masala naeyalapape. Kote lapenge gii dokopa, Goteme nyakama pii ditali pyoo lapape. Nyakamame latamino doko masoo laa naeyatami. Oli Spiritame ditamopa latami.
Akali mendapuame nyakamanya kaiminingi etete dupa enge nyepala, pyao kumasina lao maitami. Akali mendapuame nyakamanya wane dupa dopaka pitami. Wane mendapuame kandapilyetala, nyakamanya endangi takangepi dupa pyao kumasina lao, maitamiaka.
Nyakama namba tata joo katataminosa, endakali dupa pitakame nyakama etete imbu kaengitami. Dopa pitaminopapi, endakali mende kyeto joo katao, etatamo doko baa Goteme pyoo nyetana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Gote mambo napina lao kaita lyokapenge, myuku pipae dopale mende lotuu anda andake dokonya andakote nyoo setatamino dokopa, endakali Judia katatamino dupa yuu manda dupanya paka pupenge jetana” lea. (Pii dake itaki pyateno dokome tenge doko masoo nyepe.)
Gii dokopa, endakali mende baanya anda patakisa katatamo dokome, baanya oapi andakote setamo dupa nyala napupenge jeta.
Dee endakali mende eesa katatamo dokome, baanya yonge pee ketae pingi doko pilyoo nyala naeyapengeaka jeta.
Enda wane tongatapi, enda wane andu nengepi, dupa gii dokopa etete kondo pita!
Kenda pipae dutupa koo kana palitamo dokopa, naepena lao loma soo kalyepape.
Goteme yuu kaitipi wasiamo dokonya pituu, indupa tuu lao, kenda pipae epelyamo dupa pitaka kenda pipae ene ipatamo dokome ita minata. Dee kenda pipae dopale mende tanga tangapi naipata.
Kamongome yuu gii dupa muu pisala naeyatamo doko, endakali mendaipi mende nakatata. Dopaka doko, baanya endakali yapao nyepae dupa lao masetala, kenda pipaepi, yuu giipi, dupa minao muu piseta.
“Gii dokopa Gotenya yapao nyepae endakali dupa lanyoo lemba pyalanya, sambo Kraisa mane-mane pipaepi, sambo propetapi, dupame ipupala, kongalipi, mirakolo kalaipi, dupa pitami. Dopana, endakali mendeme nyakama langyoo, 'Kraisa doko asa kalyamo kanjepa! Amasa kalyamo kanjepa!' lea kandeno doko, baame kiningi lelyamona lao nyakamame masala naeyalapape.
<range>
Nambame enesa tanga pitamo dupa langilyona, nyakama kandao kalyepape” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Kenda pipae andake ipatamo dupa etapatamopa, 'kaitinya singi dupa pitaka ema-ema pita. Dopa pitamopa, niki doko iminjoo, kana doko tii napyoo, kaitinya bui dupa kondao isa ipao pita.'
<range>
Dopa petatamopa, Akalinya Ikiningi doko baanya pupu lapaepi, tii pipaepi, dupanya pituu kopa tambe-tambe ipatamopa, endakali dupame kandatami.
Dokopa yuu lemba dupa pitakanya pituu, enjele dupame Gotenya endakali yapao nyepae dupa pitaka lanyoo elyambu pyekena latana” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Nyakamame piki ita lenge dokonya mana mende nyalapape. Nyakamame piki ita mange popo pyoo, alulyamo doko kandatala, paina pyaanya pilyamona lengema.
Dokaita joo, pitamo dutupa pitaka nyakamame kandatala, Akalinya Ikiningi doko ipanya, etete tengesa pilyamona lao masalapape.
Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Endakali indupa palelyamino dupa kumao etapala naeyataminopa, dupa pitaka pita.
Yuupi kaitipi dupa pitaka alu pita. Dopaka doko, nambanya pii doko tanga tangapi alu napita” lea.
Jisasame dee mende lao pituu, “Endakali mendeme yuupi kaitipi etatamo gii doko masala naengema. Kaitinya enjele dupame masala naengemaka. Ikiningi dokome apata masala naengeaka. Takange dokome iki masingi.
Nyakamame gii doko andukupa ipatape lao masala naelyaminona, kandao isoo kalyepape.
Tenda namba isa yuu dake yakinatala pato doko, akali mendeme baanya anda doko yakinatala, yuu waka mendenya pao katenge dopale. Paanya pituu baanya kalai akali dupame anda doko isoo katekena latala, kalai wakale-wakale mokosoo maingi. Dopa petala akali lome kambu isoo katenge dokome lome kambu doko isokondape pyoo isoo katekena latala, baa penge.
Patatamopa, nyakamame anda tange doko yuu kutu-kuta ipatape, palyapenge gii dokopa ipatape, kuka andatombe ipatape, yongao minao ipatape lao masala naengema. Nyakama ambe lao luu palitaminopa, baa tanda lao ipatana, kandao isoo kalyepape.
<range>
Nambame nyakama langilyo dokoaka, endakali pitaka lamailyona, nyakamame kandao isoo kalyepape” lea.
Israele tange dupame betesa yisa napalenge nengema gii dokopa, Napinya Kaeyamo Pasopa gii dokopa, dolapo ene ipanya yuu gii lapoma siamopa, pitisa mupapi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akali dupapimi aipa petala Jisasa waa katao, anjoo nyepala, pyao kumasemape lao, kaita kutiami.
Kutapala lao pituu, “Gii epe dakenya aopyoo latala, endakali dupame naima imbu kaeyapala, pundu yaka lasetamina, dopa napimanana” leami.
Jisasa baa taono Betani dokonya akali kopetali Saimone lenge dokonya andaka nee nao peteamopa, enda mendeme penge yakane mendenya, wele tunduma pipae muni andake pupenge, tumbatae mende minao epea. Ipupala, baame penge dokonya kambu doko tambapala, Jisasanya aiyombanya wele doko kaii lakamaiya.
Kaii lakamaiyamopa, endakali yangi peteamino dupame enda doko imbu kaeyapala, mende lamai-lamai pyoo, “Wele dake endakalimi sambaminopa, silipa muni 300 yalao nyepala, endakali daa jepae dupa maipumalina, aipuma baame mee pyoo nepelyape?” leami. Dopa latala, enda doko maka kaeyapala, pyalanya leami.
<range>
Pyalanya leaminoaka doko, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Baame namba-kisa kalai epe etete mende pilyamona, pina kaeyalapa. Aipuma nyakamame enda dakenya mona kenda pisakamailyamipi?
Endakali daa jepae dupa koteaka lao nyakama-pipa apata katatami. Dokopa dokaita pitali pyoo nisetami. Dopaka doko, namba nyakama-pipa gii longo mende kalya naeyalamano.
Baame pipenge jipya doko pyomo. Baame wele tunduma pipae kaii lakalamo dokome, nambanya yonge doko malu pipenge dokonya depa lasoo pyakalamo.
Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Yuu dupa pitakanya wai pii epe doko lao taeyatamino dokopa, enda dakeme pilyamo dupa apata lao taeyataminopa, enda dakeme pilyamo dupa masetamina” lea.
Judasa Iskariota doko, 12 disaipolo dutupanya mende, dokome Jisasa enge nyotoo lao masetala, pitisa mupa dupa laitaka pyaanya pea.
Pao lamaitiamopa, nyakamame baanya pii doko sepala, eteke pyao auu kaeyami. Auu kaeyapala, muni mendatupa maimana leami. Dokopa Judasame pitisa dokaita Jisasa laitaka pyaanya kaitini kutia.
Israele tange dupame betesa yisa napalenge nengema, yuu gii tee pyao dokonya, sipisipi yakane mendapu pyapala, Napinya Kaeyamo Pasopa gii doko masoo nengema. Dopa pingima gii doko epeamopa, disaipolo dupame Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Napinya Kaeyamo Pasopa nee doko naimame anja depa lamape?” leami.
Dopa leaminopa, baanya disaipolo dupanya lapoma lamaiyoo, “Nyakamba Jerusalema pupape. Patambinopa, akali endaki kamuo singi mendeme nyakamba kandanyalapomona, doko watao pupape.
Pao baa anda kolandatamo dokonya tange doko lamaiyoo, 'Mana lenge akali dokome baanya disaipolo dupa-pipa Napinya Kaeyamo Pasopa nee doko natoo, anda panda doko andusa silyape laamona' lao lamaiyepape” lea.
Dokopa baame anda andake ketae mendenya lumu depa latae singi mende laitaka pyaapomona, dokonya nyakambame nee depa lapape” lea.
Dopa lamaitiamopa, disaipolo dolapo Jerusalema pyakamatala kandeambinopa, Jisasame leamoliaka petae siamo dokonya, nyakambame nee akipi depa leambi.
Depa lateambinopa, yuu kuiyala peamopa, Jisasa baa 12 disaipolo dutupa-pipa epeami.
Ipupala nee nao pituu, Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Nee nao pilyamano dakenya mendeme namba enge nyipumu dokome namba pyao kumasepenge akali dupa laitaka pyaapomona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, dokaitame mona kenda kaeyapala baa tipa pyoo, “Doko namba kandao leepe?” lao laa-laa peami.
Dopa leaminopa, baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakama 12 disaipolo nee disanya poeyanyoo apata nao pilyamano dakenya mendeme dopa pyaapomo.
Akalinya Ikiningi doko kumatana lao pepa pyapae singi dokonya, dopaka pyaapome-lamo. Dopaka doko, akali enge nyetamo doko yamataka andake mende lao kumata-lamo! Endangimi baa namandeali doko, yaka jialina” lea.
Nyakama nee nao pituu, Jisasame betesa mende nyepala, Gote lao yaka pilino latala konjia. Konjepala dokaita maiyoo pituu, “Dake nambanya yonge dokona, nyoo nalapa” lea.
Dopa petala baame kapo waene peteta mende nyepala, Gote lao yaka pilino latala, dokaita maiya. Maiyamopa, dokaitame dokonya nyoo neami.
Baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nambanya taiyoko kaii lelyo dakeme, Goteme endakali longo dupa nisoo, pii enenge mende lao setekelyamo.
Nambame nyakama kiningi langilyo: Namba dee waene nala naeyaowaka katao, tanga Gotenya isingi mate dokonya waene enenge doko natona” lea.
Dopa lateamopa, dokaitame wee mende latala, kamaka pyakalyetala, Olipimanda peami.
Dokopa Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “'Sipisipi setao katenge doko Goteme pyatamopa, sipisipi dupa kaita wakale-wakale dupanya patamina' lao pii pepa pyapae silyamo. Lapae silyamoliaka pyoo, nyakama pitakame namba soo yakinalamino.
Dopaka doko, Goteme namba dee sakatasetatamopa, nyakama Galilea paa naeyataminopa, namba wambao patona” lea.
Dokopa Pitame Jisasa lamaiyoo, “Yangi dupa pitakame emba soo yakinatala pataminopa, nambame emba yakinala naeyatona” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame baa lamaiyoo, “Nambame emba kiningi langilyo: Indupa kuka gii dakenya, yaka pauli pii lapo pyoo, ene laanya pitamopa, paa tepomasa embame namba nakandengena laapenona” lea.
Dokopa Pitame etete kyeto joo baa lamaiyoo, “Nambame emba yakinala naeyato. Emba kumateno dokonya namba apataka kumatambana” lea. Dokopa disaipolo yangi dupa pitakame dopaka leami.
Dokopa dokaita Gesemani ee dokonya peami. Pupala Jisasame baanya disaipolo dupa lamaiyoo, “Namba loma sotoo, nyakama asa pilyepape” lea.
Dopa latala baame Pita, Jemesa, Jonepi, dutupa lanyoo, umbisale pea. Pupala baa mona etete kenda kaeyapala, dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nambanya mona doko etete kenda petala, kumapenge julumuna, nyakama asa kandao isoo kalyepape” lea.
<range>
Dopa latala baa kuki umbisale pao, yuunya tombauli sepala, loma soo pituu, “Apane, Apane, embame dupa pitaka pingi. Embame kandatenopa, gii dake namba-kisa naepena lapenge jia kandeno doko, dopa pipi. Embame namba-kisa kenda pipae silyamo dake nyoo nepaka lapuliaka doko, nambame masilyo dokonya-kaita napipi. Embame masilino dokonya-kaita pipi” Jisasame lea.
<range>
Dopa lao loma sepala, ipao kandeamopa, disaipolo dutupa luu palyasiamisa, baame Pita lamaiyoo, “Saimone, emba luu palelepe? Embame aipuma awa mendai dokonya kandao isoo nakatalepe?
Kiningi etete nyakamanya imambumi pyuani kaeyapumupa, yongeme papa tambulyamona, makande pingi dupanya nyakama pao koeyatamina, kandao isoo loma soo kalyepape” lea.
Dopa latala baa deaka pupala, wamba loma siamo dutupaka sia.
Loma sepala dee ipao kandeamopa, disaipolo dupa lemonguti kaeyapala, paleami. Dee nyakama sakatatala, baa aipa lamaimape lao masala naeyami.
Baa deaka paa tepo pyoo pilyetala, dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakama mee luaka paliu silyamipi? Namba enge nyipumu akali doko ipatelyamo. Akalinya Ikiningi doko koo pingi endakali dupa laitaka pyaapomo gii doko ipatelyamona, mona sakatalapa” lea.
<range>
Jisasame dopa lao kateamopa, baanya 12 disaipolo dutupanya mende, Judasa lenge doko epea. Epeamo dokonya, endakali kambu mende konja-wuapi, kolyepepi, dupa minao baa apata epeami. Dupa akali pitisa mupapi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, dupame pena leaminosa, epeami.
Jisasa enge nyiamo akali dokome wambao endakali kambu doko lamaiyoo, “Nambame akali mende nunu pitu dokona, nyakamame baa anjetala, kandao isoo laminao pupape” lea.
Dopa lamaitala, ipao baa Jisasa kateamo dokonya tolao pupala, “Mana Lenge Akali” latala, baa nunu pia.
Dopa piamopa, dokaitame Jisasa minatala anjiami.
Anjiamino dokopa, akali mende baapa makisa katea dokome baanya konja-wua doko kolanyetala, pitisa mupa dokonya kalai akali mendenya kale lyanya nepea.
Dokopa Jisasame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame pake nenge mende anjala epele lao, konja-wuapi, kolyepepi, dupa minao namba anjala epelyamipi?
Koteaka lao namba lotuu anda andake dokonya, nyakamanya kaina dokonya katao, nyakama mana langio dokopa, nyakamame namba anjala naeyami. Dopaka doko, pii pepa pyapae singi doko angi panelyamona” lea.
Dokopa disaipolo dupa pitakame baa yakinatala, paka pyakao peami.
Peamino dupanya, wane kole mende lapalapa iki petae, Jisasa watao peamo doko anjalanya lapalapanya miniami.
Minateaminopa, lapalapa doko kakonya yakinatala, baa papata paka pea.
Dokopa dupame Jisasa laminao, pitisa mupa dupanya aiyomba doko kateasa peami. Dopa piaminopa, pitisa mupapi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, dupa ipao kambu piami.
Dokopa Pita waa katao maitanya Jisasa watao pea. Pupala pitisa mupa dupanya aiyomba dokonya anda kamapusa kolandatala, yanda singi dupa-pipa ita mende teamo dokonya endo soo petea.
Pitisa mupapi, kanjole kambuingi andake dokomepi, Jisasa pyao kumasemana latala, baa-kisa tenge mende setame lao kutiami. Dopa piaminoaka doko, tenge mende kandao nanyiami.
Endakali longo mendapuame baa-kisa tenge setao, sambo pii leaminoaka doko, nyakamanya pii leamino dupa mendai nanjia.
Endakali mendapuame sakatatala, baa-kisa sambo pii setao,
“Akali dakeme lao pituu, 'Nambame lotuu anda andake kingimi petae dake lakyepala, yuu gii tepomanya waka mende pitu doko, endakali kingimi napipenge mende pituna' leamopa, naimame siamana” leami.
Dopa leaminoaka doko, nyakamanya pii leamino dupa mendai nanjia.
Dokopa pitisa mupa dupanya aiyomba dokome dokaitanya kaina dokonya toeya katapala, Jisasa tipa pyoo, “Pii emba-kisa tenge setao lelyamino dake, aipuma yanu napilipi?” lea.
Dopa leamoaka doko, Jisasame ema napia. Dokopa pitisa mupa dupanya aiyomba dokome dee baa tipa pyoo, “Emba Gote Tii Pipae dokonya Ikiningi Kraisa dokope?” lea.
Jisasame pii yanu pyao, “Doko namba. Akalinya Ikiningi doko, Gote etete pupu lapae dokonya kingi tolae dokonya pituu, kaitinya kopa tambe-tambe ipatamopa, nyakamame kandatamina” lea.
Jisasame dopa leamo sulu katao, pitisa mupa dupanya aiyomba dokonya yonge pee doko tange minao lapyepala, “Baame Gote lamba lao pii lelyamo doko sepelyamino. Aipuma endakali mendapuanya pii deaka nyemape? Nyakamame aipa pimana lao masilyamipi?” lea. Dokopa pitakame, “Baa-kisa tenge silyamona, baa pyao kumasepengena” leami.
<range>
Dopa latala akali mendapuame baa sopokalimi piami. Pyapala baanya lengelyapi yaki petala, kimiame pyao pituu, “Emba kini propeta-tamo doko, emba akali dokome pilyamo lao naima langi!” leami. Dokopa yanda singi kateamino dupame baa pyao takiamiaka.
Pita baa anda kamapusa peteamopa, pitisa mupa dupanya aiyomba dokonya, kalai pyakamaiyoo petenge, wanaku dupanya mende epea.
Ipupala Pita endo soo peteamo doko kandokondape pyoo kandatala, baa lamaiyoo, “Emba Nasarete tange Jisasapa apata katengembana” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Pitame tanga lao, “Embame leeno doko namba nakandenge. Namba masala naelyona” lea. Dopa latala baa pitisa mupa dupanya aiyomba dokonya lome kambusa peamopa, yaka pauli pii mende lea.
Dopa piamopa, kalai wanaku dokome baa deaka kandatala, akali kateamino dupa lamaiyoo, “Baa akali dutupanya mendena” lea.
Dopa leamopapi, Pitame deaka tanga lea. Gii kuki pateamopa, akali kateamino dupame Pita deaka lamaiyoo, “Kini, emba Galilea tange dokonyana, emba akali dutupanya mende-lamona” leami.
Dokopa Pitame lao pituu, “Nyakamame akali lelyamino doko namba nakandengena, sambo lato doko, Goteme namba pinana” lea.
Dopa lateamopa, yaka pauli pii lapo pyoo lea. Dokopa Jisasame pii wamba leamo datupa Pitame masia: “Yaka pii lapo pyoo, ene laanya pitamopa, embame paa tepomasa namba nakandengena laapenona” leamo doko masetala, Pita putukuo ee lea.
Yongama wamba pitisa mupapi, Judamanya isingi akalipi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, kanjole kambuingi andake dupa pitaka kambuiyami. Lao kambutala, Jisasa anjoo soo, Pondiasa Pailate maiya peami.
Maitiaminopa, Pailateme baa tipa pyoo, “Emba Judamanya Kiŋi dokope?” lea. Dopa leamopa, Jisasame pii yanu pyakamaiyoo, “Embame leleno dokoakana” lea.
Dokopa pitisa mupa dupame baa-kisa tenge longo seteami.
Dokopa Pailateme baa dee tipa pyoo, “Akali dakaitame emba-kisa tenge longo lao setelyamino doko, embame piipi mende yanu pyao nalelepe?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, Jisasame dee pii mende yanu pyao naleamosa, Pailate paka kaeyapala, masepae longo nyia.
Ee kana dii lao, Napinya Kaeyamo Pasopa gii doko epelyamoli pyoo, Pailateme akali anjetae dupanya mende, endakali dupame mokekena lelyamili pyoo, mokata pyakamaingi. Gii doko paleamopa, endakali kambu dokome ipupala, akali mende mokekena leami. Akali Barabasa lenge dokopi, akali mendapuapimi wamba gapomane yanda pimaitala, endakali mendapu pyao kumasetala, anjetae paleami.
<range>
<range>
Dokopa pitisa mupa dupame Jisasa-pipa tilya nyepala, baa anjoo dimini-lamo lao Pailateme kandea. Kandatala dokaita tipa pyoo, “Nambame Judamanya Kiŋi doko mokakapili lao masilyamipi?” lea.
<range>
Dopa leamoaka doko, pitisa mupa dupame akali Barabasa doko mokekena lamana lao, endakali kambu dupa ingi tuu leami.
Dokopa Pailateme dokaita deaka tipa pyoo, “Nyakamame Judamanya Kiŋi lengema dake nambame aipa pyakaowape?” lea.
Dopa leamopa, dupame deaka puu lao, “Poko itanya pyao yuku!” leami.
Dopa leaminoaka doko, Pailateme dokaita lamaiyoo, “Baame koo aki mende pipyape?” lea. Dopa leamopa, dokaitame eteteaka puu lao, “Baa pyao yuku!” leami.
Dokopa Pailateme endakali kambu dupanya auu kaeyamili pyoo, Barabasa doko mokakamaiya. Dopa petala yanda singi dupame Jisasa konjame pyapala, pyao yukuina lao maiya.
Dokopa yanda singi dupame Jisasa laminao, gapomane isingi akali andake petenge anda dokonya kolandatala, yanda singi dupa pitaka ipao kambu pina leami.
Kambu pyatala, dupame yonge pee ketae pingi kala pepola mende baanya petakamaitala, kende nenge-nenge katapae mende nyoo makipu petala, Jisasanya aiyombanya pyakamaiyami.
Dopa petala, dupame baa lamba lao, “Judamanya Kiŋi, emba auu pyoo katape!” leami.
Dopa latala, dupame keoo konjame aiyombanya pyapa, sopokalimi pyapa petala, baa lamba lao luma lakao, mambo piami.
Dopa pyoo etapala, yonge pee kala pepola wamba pyakamaiyamino doko lyokao nyepala, baanya yonge pee ketae pingi doko tange pyakamaiyami. Dopa petala baa pyao yukulanya laminao peami.
Dokopa Alekesandapa, Rupasapanya takange Saimone yuu Sairini tange doko kamalyatena katao, taono dokonya epeamo kandanyetala, yanda singi dupame baa pyalanya latala, Jisasanya poko ita doko sakamaina leami.
Sina latala, dupame Jisasa laminao, yuu manda kenge Gologota lenge dokonya pao pyakalyiami. (Manda Gologota dokonya tenge doko, “Matena kuli.”)
Yuu manda dokonya pupala, dupame baa tanda kaeyala naena lao, waene matasini-pipa wasepala maiyaminopa, nanenya kaeya.
Kaeyateamopa, yongama 9 kiloko dokonya Jisasa pyao poko itanya yukuiyami. Yukutala baanya yonge pee wamba lyokeamino dupa setapala, yanda singi dupame apimi yonge pee dupanya mende nyilyape kandamana lao lakii piami.
<range>
Jisasa-kisa tenge seteamino pii doko, “Judamanya Kiŋi dokona” lao pepa pyatae doko poko ita ketae dokonya katea.
Jisasa poko itanya pyao yukuiyamino dokopa, akali pake nenge lapoma apata pyao yukuiyami. Mende doko baanya kingi tolae-kaita yukuiyami. Mende doko baanya kingi koeya-kaita yukuiyami.
<range>
Jisasa pyao yukutae kateamo dokonya-kaita endakali paeyamino dupame baa lamba lao, aiyomba wangatoto pyoo, “Lotuu anda andake doko lakyepala, yuu gii tepomanya waka mende pituna leeno akali dokae!
Embame emba tange pyoo nyoo, poko ita doko yakinatala, isa ipupoko!” leami.
Dopaka pyoo, pitisa mupapi, Mosesanya loo mana nyepae akalipi, dupame lamba lao, nyakamalapo laloo pyoo, “Baame endakali waka dupa pyoo nyipumuaka doko, baa tange kapa pao pyoo nyala naenge-lamo.
Kraisa dake, Israelemanya Kiŋi daape, epapu poko ita doko yakinatala, isa epena kaeya. Yakinatamo doko, naimame kandatala, baa lao masoo minamanalena” leami. Akali lapoma baa-pipa apata pyao yukutae kateambino dolapome mendai dopaka pyoo, baa-kisa lamba pii kando piambi.
Jisasa yukutae kateamopaka, 12 kilokonya pituu yuu kuiya. Kuiyamo doko kuiyataeyaka katao pao, 3 kilokonya tuu lea.
Dokopa, Jisasame etete puu lao, “Ilai, Ilai, lema sabatani?” lea. (Pii dokonya tenge doko, “Nambanya Gote, nambanya Gote, embame namba aipuma yakinelepe?”)
Dopa leamo doko endakali dosa kateamino dupanya mendapuame sepala, “Ilaija lao wii lelyamona, salapape” leami.
Dopa lateaminopa, akali mendeme alo pyao pao, koma jepae mende itakulinya tuku petala, waene kaa pipae mendenya poeyanyetala, Jisasa nena lao, makapusakamaiya. Dopa petala baame lao pituu, “Ilaijame baa kondao nyala epelyape lao kandamanana, malisalapa” lea.
Dokopa, Jisasame eteteaka puu lao ae mende latala, baa kumia.
Dokopa lotuu anda andake dokonya lapalapa andake mendeme nee nyetae katenge panda dokonya kame pinyetae katenge doko ketae pituu titi pyao isa tuu latala, lapo pyoloo pia.
Yanda singi isingi akali Jisasanya enomba-kaita kateamo dokome, Jisasa dopa pyoo kumiamo doko kandatala, “Kiningi etete, akali dake Gote Ikiningi-lamona!” lea.
Maria Magadala tange dokopi, wane kole Jemesa, Josesapanya endangi Mariapi, Salomiapi, dutupame kuki tependale pituu, kandatae peteami.
Wamba Jisasa Galilea yuu dokonya kateamo dokopa, enda dutupame baa watao paeyao nisiami. Dee enda longo mendapu Jisasa-pipa apata Jerusalema lalyoo epeamino dupa dosa kateamiaka.
Yuu kuiyalanya piamopa, Josepe Arimatia tange, kanjole dokonya akali kenge epe singi mende epea. Baa Gotenya isingi mate doko malisoo, katengeaka. Sambata depa lapenge gii paleamopa, Josepe paka nakaeyao, Pailate peteamo dokonya pupala, Jisasanya yonge doko dina lao tee lea.
<range>
Dopa leamopa, Pailateme Jisasa kumatalame-lumu lao walu lea. Walu latala baame yanda singi isingi doko epena latala, Jisasa kumatalape lao tipa pia.
Yanda singi isingi dokome Jisasa kini kumatalamona lao lamaitiamopa, Pailateme Jisasanya yonge doko Josepeme kondao nyala pena lea.
Dokopa Josepeme lapalapa epe kyeto mende sambapala pao, Jisasanya yonge doko kondao isa nyepala, lapalapa dokome yaki-yaki pia. Dopa petala akali mendenya kananda malu tumbinya setea mendenya yonge doko nyoo setapala, kana andake mende kapilya mina-mina pyoo minao pao, malu kambu doko piti pia.
Dopa piamopa, Maria Magadala tange dokopa, Josesa endangi Maria dokopame, Josepeme Jisasanya yonge doko nyoo seteamo panda doko kandao peteambi.
Sambata gii doko pateamopa, Maria Magadala tange dokopi, Maria Jemesa endangi dokopi, enda Salomiapi dutupame Jisasanya yonge doko kai pyala mona latala, welepi dopale tunduma pipae mendapu sambeami.
Wele tunduma pipae sambeamino dupa minao, Sandeenya yongama wamba niki pyakaeyamopa, malu dokonya peami.
Pao pituu nyakamalapo laloo pyoo, “Malu kambu dokonya kana piti petae doko apimi nyoo nepakatape?” leami.
Pupala kandeaminopa, kana etete andake doko nyoo, kapya latae katea.
Enda dupame malu dokonya kolandatala, akali patange, yonge pee londe kyoo lapae pingi mende kingi tolae-kaita pilyasiasa kandatala, walu leami.
Dopa piaminopa, baame enda dutupa lamaiyoo, “Nyakama walu nalalapape. Jisasa Nasarete tange, poko itanya pyao yukuiyamino doko, nyakamame kutilyamino doko sakatatalamo. Baa seteamino panda dakenya nasilyamo kanjepa.
Dopana, nyakama pupala, Pitapi, disaipolo yangi dupa lamaiyoo, 'Wamba nyakama langiamoli pyoo, baa wambao Galilea patamopa, nyakamame pao kanjaminona' lamaiyepape” lea.
Enda dutupa walu latala, malu dokonya kamaka pyakalyetala, paka peami. Nyakama paka kaeyapala, mende lamaiya naeyami.
Sandee gii dokonya yongama wamba Jisasa sakatatala, Maria Magadala tange, wamba imambu koo 7-pela paleta mende, Jisasame watao pyakamaiyamo dokome, wambao kandena lao panea.
Panateamopa, Jisasa-pipa apata kateamino endakali dupa ee lao yamataka lao peteaminopa, enda dokome pupala dokaita lamaiyoo, “Jisasa lenge tao katapumupa, nambame kanjona” lea. Dopa leamopa, dokaitame sepala, pii doko kiningina lao masala naeyami.
<range>
Maitakao disaipolo lapoma taono doko yakinatala peambinopa, dolapome nakandena lao Jisasa baa waka jetala, apata peami. Jisasa pateamopa, maitakao akali doko Jisasa-lamo lao kandeambi.
Kandatala dolapome pupala, disaipolo yangi dupa lamaiyambinopa, kiningi lelyambinona lao dupame masala naeyamiaka.
Maitakao 11 disaipolo dutupa nee nao peteaminopa, Jisasa baa dokaitame kandena lao ipao panea. Baa sakatatala paneamo kandeamino endakali dupame kiningi lelyaminona lao, disaipolo dupame masala naenya, tuu pyoo mona pyakilyiaminosa, Jisasame dokaita pyalanya lea.
Dopa latala baame dokaita lamaiyoo, “Nyakamame yuu dupa pitakanya pupala, wai pii epe doko endakali dupa pitaka lamaiyepape.
Namba tungi pyatala, kaimbu nyetamo endakali doko, Goteme pyoo nyeta. Namba tungi pyala naeyatamo endakali doko, Goteme daa latala watao pyata.
Namba tungi pyatamino endakali dupame kalai andake datupa pitaminopa, Gotenya pupu lapae doko nyakama-kisa silyame-lamo lao kandatami. Dupame nambanya kenge doko lao, imambu koo dupa watao pyatami. Dee pii tata waka dupa latamiaka.
Kanopato salenda dupa kingimi minataminopapi, tomakai dupa nataminopapi, dupa koeyala naeyatami. Endakali yaina pyapae dupa kingimi minataminopa, yaina dupa mee jetana” lea.
Kamongo Jisasame baanya disaipolo dupa pii lamaitiamopa, Goteme baa lanyoo kaiti-kisa pea. Dopa petala Goteme baanya kingi tolae-kaita petena lea.
Disaipolo dupame yuu dupa pitakanya pupala, wai pii epe doko lamaiyami. Lamaiyaminopa, Kamongonya pupu lapae doko nyakama-pipa apata mirakolo kalai piamino dokome, wai pii epe doko kyeto jisia.
